Utonia: Toward One Encoder for All Point Clouds
Authors: Yujia Zhang, Xiaoyang Wu, Yunhan Yang, Xianzhe Fan, Han Li, Yuechen Zhang, Zehao Huang, Naiyan Wang, Hengshuang Zhao
First: 2026-03-03T18:59:58+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T18:59:58+00:00
Comments: produced by Pointcept, project page: https://pointcept.github.io/Utonia
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Project1
Abstract
We dream of a future where point clouds from all domains can come together to shape a single model that benefits them all. Toward this goal, we present Utonia, a first step toward training a single self-supervised point transformer encoder across diverse domains, spanning remote sensing, outdoor LiDAR, indoor RGB-D sequences, object-centric CAD models, and point clouds lifted from RGB-only videos. Despite their distinct sensing geometries, densities, and priors, Utonia learns a consistent representation space that transfers across domains. This unification improves perception capability while revealing intriguing emergent behaviors that arise only when domains are trained jointly. Beyond perception, we observe that Utonia representations can also benefit embodied and multimodal reasoning: conditioning vision-language-action policies on Utonia features improves robotic manipulation, and integrating them into vision-language models yields gains on spatial reasoning. We hope Utonia can serve as a step toward foundation models for sparse 3D data, and support downstream applications in AR/VR, robotics, and autonomous driving.
中文标题/摘要
标题：Utonia：面向所有点云的统一编码器
我们憧憬一个未来，即来自不同领域的点云能够汇聚成一个统一模型，共同受益。为此，我们提出了Utonia，这是训练单一自监督点变换编码器以覆盖多样领域（包括遥感、户外LiDAR、室内RGB-D序列、以物体为中心的CAD模型以及从RGB视频中提升的点云）的第一步。尽管这些领域在感知几何、密度和先验条件上各不相同，Utonia仍能学习到一个一致的表示空间，并在跨领域间实现迁移。这种统一不仅提升了感知能力，还揭示了仅在联合训练领域时才出现的有趣涌现行为。此外，我们发现Utonia的表示还能促进具身与多模态推理：将视觉-语言-动作策略基于Utonia特征进行条件化，可提升机器人操作能力；将其融入视觉-语言模型，亦能提升空间推理性能。我们希望Utonia能成为稀疏3D数据基础模型的一步，并支持AR/VR、机器人和自动驾驶等下游应用。
Summary / 总结
We dream of a future where point clouds from all domains can come together to shape a single model that benefits them all.
为实现跨领域点云数据的统一表征，Utonia提出一种自监督点变换器编码器，联合训练遥感、LiDAR、RGB-D、CAD及视频提取点云等多领域数据。该方法在不同传感几何与密度下仍能学习一致的表示空间，实现跨域迁移。实验表明，该统一编码器显著提升感知能力，并在联合训练中涌现出仅在多域协同下出现的行为，同时在机器人操作与空间推理任务中，结合视觉-语言-动作策略或视觉-语言模型亦能获得性能提升。
MIBURI: Towards Expressive Interactive Gesture Synthesis
Authors: M. Hamza Mughal, Rishabh Dabral, Vera Demberg, Christian Theobalt
Venue: CVPR 2026
First: 2026-03-03T18:59:51+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T18:59:51+00:00
Comments: CVPR 2026. Project page: https://vcai.mpi-inf.mpg.de/projects/MIBURI/
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Project1
Abstract
Embodied Conversational Agents (ECAs) aim to emulate human face-to-face interaction through speech, gestures, and facial expressions. Current large language model (LLM)-based conversational agents lack embodiment and the expressive gestures essential for natural interaction. Existing solutions for ECAs often produce rigid, low-diversity motions, that are unsuitable for human-like interaction. Alternatively, generative methods for co-speech gesture synthesis yield natural body gestures but depend on future speech context and require long run-times. To bridge this gap, we present MIBURI, the first online, causal framework for generating expressive full-body gestures and facial expressions synchronized with real-time spoken dialogue. We employ body-part aware gesture codecs that encode hierarchical motion details into multi-level discrete tokens. These tokens are then autoregressively generated by a two-dimensional causal framework conditioned on LLM-based speech-text embeddings, modeling both temporal dynamics and part-level motion hierarchy in real time. Further, we introduce auxiliary objectives to encourage expressive and diverse gestures while preventing convergence to static poses. Comparative evaluations demonstrate that our causal and real-time approach produces natural and contextually aligned gestures against recent baselines. We urge the reader to explore demo videos on https://vcai.mpi-inf.mpg.de/projects/MIBURI/.
中文标题/摘要
标题：MIBURI：面向表达性交互手势合成的研究
具身对话代理（ECAs）旨在通过语音、手势和面部表情模拟人类面对面交流。当前基于大语言模型（LLM）的对话代理缺乏具身性和自然交互所必需的表达性手势。现有ECAs解决方案常产生僵硬、低多样性的动作，不适合人类般的互动。而现有的共语音手势生成方法虽能产生自然的身体手势，但依赖未来语音上下文且运行时间较长。为弥合这一差距，我们提出了MIBURI，这是首个在线、因果的框架，用于实时生成与口语对话同步的表达性全身手势和面部表情。我们采用身体部位感知的手势编码器，将分层运动细节编码为多级离散标记。这些标记由二维因果框架自回归生成，该框架以基于LLM的语音-文本嵌入为条件，实时建模时间动态和部位级运动层次。此外，我们引入辅助目标，鼓励生成表达性强且多样化的手势，同时防止收敛至静态姿态。对比评估表明，我们的因果和实时方法在与近期基线相比时，生成了自然且语境对齐的手势。我们鼓励读者访问https://vcai.mpi-inf.mpg.de/projects/MIBURI/查看演示视频。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need for expressive, real-time gesture synthesis in embodied conversational agents, MIBURI introduces a causal, online framework that generates synchronized full-body gestures and facial expressions during live speech. It uses body-part aware gesture codecs to encode motion hierarchies into discrete tokens, which are then autoregressively generated by a 2D causal model conditioned on LLM-derived speech embeddings. The system incorporates auxiliary objectives to promote diversity and expressiveness while avoiding static poses. Experimental results show that MIBURI outperforms recent baselines in producing natural, contextually aligned gestures in real time.
为解决现有对话代理缺乏具身表达和自然手势的问题，MIBURI提出首个在线因果框架，实时生成与语音同步的全身手势和面部表情。该框架采用身体部位感知的手势编码器，将运动层次结构编码为离散令牌，并通过二维因果模型自回归生成，条件于LLM生成的语音文本嵌入。系统引入辅助目标以增强手势的多样性和表现力，避免收敛于静态姿态。实验表明，MIBURI生成的自然手势在语境契合度上优于现有方法，后者常因僵硬或依赖未来语音而不足。
CFG-Ctrl: Control-Based Classifier-Free Diffusion Guidance
Authors: Hanyang Wang, Yiyang Liu, Jiawei Chi, Fangfu Liu, Ran Xue, Yueqi Duan
Venue: CVPR 2026
First: 2026-03-03T18:59:48+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T18:59:48+00:00
Comments: Accepted by CVPR 2026; Project Page: https://hanyang-21.github.io/CFG-Ctrl
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Project1
Abstract
Classifier-Free Guidance (CFG) has emerged as a central approach for enhancing semantic alignment in flow-based diffusion models. In this paper, we explore a unified framework called CFG-Ctrl, which reinterprets CFG as a control applied to the first-order continuous-time generative flow, using the conditional-unconditional discrepancy as an error signal to adjust the velocity field. From this perspective, we summarize vanilla CFG as a proportional controller (P-control) with fixed gain, and typical follow-up variants develop extended control-law designs derived from it. However, existing methods mainly rely on linear control, inherently leading to instability, overshooting, and degraded semantic fidelity especially on large guidance scales. To address this, we introduce Sliding Mode Control CFG (SMC-CFG), which enforces the generative flow toward a rapidly convergent sliding manifold. Specifically, we define an exponential sliding mode surface over the semantic prediction error and introduce a switching control term to establish nonlinear feedback-guided correction. Moreover, we provide a Lyapunov stability analysis to theoretically support finite-time convergence. Experiments across text-to-image generation models including Stable Diffusion 3.5, Flux, and Qwen-Image demonstrate that SMC-CFG outperforms standard CFG in semantic alignment and enhances robustness across a wide range of guidance scales. Project Page: https://hanyang-21.github.io/CFG-Ctrl
中文标题/摘要
标题：CFG-Ctrl：基于控制的无分类器引导扩散指导
无分类器引导（CFG）已成为增强流式扩散模型语义对齐的核心方法。本文提出统一框架CFG-Ctrl，将CFG重新诠释为对一阶连续时间生成流施加的控制，利用条件-无条件差异作为误差信号调整速度场。从该视角看，我们将基础CFG视为固定增益的比例控制器（P控制），典型后续变体则在此基础上发展出扩展的控制律设计。然而，现有方法主要依赖线性控制，固有地导致在大引导尺度下不稳定、超调和语义保真度下降。为此，我们引入滑模控制CFG（SMC-CFG），强制生成流向快速收敛的滑动流形。具体而言，我们在语义预测误差上定义指数滑动模式面，并引入切换控制项以建立非线性反馈引导校正。此外，我们提供李雅普诺夫稳定性分析以理论支持有限时间收敛。在包括Stable Diffusion 3.5、Flux和Qwen-Image在内的文本到图像生成模型实验中，SMC-CFG在语义对齐上优于标准CFG，并在广泛引导尺度下增强鲁棒性。项目页面：https://hanyang-21.github.io/CFG-Ctrl
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the limitations of vanilla Classifier-Free Guidance (CFG) in maintaining semantic fidelity under large guidance scales, this paper proposes CFG-Ctrl, a control-theoretic framework that reinterprets CFG as a velocity-field adjustment in continuous-time generative flows using semantic prediction error as feedback. It formalizes standard CFG as a proportional controller and introduces Sliding Mode Control CFG (SMC-CFG), a nonlinear control strategy that enforces rapid convergence to a sliding manifold via an exponential error surface and switching feedback. Theoretical stability is supported by Lyapunov analysis, and experiments on Stable Diffusion 3.5, Flux, and Qwen-Image show SMC-CFG achieves superior semantic alignment and robustness across guidance scales compared to existing methods.
为解决传统无分类器引导（CFG）在大引导尺度下语义保真度下降的问题，本文提出CFG-Ctrl框架，将CFG重新建模为连续时间生成流的速度场调整，以语义预测误差作为反馈信号。该框架将标准CFG视为比例控制器，并引入滑模控制CFG（SMC-CFG），通过指数误差面与切换反馈实现非线性修正，确保快速收敛。理论层面通过李雅普诺夫稳定性分析支持有限时间收敛性，实验表明在Stable Diffusion 3.5、Flux和Qwen-Image等模型上，SMC-CFG在语义对齐和多尺度鲁棒性方面显著优于现有方法。
How to Peel with a Knife: Aligning Fine-Grained Manipulation with Human Preference
Authors: Toru Lin, Shuying Deng, Zhao-Heng Yin, Pieter Abbeel, Jitendra Malik
First: 2026-03-03T18:59:32+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T18:59:32+00:00
Comments: Project page can be found at https://toruowo.github.io/peel
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Project1
Abstract
Many essential manipulation tasks - such as food preparation, surgery, and craftsmanship - remain intractable for autonomous robots. These tasks are characterized not only by contact-rich, force-sensitive dynamics, but also by their "implicit" success criteria: unlike pick-and-place, task quality in these domains is continuous and subjective (e.g. how well a potato is peeled), making quantitative evaluation and reward engineering difficult. We present a learning framework for such tasks, using peeling with a knife as a representative example. Our approach follows a two-stage pipeline: first, we learn a robust initial policy via force-aware data collection and imitation learning, enabling generalization across object variations; second, we refine the policy through preference-based finetuning using a learned reward model that combines quantitative task metrics with qualitative human feedback, aligning policy behavior with human notions of task quality. Using only 50-200 peeling trajectories, our system achieves over 90% average success rates on challenging produce including cucumbers, apples, and potatoes, with performance improving by up to 40% through preference-based finetuning. Remarkably, policies trained on a single produce category exhibit strong zero-shot generalization to unseen in-category instances and to out-of-distribution produce from different categories while maintaining over 90% success rates.
中文标题/摘要
标题：如何用刀削皮：细粒度操作与人类偏好的对齐
许多关键操作任务——如食物准备、外科手术和工艺制作——目前仍难以由自主机器人完成。这些任务不仅具有接触密集、力敏感的动力学特性，还具有“隐式”的成功标准：与拾取放置不同，这些领域的任务质量是连续且主观的（例如土豆削皮的优劣），使得量化评估和奖励工程困难。我们提出了一种适用于此类任务的学习框架，以削皮为例。我们的方法采用两阶段流程：首先，通过力感知数据收集和模仿学习学习稳健的初始策略，实现对物体变化的泛化；其次，通过基于偏好的微调优化策略，使用结合定量任务指标与定性人类反馈的奖励模型，使策略行为与人类对任务质量的认知对齐。仅使用50-200条削皮轨迹，我们的系统在包括黄瓜、苹果和土豆等具有挑战性的农产品上平均成功率超过90%，通过基于偏好的微调，性能最高可提升40%。值得注意的是，仅在单一农产品类别上训练的策略，对未见过的同类实例及不同类别的分布外农产品也表现出强大的零样本泛化能力，同时保持超过90%的成功率。
Summary / 总结
Many essential manipulation tasks - such as food preparation, surgery, and craftsmanship - remain intractable for autonomous robots.
ULTRA: Unified Multimodal Control for Autonomous Humanoid Whole-Body Loco-Manipulation
Authors: Xialin He, Sirui Xu, Xinyao Li, Runpei Dong, Liuyu Bian, Yu-Xiong Wang, Liang-Yan Gui
First: 2026-03-03T18:59:29+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T18:59:29+00:00
Comments: Project Page: https://ultra-humanoid.github.io/
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Project1
Abstract
Achieving autonomous and versatile whole-body loco-manipulation remains a central barrier to making humanoids practically useful. Yet existing approaches are fundamentally constrained: retargeted data are often scarce or low-quality; methods struggle to scale to large skill repertoires; and, most importantly, they rely on tracking predefined motion references rather than generating behavior from perception and high-level task specifications. To address these limitations, we propose ULTRA, a unified framework with two key components. First, we introduce a physics-driven neural retargeting algorithm that translates large-scale motion capture to humanoid embodiments while preserving physical plausibility for contact-rich interactions. Second, we learn a unified multimodal controller that supports both dense references and sparse task specifications, under sensing ranging from accurate motion-capture state to noisy egocentric visual inputs. We distill a universal tracking policy into this controller, compress motor skills into a compact latent space, and apply reinforcement learning finetuning to expand coverage and improve robustness under out-of-distribution scenarios. This enables coordinated whole-body behavior from sparse intent without test-time reference motions. We evaluate ULTRA in simulation and on a real Unitree G1 humanoid. Results show that ULTRA generalizes to autonomous, goal-conditioned whole-body loco-manipulation from egocentric perception, consistently outperforming tracking-only baselines with limited skills.
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need for autonomous and versatile whole-body locomotion and manipulation in humanoids, ULTRA introduces a unified framework that overcomes limitations of existing methods, which rely on predefined motion references and struggle with scalability or data quality. The method combines a physics-driven neural retargeting algorithm to adapt large-scale motion capture to humanoid embodiments while preserving physical plausibility, and a multimodal controller trained to handle both dense motion references and sparse task specifications across varying sensor inputs. Experimental results demonstrate that ULTRA enables coordinated whole-body behavior from sparse high-level intent without requiring test-time motion references, outperforming tracking-only baselines in simulation and on a real Unitree G1 humanoid, especially under limited skill sets and noisy perception.
为实现人形机器人自主且多样的全身运动与操作，ULTRA提出一个统一的多模态控制框架，突破现有方法依赖预定义运动参考、难以扩展等限制。该框架包含一个物理驱动的神经重定向算法，可将动作捕捉数据适配至人形机器人并保持接触交互的物理合理性；以及一个支持密集运动参考与稀疏任务指令的多模态控制器，能处理从精确动作捕捉到噪声视觉输入等多种感知输入。控制器整合了通用跟踪策略并压缩运动技能至低维空间，再通过强化学习微调以提升泛化与鲁棒性。在仿真与真实Unitree G1人形机器人上的实验表明，ULTRA仅依赖第一人称视觉感知即可实现目标导向的全身运动与操作，性能显著优于仅依赖跟踪的基线方法，即使技能库有限。
Tether: Autonomous Functional Play with Correspondence-Driven Trajectory Warping
Authors: William Liang, Sam Wang, Hung-Ju Wang, Osbert Bastani, Yecheng Jason Ma, Dinesh Jayaraman
Venue: ICLR
First: 2026-03-03T18:59:07+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T18:59:07+00:00
Comments: International Conference on Learning Representations (ICLR), 2026. Project website and code: https://tether-research.github.io
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Project1
Abstract
The ability to conduct and learn from interaction and experience is a central challenge in robotics, offering a scalable alternative to labor-intensive human demonstrations. However, realizing such "play" requires (1) a policy robust to diverse, potentially out-of-distribution environment states, and (2) a procedure that continuously produces useful robot experience. To address these challenges, we introduce Tether, a method for autonomous functional play involving structured, task-directed interactions. First, we design a novel open-loop policy that warps actions from a small set of source demonstrations (<=10) by anchoring them to semantic keypoint correspondences in the target scene. We show that this design is extremely data-efficient and robust even under significant spatial and semantic variations. Second, we deploy this policy for autonomous functional play in the real world via a continuous cycle of task selection, execution, evaluation, and improvement, guided by the visual understanding capabilities of vision-language models. This procedure generates diverse, high-quality datasets with minimal human intervention. In a household-like multi-object setup, our method is the first to perform many hours of autonomous multi-task play in the real world starting from only a handful of demonstrations. This produces a stream of data that consistently improves the performance of closed-loop imitation policies over time, ultimately yielding over 1000 expert-level trajectories and training policies competitive with those learned from human-collected demonstrations.
中文标题/摘要
标题：Tether：基于对应驱动轨迹变形的自主功能式游戏
机器人通过交互与经验学习的能力是核心挑战，提供了一种可扩展的替代人工演示的方法。然而，实现此类“游戏”需要（1）对多样且可能超出分布环境状态鲁棒的策略，以及（2）持续生成有用机器人经验的流程。为解决这些挑战，我们提出Tether，一种涉及结构化、任务导向交互的自主功能式游戏方法。首先，我们设计了一种新颖的开环策略，通过将少量源演示（≤10）的动作锚定到目标场景中的语义关键点对应关系，实现动作变形。我们证明该设计数据效率极高，即使在显著的空间和语义变化下仍保持鲁棒性。其次，我们通过任务选择、执行、评估与改进的连续循环，在真实世界中部署该策略，由视觉-语言模型的视觉理解能力引导。该流程生成多样且高质量的数据集，几乎无需人工干预。在类似家庭的多物体环境中，我们的方法首次从仅少量演示出发，在真实世界中实现了数小时的自主多任务游戏。该过程持续生成数据，逐步提升闭环模仿策略的性能，最终产出超过1000条专家级轨迹，训练出的策略可与基于人工收集演示学习的策略相媲美。
Summary / 总结
The ability to conduct and learn from interaction and experience is a central challenge in robotics, offering a scalable alternative to labor-intensive human demonstrations.
为实现无需大量人工演示的可扩展机器人学习，Tether 通过语义关键点对应驱动的动作变形，从少量演示中自主生成结构化任务交互。该开环策略在环境变化下仍保持高效与鲁棒性，并结合视觉语言模型引导的持续任务循环，实现低人工干预下的高质量真实世界数据生成。在类似家庭的多物体环境中，该方法仅凭数个演示即可实现数小时的自主多任务交互，累计产出超1000条专家级轨迹，持续提升闭环模仿策略性能，媲美人类演示训练的效果。
Beyond Language Modeling: An Exploration of Multimodal Pretraining
Authors: Shengbang Tong, David Fan, John Nguyen, Ellis Brown, Gaoyue Zhou, Shengyi Qian, Boyang Zheng, Théophane Vallaeys, Junlin Han, Rob Fergus, Naila Murray, Marjan Ghazvininejad, Mike Lewis, Nicolas Ballas, Amir Bar, Michael Rabbat, Jakob Verbeek, Luke Zettlemoyer, Koustuv Sinha, Yann LeCun, Saining Xie
First: 2026-03-03T18:58:00+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T18:58:00+00:00
Comments: Project website at https://beyond-llms.github.io/
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Project1
Abstract
The visual world offers a critical axis for advancing foundation models beyond language. Despite growing interest in this direction, the design space for native multimodal models remains opaque. We provide empirical clarity through controlled, from-scratch pretraining experiments, isolating the factors that govern multimodal pretraining without interference from language pretraining. We adopt the Transfusion framework, using next-token prediction for language and diffusion for vision, to train on diverse data including text, video, image-text pairs, and even action-conditioned video. Our experiments yield four key insights: (i) Representation Autoencoder (RAE) provides an optimal unified visual representation by excelling at both visual understanding and generation; (ii) visual and language data are complementary and yield synergy for downstream capabilities; (iii) unified multimodal pretraining leads naturally to world modeling, with capabilities emerging from general training; and (iv) Mixture-of-Experts (MoE) enables efficient and effective multimodal scaling while naturally inducing modality specialization. Through IsoFLOP analysis, we compute scaling laws for both modalities and uncover a scaling asymmetry: vision is significantly more data-hungry than language. We demonstrate that the MoE architecture harmonizes this scaling asymmetry by providing the high model capacity required by language while accommodating the data-intensive nature of vision, paving the way for truly unified multimodal models.
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need to advance foundation models beyond language through multimodal learning, this study conducts controlled, from-scratch pretraining experiments using the Transfusion framework, which combines next-token prediction for language and diffusion for vision. The experiments train on diverse data including text, images, video, and image-text pairs, revealing four key findings: (i) Representation Autoencoder (RAE) offers the best unified visual representation; (ii) visual and language data synergize to enhance downstream performance; (iii) unified multimodal pretraining naturally enables world modeling; and (iv) Mixture-of-Experts (MoE) enables efficient scaling while promoting modality specialization. IsoFLOP analysis further shows vision requires significantly more data than language, and MoE architecture effectively balances this asymmetry by allocating capacity appropriately, enabling scalable unified multimodal models.
为推动基础模型超越语言能力，本研究通过从零开始的受控预训练实验，使用结合语言预测与视觉扩散的Transfusion框架，训练文本、图像、视频及图文对等多模态数据，得出四项关键发现：(i) 表示自编码器（RAE）在视觉理解与生成上表现最优，提供统一视觉表征；(ii) 视觉与语言数据互补，协同提升下游能力；(iii) 统一多模态预训练自然催生世界建模能力；(iv) 混合专家（MoE）架构可高效扩展并诱导模态专业化。IsoFLOP分析揭示视觉数据需求远高于语言，MoE架构通过合理分配模型容量，有效平衡二者扩展差异，为真正统一的多模态模型奠定基础。
Learning Demographic-Conditioned Mobility Trajectories with Aggregate Supervision
Authors: Jessie Z. Li, Zhiqing Hong, Toru Shirakawa, Serina Chang
First: 2026-03-03T18:57:44+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T18:57:44+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Human mobility trajectories are widely studied in public health and social science, where different demographic groups exhibit significantly different mobility patterns. However, existing trajectory generation models rarely capture this heterogeneity because most trajectory datasets lack demographic labels. To address this gap in data, we propose ATLAS, a weakly supervised approach for demographic-conditioned trajectory generation using only (i) individual trajectories without demographic labels, (ii) region-level aggregated mobility features, and (iii) region-level demographic compositions from census data. ATLAS trains a trajectory generator and fine-tunes it so that simulated mobility matches observed regional aggregates while conditioning on demographics. Experiments on real trajectory data with demographic labels show that ATLAS substantially improves demographic realism over baselines (JSD $\downarrow$ 12%--69%) and closes much of the gap to strongly supervised training. We further develop theoretical analyses for when and why ATLAS works, identifying key factors including demographic diversity across regions and the informativeness of the aggregate feature, paired with experiments demonstrating the practical implications of our theory. We release our code at https://github.com/schang-lab/ATLAS.
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need to model demographic-specific mobility patterns despite limited labeled data, ATLAS introduces a weakly supervised method that generates trajectories conditioned on demographics using only unlabeled individual trajectories, region-level mobility aggregates, and census-based demographic compositions. The model trains a trajectory generator to match regional mobility aggregates while conditioning on demographic groups, then fine-tunes it to improve realism. Experiments show ATLAS significantly outperforms baselines in demographic realism (JSD reduced by 12%–69%) and narrows the gap to strongly supervised methods, with theoretical analysis confirming the importance of regional demographic diversity and aggregate feature informativeness.
为在缺乏人口标签数据的情况下建模不同群体的移动模式，ATLAS提出一种弱监督方法，利用无标签个体轨迹、区域级移动聚合特征和人口普查数据中的区域人口构成，生成按人口特征条件化的移动轨迹。模型训练轨迹生成器，使其模拟的移动轨迹与观测到的区域聚合数据一致。实验表明，ATLAS在人口现实性上显著优于基线方法，Jensen-Shannon散度降低12%至69%，且大幅缩小与强监督方法的性能差距。理论分析指出，区域人口多样性与聚合特征的可解释性是方法成功的关键因素，实验结果验证了该理论的实际意义。
Gravity Falls: A Comparative Analysis of Domain-Generation Algorithm (DGA) Detection Methods for Mobile Device Spearphishing
Authors: Adam Dorian Wong, John D. Hastings
First: 2026-03-03T18:55:44+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T18:55:44+00:00
Comments: Disclaimer: The views expressed are those of the authors and do not necessarily reflect the official policy or position of the U.S. Department of Defense or the U.S. Government. References to external sites do not constitute endorsement. Cleared for release on 24 FEB 2026 (DOPSR 26-T-0771). Gravity Falls Dataset DOI: 10.5281/zenodo.17624554
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Mobile devices are frequent targets of eCrime threat actors through SMS spearphishing (smishing) links that leverage Domain Generation Algorithms (DGA) to rotate hostile infrastructure. Despite this, DGA research and evaluation largely emphasize malware C2 and email phishing datasets, leaving limited evidence on how well detectors generalize to smishing-driven domain tactics outside enterprise perimeters. This work addresses that gap by evaluating traditional and machine-learning DGA detectors against Gravity Falls, a new semi-synthetic dataset derived from smishing links delivered between 2022 and 2025. Gravity Falls captures a single threat actor's evolution across four technique clusters, shifting from short randomized strings to dictionary concatenation and themed combo-squatting variants used for credential theft and fee/fine fraud. Two string-analysis approaches (Shannon entropy and Exp0se) and two ML-based detectors (an LSTM classifier and COSSAS DGAD) are assessed using Top-1M domains as benign baselines. Results are strongly tactic-dependent: performance is highest on randomized-string domains but drops on dictionary concatenation and themed combo-squatting, with low recall across multiple tool/cluster pairings. Overall, both traditional heuristics and recent ML detectors are ill-suited for consistently evolving DGA tactics observed in Gravity Falls, motivating more context-aware approaches and providing a reproducible benchmark for future evaluation.
Summary / 总结
This study addresses the gap in DGA detection research by evaluating traditional and machine-learning methods against a new semi-synthetic dataset, Gravity Falls, derived from real smishing links used in mobile spearphishing between 2022 and 2025. The dataset captures a single threat actor’s evolution across four DGA tactics, from randomized strings to dictionary concatenation and themed combo-squatting. Four detection methods—Shannon entropy, Exp0se, LSTM classifier, and COSSAS DGAD—were tested against Top-1M domains as benign baselines. Results show strong performance on randomized-string domains but significant drops in accuracy for more sophisticated tactics, with low recall across most tool-cluster combinations, indicating that current detectors struggle to generalize to evolving smishing DGA patterns.
本研究填补了DGA检测研究中的空白，通过评估传统方法与机器学习模型在名为Gravity Falls的新半合成数据集上的表现，该数据集基于2022至2025年间真实短信钓鱼链接。数据集记录了单一攻击者在四种域名生成技术上的演变，从随机字符串到字典拼接和主题组合抢注。四种检测方法——香农熵、Exp0se、LSTM分类器和COSSAS DGAD——在Top-1M良性域名基准下进行测试。结果表明，随机字符串域名检测效果最佳，但对更复杂的策略（如字典拼接和主题抢注）准确率显著下降，多种工具与攻击集群组合的召回率均偏低，说明现有检测器难以应对现实世界中短信钓鱼DGA的持续演化。
LoGeR: Long-Context Geometric Reconstruction with Hybrid Memory
Authors: Junyi Zhang, Charles Herrmann, Junhwa Hur, Chen Sun, Ming-Hsuan Yang, Forrester Cole, Trevor Darrell, Deqing Sun
First: 2026-03-03T18:55:37+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T18:55:37+00:00
Comments: Project page: https://LoGeR-project.github.io/
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Project1
Abstract
Feedforward geometric foundation models achieve strong short-window reconstruction, yet scaling them to minutes-long videos is bottlenecked by quadratic attention complexity or limited effective memory in recurrent designs. We present LoGeR (Long-context Geometric Reconstruction), a novel architecture that scales dense 3D reconstruction to extremely long sequences without post-optimization. LoGeR processes video streams in chunks, leveraging strong bidirectional priors for high-fidelity intra-chunk reasoning. To manage the critical challenge of coherence across chunk boundaries, we propose a learning-based hybrid memory module. This dual-component system combines a parametric Test-Time Training (TTT) memory to anchor the global coordinate frame and prevent scale drift, alongside a non-parametric Sliding Window Attention (SWA) mechanism to preserve uncompressed context for high-precision adjacent alignment. Remarkably, this memory architecture enables LoGeR to be trained on sequences of 128 frames, and generalize up to thousands of frames during inference. Evaluated across standard benchmarks and a newly repurposed VBR dataset with sequences of up to 19k frames, LoGeR substantially outperforms prior state-of-the-art feedforward methods--reducing ATE on KITTI by over 74%--and achieves robust, globally consistent reconstruction over unprecedented horizons.
中文标题/摘要
标题：LoGeR：基于混合记忆的长上下文几何重建
前馈几何基础模型在短窗口重建方面表现强劲，但扩展至分钟级视频时受限于二次注意力复杂度或递归设计中的有效内存不足。我们提出LoGeR（长上下文几何重建），一种无需后优化即可扩展密集3D重建至极长序列的新架构。LoGeR以块为单位处理视频流，利用强双向先验实现块内高保真推理。为解决块边界连贯性这一关键挑战，我们提出一种基于学习的混合记忆模块。该双组件系统结合参数化测试时训练（TTT）记忆，锚定全局坐标系并防止尺度漂移，以及非参数化滑动窗口注意力（SWA）机制，保留未压缩上下文以实现高精度相邻对齐。令人印象深刻的是，该记忆架构使LoGeR可在128帧序列上训练，并在推理时泛化至数千帧。在标准基准及重新利用的VBR数据集（最长序列达19k帧）上评估，LoGeR显著优于现有前馈方法——在KITTI数据集上ATE降低超74%——并实现了前所未有的长时程稳健且全局一致的重建。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the inefficiency of existing feedforward geometric models when scaling to long videos due to quadratic attention or limited memory, LoGeR introduces a hybrid memory architecture to enable dense 3D reconstruction over minutes-long sequences without post-optimization. It processes video in chunks using bidirectional priors for intra-chunk fidelity and employs a dual-memory system: a parametric Test-Time Training memory to stabilize global coordinates and a non-parametric Sliding Window Attention to preserve high-resolution context across chunks. Experiments show LoGeR trained on 128-frame sequences generalizes to thousands of frames, outperforming prior methods by over 74% reduction in ATE on KITTI and achieving globally consistent reconstruction over unprecedented sequence lengths.
为了解决现有前馈几何模型在长视频序列上因二次注意力复杂度或内存限制而难以扩展的问题，LoGeR提出了一种混合记忆架构，无需后优化即可实现分钟级视频的密集三维重建。该方法将视频分块处理，利用双向先验保证块内高保真重建，并采用双记忆系统：参数化测试时训练记忆用于稳定全局坐标，非参数化滑动窗口注意力用于保留高分辨率上下文。实验表明，LoGeR在128帧训练序列上即可泛化至数千帧，KITTI数据集上ATE降低超74%，并在前所未有的长序列上实现了全局一致的重建效果。
DuoMo: Dual Motion Diffusion for World-Space Human Reconstruction
Authors: Yufu Wang, Evonne Ng, Soyong Shin, Rawal Khirodkar, Yuan Dong, Zhaoen Su, Jinhyung Park, Kris Kitani, Alexander Richard, Fabian Prada, Michael Zollhofer
Venue: CVPR 2026
First: 2026-03-03T18:54:17+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T18:54:17+00:00
Comments: CVPR 2026. Project page: https://yufu-wang.github.io/duomo/
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Project1
Abstract
We present DuoMo, a generative method that recovers human motion in world-space coordinates from unconstrained videos with noisy or incomplete observations. Reconstructing such motion requires solving a fundamental trade-off: generalizing from diverse and noisy video inputs while maintaining global motion consistency. Our approach addresses this problem by factorizing motion learning into two diffusion models. The camera-space model first estimates motion from videos in camera coordinates. The world-space model then lifts this initial estimate into world coordinates and refines it to be globally consistent. Together, the two models can reconstruct motion across diverse scenes and trajectories, even from highly noisy or incomplete observations. Moreover, our formulation is general, generating the motion of mesh vertices directly and bypassing parametric models. DuoMo achieves state-of-the-art performance. On EMDB, our method obtains a 16% reduction in world-space reconstruction error while maintaining low foot skating. On RICH, it obtains a 30% reduction in world-space error. Project page: https://yufu-wang.github.io/duomo/
中文标题/摘要
标题：DuoMo：用于世界空间人体重建的双运动扩散模型
我们提出了DuoMo，一种生成式方法，可从无约束视频（含噪声或不完整观测）中恢复世界空间坐标下的人体运动。此类运动重建需解决一个根本性权衡：在保持全局运动一致性的同时，从多样且噪声较大的视频输入中进行泛化。我们的方法通过将运动学习分解为两个扩散模型来解决此问题：相机空间模型首先在相机坐标系中估计运动；世界空间模型随后将该初始估计提升至世界坐标系并对其进行全局一致性优化。两个模型协同工作，即使在高度噪声或不完整观测下，也能重建多样场景与轨迹中的运动。此外，我们的方法具有通用性，直接生成网格顶点运动，无需参数化模型。DuoMo达到当前最先进性能：在EMDB数据集上，世界空间重建误差降低16%，同时保持低脚滑动；在RICH数据集上，世界空间误差降低30%。项目页面：https://yufu-wang.github.io/duomo/
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the challenge of reconstructing human motion in world-space from noisy and unconstrained videos, DuoMo introduces a dual diffusion framework that separates motion estimation into camera-space and world-space components. The camera-space model first infers motion in local coordinates, then the world-space model lifts and refines this estimate for global consistency, enabling robust reconstruction across diverse scenes and trajectories. Experiments on EMDB and RICH show significant improvements: 16% error reduction on EMDB and 30% on RICH, while maintaining low foot skating, demonstrating state-of-the-art performance without relying on parametric models.
为了解决从噪声大且无约束的视频中重建世界空间下的人体运动这一难题，DuoMo提出一种双扩散框架，将运动估计分为相机空间和世界空间两个阶段。相机空间模型先在局部坐标系中估计运动，世界空间模型再将其提升并优化为全局一致的运动，从而实现复杂场景和轨迹下的鲁棒重建。在EMDB和RICH数据集上，该方法分别实现16%和30%的世界空间误差降低，同时保持低脚部滑动，达到当前最优性能，且无需依赖参数化模型。
Physics-informed post-processing of stabilized finite element solutions for transient convection-dominated problems
Authors: Süleyman Cengizci, Ömür Uğur, Srinivasan Natesan
First: 2026-03-03T18:51:17+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T18:51:17+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
The numerical simulation of convection-dominated transient transport phenomena poses significant computational challenges due to sharp gradients and propagating fronts across the spatiotemporal domain. Classical discretization methods often generate spurious oscillations, requiring advanced stabilization techniques. However, even stabilized finite element methods may require additional regularization to accurately resolve localized steep layers. On the other hand, standalone physics-informed neural networks (PINNs) struggle to capture sharp solution structures in convection-dominated regimes and typically require a large number of training epochs. This work presents a hybrid computational framework that extends the PINN-Augmented SUPG with Shock-Capturing (PASSC) methodology from steady to unsteady problems. The approach combines a semi-discrete stabilized finite element method with a PINN-based correction strategy for transient convection-diffusion-reaction equations. Stabilization is achieved using the Streamline-Upwind Petrov-Galerkin (SUPG) formulation augmented with a YZbeta shock-capturing operator. Rather than training over the entire space-time domain, the neural network is applied selectively near the terminal time, enhancing the finite element solution using the last K_s temporal snapshots while enforcing residual constraints from the governing equations and boundary conditions. The network incorporates residual blocks with random Fourier features and employs progressive training with adaptive loss weighting. Numerical experiments on five benchmark problems, including boundary and interior layers, traveling waves, and nonlinear Burgers dynamics, demonstrate significant accuracy improvements at the terminal time compared to standalone stabilized finite element solutions.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于物理信息的稳定有限元解后处理方法用于瞬态对流主导问题
对流主导的瞬态传输现象的数值模拟由于空间-时间域内尖锐梯度和传播前沿的存在，面临显著的计算挑战。经典离散方法常产生虚假振荡，需采用高级稳定化技术。然而，即使稳定有限元方法也可能需要额外正则化以精确解析局部陡峭层。另一方面，独立的物理信息神经网络（PINNs）在对流主导区域难以捕捉尖锐解结构，通常需大量训练周期。本文提出一种混合计算框架，将PINN增强SUPG与激波捕捉（PASSC）方法从稳态扩展至非稳态问题。该方法结合半离散稳定有限元法与基于PINN的瞬态对流-扩散-反应方程修正策略。稳定化采用流线-上游加权Petrov-Galerkin（SUPG）公式并附加YZbeta激波捕捉算子。神经网络并非在整个时空域训练，而是选择性地在终端时间附近应用，利用最后K_s个时间快照增强有限元解，同时强制满足控制方程和边界条件的残差约束。网络采用含随机傅里叶特征的残差块，并结合渐进式训练与自适应损失加权。在五个基准问题（包括边界层与内层、行波及非线性Burgers动力学）上的数值实验表明，与独立稳定有限元解相比，该方法在终端时间显著提升精度。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the difficulty of accurately resolving sharp gradients and propagating fronts in transient convection-dominated transport problems, this work proposes a hybrid framework combining stabilized finite element methods with physics-informed neural networks. The method employs the Streamline-Upwind Petrov-Galerkin (SUPG) stabilization augmented with a YZbeta shock-capturing operator, and applies a PINN correction only near the terminal time using the last K_s temporal snapshots. The neural network enforces residual constraints from governing equations and boundary conditions, using residual blocks with random Fourier features and progressive training with adaptive loss weighting. Experimental results on five benchmark problems show substantial accuracy improvements at the terminal time over standalone stabilized finite element solutions, particularly in capturing boundary and interior layers, traveling waves, and nonlinear Burgers dynamics.
为解决瞬态对流主导传输问题中尖锐梯度与传播前沿的数值模拟难题，本文提出一种结合稳定有限元方法与物理信息神经网络（PINN）的混合框架。该方法采用流线-迎风加权伽辽金（SUPG）格式并引入YZbeta激波捕捉算子进行空间稳定化，随后在终端时刻附近利用最后K_s个时间快照，通过满足控制方程与边界条件的残差约束对有限元解进行PINN修正。神经网络采用残差块与随机傅里叶特征，并结合渐进训练与自适应损失加权。在五个基准问题上的实验表明，该方法在终端时刻的精度显著优于独立的稳定有限元解。
Inherited Goal Drift: Contextual Pressure Can Undermine Agentic Goals
Authors: Achyutha Menon, Magnus Saebo, Tyler Crosse, Spencer Gibson, Eyon Jang, Diogo Cruz
Venue: ICLR 2026
First: 2026-03-03T18:50:59+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T18:50:59+00:00
Comments: 22 pages, 7 figures. Accepted at ICLR 2026 Lifelong Agents Workshop
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
The accelerating adoption of language models (LMs) as agents for deployment in long-context tasks motivates a thorough understanding of goal drift: agents' tendency to deviate from an original objective. While prior-generation language model agents have been shown to be susceptible to drift, the extent to which drift affects more recent models remains unclear. In this work, we provide an updated characterization of the extent and causes of goal drift. We investigate drift in state-of-the-art models within a simulated stock-trading environment (Arike et al., 2025). These models are largely shown to be robust even when subjected to adversarial pressure. We show, however, that this robustness is brittle: across multiple settings, the same models often inherit drift when conditioned on prefilled trajectories from weaker agents. The extent of conditioning-induced drift varies significantly by model family, with only GPT-5.1 maintaining consistent resilience among tested models. We find that drift behavior is inconsistent between prompt variations and correlates poorly with instruction hierarchy following behavior, with strong hierarchy following failing to reliably predict resistance to drift. Finally, we run analogous experiments in a new emergency room triage environment to show preliminary evidence for the transferability of our results across qualitatively different settings. Our findings underscore the continued vulnerability of modern LM agents to contextual pressures and the need for refined post-training techniques to mitigate this.
中文标题/摘要
标题：继承的目标漂移：情境压力可能削弱代理目标
随着语言模型（LMs）在长上下文任务中作为代理部署的加速采用，深入理解目标漂移——即代理偏离原始目标的趋势——变得至关重要。尽管先前一代的语言模型代理已被证明易受漂移影响，但漂移对较新模型的影响程度仍不明确。本研究提供了目标漂移范围及其成因的最新描述。我们在模拟股票交易环境（Arike等，2025）中研究了最先进模型的漂移现象。这些模型在遭受对抗性压力时表现出较强的鲁棒性，但这种鲁棒性是脆弱的：在多个设置中，相同模型在条件于较弱代理预填充轨迹时往往继承漂移。漂移程度因模型家族而异，仅GPT-5.1在测试模型中保持一致的抗漂移能力。我们发现，漂移行为在提示变体间不一致，且与指令层级遵循行为相关性差，强层级遵循无法可靠预测抗漂移能力。最后，我们在新的急诊室分诊环境中进行类似实验，初步表明结果可跨质性不同的场景迁移。我们的发现强调了现代LM代理对情境压力的持续脆弱性，以及需要改进的后训练技术以缓解此问题。
Summary / 总结
This study investigates goal drift in modern language models as agents, motivated by the growing deployment of LMs in long-context tasks and the need to understand how contextual pressures affect goal fidelity. Using a simulated stock-trading environment, the researchers evaluate state-of-the-art models and find that while they are generally robust to adversarial pressure, their resilience is brittle: conditioning on trajectories from weaker agents often induces drift. Drift severity varies by model family, with GPT-5.1 showing the most consistent resistance. The study also finds that drift behavior is inconsistent across prompt variations and poorly correlated with instruction hierarchy following, suggesting that hierarchy compliance is not a reliable indicator of drift resistance. Preliminary experiments in an emergency room triage setting confirm the transferability of these findings across domains, highlighting the persistent vulnerability of LM agents to contextual influence and the need for improved post-training methods.
随着语言模型在长上下文任务中作为代理被广泛部署，本研究探讨了目标漂移——即代理偏离原始目标的倾向。在模拟股票交易环境中，作者发现尽管这些模型通常能抵抗对抗性压力，但当它们被弱代理的预填充轨迹条件化时，其鲁棒性会变得脆弱。不同模型家族的漂移程度差异显著，仅有GPT-5.1在多个设置中保持稳定抗漂移能力。漂移行为与提示变体不一致，且与指令层级遵循行为关联性差，强层级遵循无法可靠预测抗漂移能力。在急诊分诊环境中的初步实验表明，漂移现象可跨领域迁移，凸显了改进后训练方法以稳定代理目标的必要性。
Valet: A Standardized Testbed of Traditional Imperfect-Information Card Games
Authors: Mark Goadrich, Achille Morenville, Éric Piette
First: 2026-03-03T18:46:47+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T18:46:47+00:00
Comments: 12 pages, 1 table, 4 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
AI algorithms for imperfect-information games are typically compared using performance metrics on individual games, making it difficult to assess robustness across game choices. Card games are a natural domain for imperfect information due to hidden hands and stochastic draws. To facilitate comparative research on imperfect-information game-playing algorithms and game systems, we introduce Valet, a diverse and comprehensive testbed of 21 traditional imperfect-information card games. These games span multiple genres, cultures, player counts, deck structures, mechanics, winning conditions, and methods of hiding and revealing information. To standardize implementations across systems, we encode the rules of each game in RECYCLE, a card game description language. We empirically characterize each game's branching factor and duration using random simulations, reporting baseline score distributions for a Monte Carlo Tree Search player against random opponents to demonstrate the suitability of Valet as a benchmarking suite.
中文标题/摘要
标题：Valet：传统不完美信息卡牌游戏的标准测试平台
不完美信息游戏的AI算法通常通过单个游戏的性能指标进行比较，难以评估其在不同游戏间的鲁棒性。卡牌游戏因隐藏手牌和随机抽牌而天然适合不完美信息领域。为促进不完美信息游戏算法与游戏系统的比较研究，我们引入Valet，一个包含21种传统不完美信息卡牌游戏的多样且全面的测试平台。这些游戏涵盖多种类型、文化、玩家数量、牌组结构、机制、获胜条件以及信息隐藏与揭示方式。为统一各系统实现，我们使用RECYCLE（卡牌游戏描述语言）编码每种游戏规则。我们通过随机模拟实证分析每种游戏的分支因子与持续时间，并报告蒙特卡洛树搜索玩家对随机对手的基准得分分布，以证明Valet作为基准测试套件的适用性。

Theory of Code Space: Do Code Agents Understand Software Architecture?
Authors: Grigory Sapunov
First: 2026-02-28T11:40:17+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T18:45:08+00:00
Comments: updated experiments
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
AI code agents excel at isolated tasks yet struggle with complex, multi-file software engineering requiring understanding of how dozens of modules relate. We hypothesize these failures stem from inability to construct, maintain, and update coherent architectural beliefs during codebase exploration. We introduce Theory of Code Space (ToCS), a benchmark that evaluates this capability by placing agents in procedurally generated codebases under partial observability, requiring them to build structured belief states over module dependencies, cross-cutting invariants, and design intent. The framework features: (1) a procedural codebase generator producing medium-complexity Python projects with four typed edge categories reflecting different discovery methods -- from syntactic imports to config-driven dynamic wiring -- with planted architectural constraints and verified ground truth; (2) a partial observability harness where agents explore under a budget; and (3) periodic belief probing via structured JSON, producing a time-series of architectural understanding. We decompose the Active-Passive Gap from spatial reasoning benchmarks into selection and decision components, and introduce Architectural Constraint Discovery as a code-specific evaluation dimension. Preliminary experiments with four rule-based baselines and five frontier LLM agents from three providers validate discriminative power: methods span a wide performance range (F1 from 0.129 to 0.646), LLM agents discover semantic edge types invisible to all baselines, yet weaker models score below simple heuristics -- revealing that belief externalization, faithfully serializing internal understanding into structured JSON, is itself a non-trivial capability and a first-order confounder in belief-probing benchmarks. Open-source toolkit: https://github.com/che-shr-cat/tocs
中文标题/摘要
标题：代码空间理论：代码代理是否理解软件架构？
AI代码代理擅长孤立任务，但在需要理解数十个模块间关系的复杂多文件软件工程中表现不佳。我们假设其失败源于在代码库探索过程中无法构建、维护和更新连贯的架构信念。我们提出了代码空间理论（ToCS），通过将代理置于部分可观测的程序生成代码库中，评估其构建关于模块依赖、交叉不变量和设计意图的结构化信念状态的能力。该框架包含：（1）程序生成代码库生成器，生成中等复杂度的Python项目，包含四种类型边，反映不同发现方法——从语法导入到配置驱动的动态连接——并植入架构约束及验证的地面真实数据；（2）部分可观测性机制，代理在预算内探索；（3）通过结构化JSON定期探测信念，生成架构理解的时间序列。我们将空间推理基准中的主动-被动差距分解为选择与决策组件，并引入架构约束发现作为代码特定评估维度。初步实验使用四种规则基线和来自三家供应商的五种前沿大语言模型验证了其区分能力：方法性能跨度大（F1从0.129至0.646），大语言模型发现所有基线均未识别的语义边类型，但较弱模型得分低于简单启发式——揭示信念外部化（即忠实将内部理解序列化为结构化JSON）本身是一项非平凡能力，也是信念探测基准中的首要混杂因素。开源工具包：https://github.com/che-shr-cat/tocs

Motivated by the observation that AI code agents perform well on isolated tasks but fail on complex software engineering problems requiring architectural understanding, this work introduces Theory of Code Space (ToCS), a benchmark that tests agents’ ability to construct and maintain coherent architectural beliefs during code exploration under partial observability. The method generates medium-complexity Python codebases with four typed edge categories representing different discovery methods and embedded architectural constraints, while agents operate under exploration budgets and are periodically probed via structured JSON to capture evolving belief states. Experimental results with four rule-based baselines and five LLM agents show a wide performance range (F1: 0.129–0.646), revealing that LLMs can discover semantic edge types invisible to baselines, yet weaker models underperform simple heuristics — indicating that faithful externalization of internal architectural understanding into structured JSON is a critical and non-trivial capability.
鉴于AI代码代理在孤立任务中表现优异但在需要理解模块间关系的复杂软件工程任务中表现不佳，本研究提出Theory of Code Space（ToCS）基准，用于评估代理在部分可观测环境下探索代码库时构建和维护架构信念的能力。该方法通过生成包含四种类型边（代表不同发现方式）和嵌入式架构约束的中等复杂度Python项目，并限制代理探索预算，同时通过结构化JSON定期探测其信念状态。实验结果显示，四种规则基线与五个大语言模型代理的性能跨度大（F1值0.129至0.646），表明LLM可发现基线无法识别的语义边类型，但较弱模型表现甚至低于简单启发式方法——说明将内部架构理解忠实外部化为结构化JSON本身是一项关键且非平凡的能力。
Speculative Speculative Decoding
Authors: Tanishq Kumar, Tri Dao, Avner May
First: 2026-03-03T18:41:32+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T18:41:32+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Autoregressive decoding is bottlenecked by its sequential nature. Speculative decoding has become a standard way to accelerate inference by using a fast draft model to predict upcoming tokens from a slower target model, and then verifying them in parallel with a single target model forward pass. However, speculative decoding itself relies on a sequential dependence between speculation and verification. We introduce speculative speculative decoding (SSD) to parallelize these operations. While a verification is ongoing, the draft model predicts likely verification outcomes and prepares speculations pre-emptively for them. If the actual verification outcome is then in the predicted set, a speculation can be returned immediately, eliminating drafting overhead entirely. We identify three key challenges presented by speculative speculative decoding, and suggest principled methods to solve each. The result is Saguaro, an optimized SSD algorithm. Our implementation is up to 2x faster than optimized speculative decoding baselines and up to 5x faster than autoregressive decoding with open source inference engines.
中文标题/摘要
标题：推测性推测解码
自回归解码受限于其串行特性。推测解码通过使用快速草稿模型预测慢速目标模型的下一个词元，再并行验证，已成为加速推理的标准方法。然而，推测解码本身依赖于推测与验证之间的串行依赖。我们引入推测性推测解码（SSD）以并行化这些操作：在验证进行时，草稿模型预测可能的验证结果，并提前准备相应的推测。若实际验证结果在预测集合中，可立即返回推测，完全消除草稿生成开销。我们识别了SSD带来的三个关键挑战，并提出解决方法。最终得到Saguaro，一种优化的SSD算法。我们的实现比优化的推测解码基线快2倍，比自回归解码快5倍（使用开源推理引擎）。
Summary / 总结
To overcome the sequential bottleneck of autoregressive decoding, the paper proposes speculative speculative decoding (SSD), which parallelizes the draft and verification phases by having the draft model predict likely verification outcomes and pre-generate speculations in advance. This allows immediate return of a token if the actual verification matches a prediction, eliminating drafting overhead. The method addresses three key challenges through principled solutions, resulting in Saguaro—an optimized SSD algorithm that achieves up to 2x speedup over standard speculative decoding and up to 5x speedup over autoregressive decoding using open-source inference engines.
为突破自回归解码的串行瓶颈，本文提出“推测式推测解码”（SSD），通过让草稿模型提前预测验证结果并预生成推测内容，实现解码阶段的并行化。当实际验证结果与预测匹配时，可立即返回推测结果，完全消除草稿生成开销。该方法针对三大挑战提出原理性解决方案，最终实现名为Saguaro的优化SSD算法，其在开源推理引擎下比标准推测解码快2倍，比自回归解码快5倍。
UniDrive-WM: Unified Understanding, Planning and Generation World Model For Autonomous Driving
Authors: Zhexiao Xiong, Xin Ye, Burhan Yaman, Sheng Cheng, Yiren Lu, Jingru Luo, Nathan Jacobs, Liu Ren
First: 2026-01-07T23:49:52+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T18:40:54+00:00
Comments: Project Page: https://unidrive-wm.github.io/UniDrive-WM
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Project1
Abstract
World models have become central to autonomous driving, where accurate scene understanding and future prediction are crucial for safe control. Recent work has explored using vision-language models (VLMs) for planning, yet existing approaches typically treat perception, prediction, and planning as separate modules. We propose UniDrive-WM, a unified VLM-based world model that jointly performs driving-scene understanding, trajectory planning, and trajectory-conditioned future image generation within a single architecture. UniDrive-WM's trajectory planner predicts a future trajectory, which conditions a VLM-based image generator to produce plausible future frames. These predictions provide additional supervisory signals that enhance scene understanding and iteratively refine trajectory generation. We further compare discrete and continuous output representations for future image prediction, analyzing their influence on downstream driving performance. Experiments on the challenging Bench2Drive benchmark show that UniDrive-WM produces high-fidelity future images and improves planning performance by 5.9% in L2 trajectory error and 9.2% in collision rate over the previous best method. These results demonstrate the advantages of tightly integrating VLM-driven reasoning, planning, and generative world modeling for autonomous driving. The project page is available at https://unidrive-wm.github.io/UniDrive-WM .
中文标题/摘要
标题：UniDrive-WM：面向自动驾驶的统一理解、规划与生成世界模型
世界模型已成为自动驾驶的核心，其中准确的场景理解与未来预测对安全控制至关重要。近期研究探索使用视觉-语言模型（VLM）进行规划，但现有方法通常将感知、预测和规划视为独立模块。我们提出UniDrive-WM，这是一种统一的基于VLM的世界模型，可在单一架构内联合执行驾驶场景理解、轨迹规划及轨迹条件下的未来图像生成。UniDrive-WM的轨迹规划器预测未来轨迹，该轨迹作为条件引导基于VLM的图像生成器生成合理的未来帧。这些预测提供额外的监督信号，增强场景理解并迭代优化轨迹生成。我们进一步比较了未来图像预测中离散与连续输出表示的效果，分析其对下游驾驶性能的影响。在具有挑战性的Bench2Drive基准测试中，UniDrive-WM生成高保真度的未来图像，并在L2轨迹误差上比现有最佳方法提升5.9%，碰撞率降低9.2%。结果表明，紧密集成VLM驱动的推理、规划与生成式世界建模对自动驾驶具有优势。项目页面见https://unidrive-wm.github.io/UniDrive-WM。

Experiments on Bench2Drive show that this tightly coupled approach improves trajectory accuracy by 5.9% in L2 error and reduces collision rate by 9.2% compared to prior methods, demonstrating the effectiveness of integrating reasoning, planning, and generative modeling within a single VLM framework.

Using Learning Progressions to Guide AI Feedback for Science Learning
Authors: Xin Xia, Nejla Yuruk, Yun Wang, Xiaoming Zhai
First: 2026-03-03T18:39:58+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T18:39:58+00:00
Comments: 15pages, 4 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Generative artificial intelligence (AI) offers scalable support for formative feedback, yet most AI-generated feedback relies on task-specific rubrics authored by domain experts. While effective, rubric authoring is time-consuming and limits scalability across instructional contexts. Learning progressions (LP) provide a theoretically grounded representation of students' developing understanding and may offer an alternative solution. This study examines whether an LP-driven rubric generation pipeline can produce AI-generated feedback comparable in quality to feedback guided by expert-authored task rubrics. We analyzed AI-generated feedback for written scientific explanations produced by 207 middle school students in a chemistry task. Two pipelines were compared: (a) feedback guided by a human expert-designed, task-specific rubric, and (b) feedback guided by a task-specific rubric automatically derived from a learning progression prior to grading and feedback generation. Two human coders evaluated feedback quality using a multi-dimensional rubric assessing Clarity, Accuracy, Relevance, Engagement and Motivation, and Reflectiveness (10 sub-dimensions). Inter-rater reliability was high, with percent agreement ranging from 89% to 100% and Cohen's kappa values for estimable dimensions (kappa = .66 to .88). Paired t-tests revealed no statistically significant differences between the two pipelines for Clarity (t1 = 0.00, p1 = 1.000; t2 = 0.84, p2 = .399), Relevance (t1 = 0.28, p1 = .782; t2 = -0.58, p2 = .565), Engagement and Motivation (t1 = 0.50, p1 = .618; t2 = -0.58, p2 = .565), or Reflectiveness (t = -0.45, p = .656). These findings suggest that the LP-driven rubric pipeline can serve as an alternative solution.
中文标题/摘要
标题：利用学习进阶指导人工智能反馈以支持科学学习
生成式人工智能（AI）可提供可扩展的形成性反馈支持，但多数AI生成的反馈依赖于由领域专家编写的任务特定评分标准。虽然有效，但评分标准的编写耗时且限制了其在不同教学情境中的可扩展性。学习进阶（LP）提供了学生理解逐步发展的理论基础表征，或可作为替代方案。本研究考察了由学习进阶驱动的评分标准生成流程能否产生与专家编写评分标准引导的反馈质量相当的AI生成反馈。我们分析了207名中学生在化学任务中撰写的科学解释所获得的AI生成反馈。比较了两种流程：(a) 由人类专家设计的任务特定评分标准引导的反馈；(b) 在评分和反馈生成前，由学习进阶自动推导出的任务特定评分标准引导的反馈。两名人类编码员使用评估清晰度、准确性、相关性、参与度与动机、反思性（10个子维度）的多维评分标准评价反馈质量。评分者间信度高，百分比一致率在89%至100%之间，可计算维度的Cohen's kappa值为0.66至0.88。配对t检验显示，两种流程在清晰度（t1=0.00, p1=1.000; t2=0.84, p2=0.399）、相关性（t1=0.28, p1=0.782; t2=-0.58, p2=0.565）、参与度与动机（t1=0.50, p1=0.618; t2=-0.58, p2=0.565）或反思性（t=-0.45, p=0.656）方面无统计学显著差异。这些发现表明，学习进阶驱动的评分标准流程可作为替代方案。
Summary / 总结
This study addresses the challenge of scalable AI feedback in science education by exploring whether learning progressions (LPs) can replace expert-authored rubrics in generating high-quality feedback. The researchers compared two pipelines: one using human-designed task-specific rubrics and another using rubrics automatically derived from LPs. Feedback was generated for 207 middle school students’ chemistry explanations and evaluated by two coders across five dimensions (Clarity, Accuracy, Relevance, Engagement and Motivation, Reflectiveness). High inter-rater reliability was observed, and paired t-tests showed no statistically significant differences between the LP-driven and expert-rubric pipelines across all evaluated dimensions, suggesting LPs can effectively support AI feedback generation without sacrificing quality.
本研究旨在解决科学教育中AI反馈规模化应用的难题，探索学习进阶（LP）能否替代专家编写的评分标准来生成高质量反馈。研究对比了两种流程：一种使用人工设计的特定任务评分标准，另一种使用从学习进阶自动推导的评分标准。对207名初中生的化学解释文本生成反馈，并由两名编码员从五个维度（清晰度、准确性、相关性、参与度与动机、反思性）进行评估。结果显示编码员间一致性高，且配对t检验表明两种流程在所有评估维度上无显著差异，说明基于学习进阶的评分标准可有效支持AI反馈生成而不降低质量。
HoMMI: Learning Whole-Body Mobile Manipulation from Human Demonstrations
Authors: Xiaomeng Xu, Jisang Park, Han Zhang, Eric Cousineau, Aditya Bhat, Jose Barreiros, Dian Wang, Shuran Song
First: 2026-03-03T18:36:49+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T18:36:49+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Project1
Abstract
We present Whole-Body Mobile Manipulation Interface (HoMMI), a data collection and policy learning framework that learns whole-body mobile manipulation directly from robot-free human demonstrations. We augment UMI interfaces with egocentric sensing to capture the global context required for mobile manipulation, enabling portable, robot-free, and scalable data collection. However, naively incorporating egocentric sensing introduces a larger human-to-robot embodiment gap in both observation and action spaces, making policy transfer difficult. We explicitly bridge this gap with a cross-embodiment hand-eye policy design, including an embodiment agnostic visual representation; a relaxed head action representation; and a whole-body controller that realizes hand-eye trajectories through coordinated whole-body motion under robot-specific physical constraints. Together, these enable long-horizon mobile manipulation tasks requiring bimanual and whole-body coordination, navigation, and active perception. Results are best viewed on: https://hommi-robot.github.io
中文标题/摘要
标题：HoMMI：从人类演示中学习全身移动操作
我们提出了全身移动操作接口（HoMMI），这是一种数据收集与策略学习框架，可直接从无机器人参与的人类演示中学习全身移动操作。我们通过加入第一人称感知，增强UMI接口以捕捉移动操作所需的全局上下文，从而实现便携、无机器人参与且可扩展的数据收集。然而，直接引入第一人称感知会扩大观察与动作空间中的人机具身差距，使策略迁移变得困难。我们通过跨具身手眼策略设计显式弥合这一差距，包括具身无关的视觉表征、放松的头部动作表征，以及在满足机器人特定物理约束下通过全身协调运动实现手眼轨迹的全身控制器。这些设计共同支持需要双手协调、全身运动、导航和主动感知的长时程移动操作任务。结果最佳查看：https://hommi-robot.github.io
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need for scalable and robot-free data collection for mobile manipulation, this work introduces HoMMI, a framework that learns whole-body mobile manipulation policies directly from human demonstrations using egocentric sensing augmented UMI interfaces. To address the increased embodiment gap between humans and robots introduced by egocentric sensing, the method employs a cross-embodiment hand-eye policy design featuring an embodiment-agnostic visual representation, a relaxed head action space, and a whole-body controller that generates hand-eye trajectories under robot-specific physical constraints. Experimental results demonstrate successful transfer to long-horizon tasks requiring bimanual coordination, navigation, and active perception, validating the framework’s effectiveness in enabling complex mobile manipulation without direct robot demonstrations.
为实现可扩展且无需机器人参与的数据采集，HoMMI 直接从人类演示中学习全身移动操作策略，通过增强的 UMI 接口结合第一人称视觉感知捕捉全局上下文。为弥合人机在观测与动作空间的本体差异，该框架采用跨本体手眼策略：包括无本体依赖的视觉表征、放松的头部动作空间，以及在机器人物理约束下协调全身运动的控制器。实验表明，该方法可有效完成需双手协作、导航与主动感知的长时程移动操作任务，验证了其无需机器人演示即可实现复杂操作的能力。
Density-Guided Response Optimization: Community-Grounded Alignment via Implicit Acceptance Signals
Authors: Patrick Gerard, Svitlana Volkova
First: 2026-03-03T18:36:25+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T18:36:25+00:00
Comments: 27 Pages
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Language models deployed in online communities must adapt to norms that vary across social, cultural, and domain-specific contexts. Prior alignment approaches rely on explicit preference supervision or predefined principles, which are effective for well-resourced settings but exclude most online communities -- particularly those without institutional backing, annotation infrastructure, or organized around sensitive topics -- where preference elicitation is costly, ethically fraught, or culturally misaligned. We observe that communities already express preferences implicitly through what content they accept, engage with, and allow to persist. We show that this acceptance behavior induces measurable geometric structure in representation space: accepted responses occupy coherent, high-density regions that reflect community-specific norms, while rejected content falls in sparser or misaligned areas. We operationalize this structure as an implicit preference signal for alignment and introduce density-guided response optimization (DGRO), a method that aligns language models to community norms without requiring explicit preference labels. Using labeled preference data, we demonstrate that local density recovers pairwise community judgments, indicating that geometric structure encodes meaningful preference signal. We then apply DGRO in annotation-scarce settings across diverse communities spanning platform, topic, and language. DGRO-aligned models consistently produce responses preferred by human annotators, domain experts, and model-based judges over supervised and prompt-based baselines. We position DGRO as a practical alignment alternative for communities where explicit preference supervision is unavailable or misaligned with situated practices, and discuss the implications and risks of learning from emergent acceptance behavior.
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the challenge of aligning language models with norms in under-resourced online communities lacking explicit preference data, the paper proposes density-guided response optimization (DGRO), which leverages implicit acceptance signals from community behavior. It observes that accepted responses cluster in high-density regions in representation space, while rejected content lies in sparser areas, forming a geometric structure that encodes community norms. DGRO uses this density structure to guide model alignment without explicit preference labels. Experiments show that local density correlates with human pairwise judgments and that DGRO outperforms supervised and prompt-based baselines across diverse, annotation-scarce communities, producing responses preferred by human annotators, domain experts, and model-based judges.
为解决缺乏显式偏好标注的在线社区中语言模型对齐难题，该研究提出密度引导响应优化（DGRO）方法，利用社区隐式接受行为作为对齐信号。研究发现，被接受的响应在表示空间中形成高密度区域，而被拒绝的内容则分布稀疏，这种几何结构反映了社区规范。DGRO通过密度结构引导模型对齐，无需显式偏好标签。实验表明，局部密度可预测人类配对判断，且在多种低标注社区中，DGRO优于监督和提示基线方法，其生成的响应更受人类标注者、领域专家及模型裁判的青睐。
UniG2U-Bench: Do Unified Models Advance Multimodal Understanding?
Authors: Zimo Wen, Boxiu Li, Wanbo Zhang, Junxiang Lei, Xiaoyu Chen, Yijia Fan, Qi Zhang, Yujiang Wang, Lili Qiu, Bo Li, Ziwei Liu, Caihua Shan, Yifan Yang, Yifei Shen
First: 2026-03-03T18:36:16+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T18:36:16+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Unified multimodal models have recently demonstrated strong generative capabilities, yet whether and when generation improves understanding remains unclear. Existing benchmarks lack a systematic exploration of the specific tasks where generation facilitates understanding. To this end, we introduce UniG2U-Bench, a comprehensive benchmark categorizing generation-to-understanding (G2U) evaluation into 7 regimes and 30 subtasks, requiring varying degrees of implicit or explicit visual transformations. Extensive evaluation of over 30 models reveals three core findings: 1) Unified models generally underperform their base Vision-Language Models (VLMs), and Generate-then-Answer (GtA) inference typically degrades performance relative to direct inference. 2) Consistent enhancements emerge in spatial intelligence, visual illusions, or multi-round reasoning subtasks, where enhanced spatial and shape perception, as well as multi-step intermediate image states, prove beneficial. 3) Tasks with similar reasoning structures and models sharing architectures exhibit correlated behaviors, suggesting that generation-understanding coupling induces class-consistent inductive biases over tasks, pretraining data, and model architectures. These findings highlight the necessity for more diverse training data and novel paradigms to fully unlock the potential of unified multimodal modeling.
中文标题/摘要
标题：UniG2U-Bench：统一模型是否促进多模态理解？
统一多模态模型近期展现了强大的生成能力，但生成是否以及何时能提升理解仍不明确。现有基准缺乏对生成促进理解的具体任务的系统性探索。为此，我们提出了UniG2U-Bench，一个全面的基准，将生成到理解（G2U）评估划分为7类和30个子任务，要求不同程度的隐式或显式视觉转换。对30多个模型的广泛评估揭示了三个核心发现：1）统一模型通常表现不如其基础视觉-语言模型（VLMs），且生成后回答（GtA）推理通常比直接推理表现更差。2）在空间智能、视觉错觉或多轮推理子任务中，一致的性能提升出现，增强的空间和形状感知能力以及多步中间图像状态证明有益。3）具有相似推理结构的任务和共享架构的模型表现出相关行为，表明生成-理解耦合在任务、预训练数据和模型架构上诱导了类别一致的归纳偏置。这些发现强调了需要更多样化的训练数据和新颖范式，以充分释放统一多模态建模的潜力。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the unclear relationship between generation and understanding in unified multimodal models, this study introduces UniG2U-Bench, a benchmark categorizing G2U tasks into seven regimes and thirty subtasks requiring varying visual transformations. Evaluating over thirty models, it finds that unified models typically underperform their base VLMs and that GtA inference often degrades performance. However, generation consistently improves performance in tasks demanding spatial intelligence, visual illusions, or multi-round reasoning, where intermediate visual states and enhanced perception help. The study also observes that models with similar architectures and reasoning structures show correlated behaviors, indicating generation-understanding coupling creates consistent inductive biases across tasks and architectures.
为探究统一多模态模型的生成能力是否提升理解能力，该研究构建了UniG2U-Bench基准，包含7类任务和30个子任务，考察生成如何通过不同视觉变换促进理解。对30多个模型的评估发现，统一模型通常不如其基础视觉语言模型表现，且生成后再回答的推理方式常导致性能下降。但在需要空间智能、视觉错觉或多轮推理的任务中，生成能带来稳定提升，因中间图像状态和增强感知能力有益。此外，结构相似的模型在任务中表现相关，表明生成与理解的耦合会形成跨任务、数据和架构一致的归纳偏置。
Monitoring AI-Modified Content at Scale: A Case Study on the Impact of ChatGPT on AI Conference Peer Reviews
Authors: Weixin Liang, Zachary Izzo, Yaohui Zhang, Haley Lepp, Hancheng Cao, Xuandong Zhao, Lingjiao Chen, Haotian Ye, Sheng Liu, Zhi Huang, Daniel A. McFarland, James Y. Zou
Venue: ICML
First: 2024-03-11T21:51:39+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T18:36:00+00:00
Comments: 46 pages, 31 figures, ICML '24
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We present an approach for estimating the fraction of text in a large corpus which is likely to be substantially modified or produced by a large language model (LLM). Our maximum likelihood model leverages expert-written and AI-generated reference texts to accurately and efficiently examine real-world LLM-use at the corpus level. We apply this approach to a case study of scientific peer review in AI conferences that took place after the release of ChatGPT: ICLR 2024, NeurIPS 2023, CoRL 2023 and EMNLP 2023. Our results suggest that between 6.5% and 16.9% of text submitted as peer reviews to these conferences could have been substantially modified by LLMs, i.e. beyond spell-checking or minor writing updates. The circumstances in which generated text occurs offer insight into user behavior: the estimated fraction of LLM-generated text is higher in reviews which report lower confidence, were submitted close to the deadline, and from reviewers who are less likely to respond to author rebuttals. We also observe corpus-level trends in generated text which may be too subtle to detect at the individual level, and discuss the implications of such trends on peer review. We call for future interdisciplinary work to examine how LLM use is changing our information and knowledge practices.
Summary / 总结
We present an approach for estimating the fraction of text in a large corpus which is likely to be substantially modified or produced by a large language model (LLM).
为量化真实学术场景中AI生成内容的规模，该研究构建了一种最大似然模型，通过对比专家撰写与AI生成文本，估算大规模语料库中经大型语言模型大幅修改的内容比例。应用于ChatGPT发布后四大AI会议（ICLR 2024、NeurIPS 2023、CoRL 2023、EMNLP 2023）的同行评审文本，结果显示6.5%至16.9%的提交评审可能经LLM大幅修改（超出拼写检查或微调）。关键发现包括：低置信度评审、临近截止日期提交、以及较少回应作者反驳的评审者更倾向使用AI。研究还揭示了语料层面的隐蔽趋势，暗示其对同行评审体系的潜在影响，并呼吁跨学科研究探索AI工具如何重塑学术信息与知识实践。
COP-GEN: Latent Diffusion Transformer for Copernicus Earth Observation Data -- Generation Stochastic by Design
Authors: Miguel Espinosa, Eva Gmelich Meijling, Valerio Marsocci, Elliot J. Crowley, Mikolaj Czerkawski
First: 2026-03-03T18:31:46+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T18:31:46+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Earth observation applications increasingly rely on data from multiple sensors, including optical, radar, elevation, and land-cover products. Relationships between these modalities are fundamental for data integration but are inherently non-injective: identical conditioning information can correspond to multiple physically plausible observations. Thus, such conditional mappings should be parametrised as data distributions. As a result, deterministic models tend to collapse toward conditional means and fail to represent the uncertainty and variability required for tasks such as data completion and cross-sensor translation. We introduce COP-GEN, a multimodal latent diffusion transformer that models the joint distribution of heterogeneous Earth Observation modalities at their native spatial resolutions. By parameterising cross-modal mappings as conditional distributions, COP-GEN enables flexible any-to-any conditional generation, including zero-shot modality translation, spectral band infilling, and generation under partial or missing inputs, without task-specific retraining. Experiments on a large-scale global multimodal dataset show that COP-GEN generates diverse yet physically consistent realisations while maintaining strong peak fidelity across optical, radar, and elevation modalities. Qualitative and quantitative analyses demonstrate that the model captures meaningful cross-modal structure and systematically adapts its output uncertainty as conditioning information increases. These results highlight the practical importance of stochastic generative modeling for Earth observation and motivate evaluation protocols that move beyond single-reference, pointwise metrics. Website: https:// miquel-espinosa.github.io/cop-gen
中文标题/摘要
标题：COP-GEN：用于哥白尼地球观测数据的潜在扩散变换器——设计上具有生成随机性
地球观测应用日益依赖多种传感器数据，包括光学、雷达、高程和地表覆盖产品。这些模态间的关联关系是数据集成的基础，但本质上是非单射的：相同的条件信息可能对应多个物理上合理的观测结果。因此，此类条件映射应参数化为数据分布。由此，确定性模型往往趋向于条件均值，无法有效表示数据补全和跨传感器转换等任务所需的不确定性和变异性。我们提出了COP-GEN，一种多模态潜在扩散变换器，能够在各自原生空间分辨率下建模异构地球观测模态的联合分布。通过将跨模态映射参数化为条件分布，COP-GEN支持灵活的任意模态到任意模态条件生成，包括零样本模态转换、光谱波段填充以及在部分或缺失输入下的生成，无需针对特定任务重新训练。在大规模全球多模态数据集上的实验表明，COP-GEN生成多样化且物理一致的结果，同时在光学、雷达和高程模态中保持高保真度。定性和定量分析表明，该模型捕捉了有意义的跨模态结构，并能系统性地根据条件信息增加而调整输出不确定性。这些结果突显了随机生成建模在地球观测中的实际重要性，并推动评估协议超越单一参考点度量。网站：https://miquel-espinosa.github.io/cop-gen

On Geometry Regularization in Autoencoder Reduced-Order Models with Latent Neural ODE Dynamics
Authors: Mikhail Osipov
First: 2026-03-03T18:31:13+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T18:31:13+00:00
Comments: 25 pages, 2 figures, 3 tables
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We investigate geometric regularization strategies for learned latent representations in encoder--decoder reduced-order models. In a fixed experimental setting for the advection--diffusion--reaction (ADR) equation, we model latent dynamics using a neural ODE and evaluate four regularization approaches applied during autoencoder pre-training: (a) near-isometry regularization of the decoder Jacobian, (b) a stochastic decoder gain penalty based on random directional gains, (c) a second-order directional curvature penalty, and (d) Stiefel projection of the first decoder layer. Across multiple seeds, we find that (a)--(c) often produce latent representations that make subsequent latent-dynamics training with a frozen autoencoder more difficult, especially for long-horizon rollouts, even when they improve local decoder smoothness or related sensitivity proxies. In contrast, (d) consistently improves conditioning-related diagnostics of the learned latent dynamics and tends to yield better rollout performance. We discuss the hypothesis that, in this setting, the downstream impact of latent-geometry mismatch outweighs the benefits of improved decoder smoothness.
中文标题/摘要
标题：关于自编码器降阶模型中潜空间神经ODE动力学的几何正则化研究
我们研究了编码器-解码器降阶模型中学习到的潜空间表示的几何正则化策略。在固定实验设置下，针对对流-扩散-反应（ADR）方程，我们使用神经ODE建模潜空间动力学，并评估四种在自编码器预训练阶段应用的正则化方法：(a) 解码器雅可比矩阵的近等距正则化，(b) 基于随机方向增益的随机解码器增益惩罚，(c) 二阶方向曲率惩罚，以及(d) 解码器第一层的Stiefel投影。在多个随机种子下，我们发现(a)-(c)通常会导致潜空间表示在后续使用冻结自编码器训练潜空间动力学时更难优化，尤其在长时域滚动预测中，即使它们能改善局部解码器平滑性或相关敏感性代理指标。相比之下，(d)始终能改善所学潜空间动力学的条件相关诊断指标，并倾向于获得更好的滚动预测性能。我们讨论了如下假设：在此设置下，潜空间几何不匹配对下游任务的负面影响超过了解码器平滑性提升带来的益处。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need to improve latent representation geometry in autoencoder-based reduced-order models for the advection-diffusion-reaction equation, the study evaluates four regularization methods applied during autoencoder pre-training: near-isometry Jacobian regularization, stochastic decoder gain penalty, directional curvature penalty, and Stiefel projection of the first decoder layer. Experimental results across multiple seeds show that the first three methods often degrade downstream latent-dynamics training, especially for long-horizon rollouts, despite improving local decoder smoothness. In contrast, Stiefel projection consistently enhances conditioning diagnostics and yields superior rollout performance, suggesting that latent-geometry mismatch may negatively impact downstream dynamics learning more than decoder smoothness benefits.
为提升自编码器驱动的降阶模型在对流-扩散-反应方程中的潜在表示几何结构，本文评估了四种预训练阶段的正则化方法：解码器雅可比近等距正则化、随机方向增益惩罚、二阶曲率惩罚及第一层解码器的Stiefel投影。实验表明，前三类方法虽能提升局部解码器平滑性，却常导致后续潜在动力学训练困难，尤其在长时预测中表现更差；而Stiefel投影则持续改善潜在动力学的条件诊断指标，并提升预测性能，暗示潜在几何不匹配对下游动力学学习的负面影响可能超过解码器平滑性的提升。
Characterizing the Multiclass Learnability of Forgiving 0-1 Loss Functions
Authors: Jacob Trauger, Tyson Trauger, Ambuj Tewari
First: 2025-10-09T16:07:55+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T18:31:08+00:00
Comments: 15 pages
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
In this paper we will give a characterization of the learnability of forgiving 0-1 loss functions in the multiclass setting with effectively finite cardinality of the output and label space. To do this, we create a new combinatorial dimension that is based off of the Natarajan Dimension and we show that a hypothesis class is learnable in our setting if and only if this Generalized Natarajan Dimension is finite. We also show how this dimension characterizes other known learning settings such as a vast amount of instantiations of learning with set-valued feedback and a modified version of list learning.
中文标题/摘要
标题：多类可学习性下宽容0-1损失函数的刻画
本文刻画了在输出和标签空间具有有效有限基数的多类设置下，宽容0-1损失函数的可学习性。为此，我们提出了一种基于Natarajan维数的新组合维数，并证明：一个假设类在该设置下可学习，当且仅当该广义Natarajan维数有限。此外，我们还展示了该维数如何刻画其他已知学习场景，如大量集合反馈学习的实例及列表学习的一种修改版本。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need to understand learnability in multiclass settings with forgiving 0-1 loss functions and finite output/label spaces, the paper introduces a new combinatorial dimension called the Generalized Natarajan Dimension, extending the classical Natarajan Dimension. It demonstrates that a hypothesis class is learnable under this framework if and only if this generalized dimension is finite. The study further shows that this dimension unifies and characterizes various learning scenarios, including set-valued feedback and modified list learning, providing a unified theoretical framework for multiclass learnability.

CASR-Net: An Image Processing-focused Deep Learning-based Coronary Artery Segmentation and Refinement Network for X-ray Coronary Angiogram
Authors: Alvee Hassan, Rusab Sarmun, Muhammad E. H. Chowdhury, M Murugappan, Abdulrahman Alqahtani, Balamurugan Balusamy, Sohaib Bassam Zoghoul
First: 2025-10-31T09:40:29+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T18:28:59+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Early detection of coronary artery disease (CAD) is critical for reducing mortality and improving patient treatment planning. While angiographic image analysis from X-rays is a common and cost-effective method for identifying cardiac abnormalities, including stenotic coronary arteries, poor image quality can significantly impede clinical diagnosis. We present the Coronary Artery Segmentation and Refinement Network (CASR-Net), a three-stage pipeline comprising image preprocessing, segmentation, and refinement. A novel multichannel preprocessing strategy combining CLAHE and an improved Ben Graham method provides incremental gains, increasing Dice Score Coefficient (DSC) by 0.31-0.89% and Intersection over Union (IoU) by 0.40-1.16% compared with using the techniques individually. The core innovation is a segmentation network built on a UNet with a DenseNet121 encoder and a Self-organized Operational Neural Network (Self-ONN) based decoder, which preserves the continuity of narrow and stenotic vessel branches. A final contour refinement module further suppresses false positives. Evaluated with 5-fold cross-validation on a combination of two public datasets that contain both healthy and stenotic arteries, CASR-Net outperformed several state-of-the-art models, achieving an IoU of 61.43%, a DSC of 76.10%, and clDice of 79.36%. These results highlight a robust approach to automated coronary artery segmentation, offering a valuable tool to support clinicians in diagnosis and treatment planning.
中文标题/摘要
标题：CASR-Net：一种面向X射线冠状动脉造影图像处理的深度学习冠状动脉分割与优化网络
早期发现冠状动脉疾病（CAD）对降低死亡率和改善患者治疗规划至关重要。虽然X射线血管造影图像分析是识别心脏异常（包括狭窄冠状动脉）的常用且经济的方法，但图像质量不佳会显著阻碍临床诊断。本文提出冠状动脉分割与优化网络（CASR-Net），包含图像预处理、分割和优化三个阶段。一种新颖的多通道预处理策略结合CLAHE与改进的Ben Graham方法，相比单独使用各技术，可使Dice系数（DSC）提升0.31-0.89%，交并比（IoU）提升0.40-1.16%。核心创新是基于UNet架构的分割网络，采用DenseNet121编码器和基于自组织运算神经网络（Self-ONN）的解码器，有效保持狭窄和狭窄血管分支的连续性。最终轮廓优化模块进一步抑制假阳性。在包含健康与狭窄动脉的两个公开数据集组合上进行5折交叉验证，CASR-Net优于多个现有先进模型，实现IoU 61.43%、DSC 76.10%、clDice 79.36%。这些结果展示了自动化冠状动脉分割的稳健方法，为临床诊断与治疗规划提供有力支持。
