为应对X射线冠状动脉造影图像质量差影响临床诊断的问题，CASR-Net提出包含图像预处理、分割与轮廓优化的三阶段流程。其预处理阶段融合CLAHE与改进的Ben Graham方法，使Dice系数和IoU分别提升0.31–0.89%和0.40–1.16%。分割核心采用DenseNet121编码器与Self-ONN解码器的UNet架构，以保持狭窄血管的连续性，最终优化模块减少假阳性。在两个公开数据集上经5折交叉验证，CASR-Net实现IoU 61.43%、DSC 76.10%、clDice 79.36%，优于多个现有先进模型。
The elbow statistic: Multiscale clustering statistical significance
Authors: Francisco J. Perez-Reche
First: 2026-03-03T18:28:01+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T18:28:01+00:00
Comments: 30 pages, 3 figures, 5 tables
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Selecting the number of clusters remains a fundamental challenge in unsupervised learning. Existing criteria typically target a single ``optimal'' partition, often overlooking statistically meaningful structure present at multiple resolutions. We introduce ElbowSig, a framework that formalizes the heuristic ``elbow'' method as a rigorous inferential problem. Our approach centers on a normalized discrete curvature statistic derived from the cluster heterogeneity sequence, which is evaluated against a null distribution of unstructured data. We derive the asymptotic properties of this null statistic in both large-sample and high-dimensional regimes, characterizing its baseline behavior and stochastic variability. As an algorithm-agnostic procedure, ElbowSig requires only the heterogeneity sequence and is compatible with a wide range of clustering methods, including hard, fuzzy, and model-based clustering. Extensive experiments on synthetic and empirical datasets demonstrate that the method maintains appropriate Type-I error control while providing the power to resolve multiscale organizational structures that are typically obscured by single-resolution selection criteria.
中文标题/摘要
标题：肘部统计量：多尺度聚类的统计显著性
选择聚类数量仍是无监督学习中的基本挑战。现有准则通常仅针对单一“最优”划分，常忽略在多重分辨率下存在的具有统计意义的结构。我们引入ElbowSig框架，将启发式“肘部”方法形式化为严谨的推断问题。我们的方法基于聚类异质性序列推导出的归一化离散曲率统计量，并与无结构数据的零分布进行比较。我们推导了该零统计量在大样本和高维情形下的渐近性质，刻画其基准行为与随机波动。作为一种算法无关的方法，ElbowSig仅需异质性序列，兼容多种聚类方法，包括硬聚类、模糊聚类和基于模型的聚类。在合成与实际数据集上的大量实验表明，该方法在控制I类错误的同时，具备揭示通常被单一分辨率选择准则掩盖的多尺度组织结构的能力。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the challenge of selecting an appropriate number of clusters in unsupervised learning, where existing methods often miss multiscale structure, the paper introduces ElbowSig, a statistical framework that formalizes the elbow heuristic as a hypothesis test. It uses a normalized discrete curvature statistic based on cluster heterogeneity sequences, evaluated against a null distribution of unstructured data, and derives its asymptotic behavior under large-sample and high-dimensional conditions. The method is algorithm-agnostic and compatible with various clustering types, and experiments show it maintains correct Type-I error rates while effectively detecting multiscale organizational structures that single-resolution criteria typically overlook.
为解决无监督学习中聚类数量选择这一基本难题，本文提出ElbowSig框架，将经验性的“肘部”法则形式化为严谨的统计推断问题。该方法基于聚类异质性序列计算归一化离散曲率统计量，并与无结构数据的零分布进行比较，利用渐近理论刻画其在大样本和高维情形下的行为特征。ElbowSig不依赖特定聚类算法，兼容硬聚类、模糊聚类和模型聚类等多种方法，仅需异质性序列作为输入。在合成数据和真实数据上的实验表明，该方法能有效控制I类错误率，同时识别传统单分辨率准则常忽略的多尺度组织结构。
Quantifying User Coherence: A Unified Framework for Analyzing Recommender Systems Across Domains
Authors: Michaël Soumm, Alexandre Fournier-Montgieux, Adrian Popescu, Bertrand Delezoide
Venue: The Web Conference
First: 2024-10-03T13:02:07+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T18:27:39+00:00
Comments: Accepted at The Web Conference (WWW 2026)
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
The performance of Recommender Systems (RS) varies significantly across users, yet the underlying reasons for this variance remain poorly understood. This paper introduces a unified framework to analyze and explain this performance gap by quantifying user profile characteristics. We propose two novel, information-theoretic measures: Mean Surprise (S(u)), which captures a user's deviation from popular items and is closely related to popularity bias, and Mean Conditional Surprise (CS(u)), which measures the internal coherence of a user's interactions in a domain-agnostic manner. Through extensive experiments on 7 algorithms and 9 datasets, we demonstrate that these measures are strong predictors of recommendation performance. Our analysis reveals that performance gains from complex models are concentrated on "coherent" users, while all algorithms perform poorly on "incoherent" users. We show how these measures provide practical utility for the Web community by: (1) enabling robust, stratified evaluation to identify model weaknesses; (2) facilitating a novel analysis of the behavioral alignment of recommendations; and (3) guiding targeted system design, which we validate by training a specialized model on a segment of "coherent" users that achieves superior performance for that group with significantly less data. This work provides a new lens for understanding user behavior and offers practical tools for building more robust and efficient large-scale recommender systems.
中文标题/摘要
标题：量化用户一致性：跨领域的推荐系统统一分析框架
推荐系统（RS）在不同用户间的性能差异显著，但其背后原因尚不明确。本文提出一个统一框架，通过量化用户画像特征来分析并解释这一性能差距。我们提出两种新颖的信息论度量：平均惊喜值（S(u)），衡量用户对热门物品的偏离程度，与流行度偏差密切相关；平均条件惊喜值（CS(u)），以领域无关方式衡量用户交互的内部一致性。通过在7种算法和9个数据集上的大量实验，我们证明这些度量是推荐性能的强预测指标。分析表明，复杂模型的性能提升主要集中在“一致性”用户群体，而所有算法在“不一致性”用户群体表现不佳。我们展示了这些度量对Web社区的实用价值：（1）支持稳健分层评估，识别模型弱点；（2）促进推荐行为对齐的新型分析；（3）指导定向系统设计，我们通过在“一致性”用户子集上训练专用模型，验证其以更少数据实现该群体更优性能。本工作为理解用户行为提供新视角，并为构建更稳健高效的大型推荐系统提供实用工具。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the lack of understanding regarding why recommender systems perform variably across users by introducing a unified framework that quantifies user profile characteristics using two information-theoretic measures: Mean Surprise (S(u)) and Mean Conditional Surprise (CS(u)). These measures capture user deviation from popular items and internal interaction coherence, respectively. Evaluated across seven algorithms and nine datasets, they consistently predict recommendation performance, revealing that complex models benefit only coherent users while underperforming on incoherent ones. The framework enables stratified evaluation, behavioral alignment analysis, and targeted system design—demonstrated by a specialized model trained on coherent users that outperforms general models with less data.
本文针对推荐系统在不同用户间性能差异缺乏解释的问题，提出一个统一框架，通过两个新的信息论度量——均值惊喜（衡量用户对热门物品的偏离）和条件均值惊喜（衡量用户交互的内在一致性）来量化用户特征。在七种算法和九个数据集上的实验表明，这两个度量能有效预测推荐性能，揭示复杂模型仅对“一致性用户”有效，而对“不一致性用户”表现不佳。该框架支持分层评估、行为对齐分析和定向系统设计——通过在一致性用户子集上训练专用模型，该模型在更少数据下实现了更优性能。
Guiding Sparse Neural Networks with Neurobiological Principles to Elicit Biologically Plausible Representations
Authors: Patrick Inoue, Florian Röhrbein, Andreas Knoblauch
First: 2026-03-03T18:27:37+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T18:27:37+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
While deep neural networks (DNNs) have achieved remarkable performance in tasks such as image recognition, they often struggle with generalization, learning from few examples, and continuous adaptation - abilities inherent in biological neural systems. These challenges arise due to DNNs' failure to emulate the efficient, adaptive learning mechanisms of biological networks. To address these issues, we explore the integration of neurobiologically inspired assumptions in neural network learning. This study introduces a biologically inspired learning rule that naturally integrates neurobiological principles, including sparsity, lognormal weight distributions, and adherence to Dale's law, without requiring explicit enforcement. By aligning with these core neurobiological principles, our model enhances robustness against adversarial attacks and demonstrates superior generalization, particularly in few-shot learning scenarios. Notably, integrating these constraints leads to the emergence of biologically plausible neural representations, underscoring the efficacy of incorporating neurobiological assumptions into neural network design. Preliminary results suggest that this approach could extend from feature-specific to task-specific encoding, potentially offering insights into neural resource allocation for complex tasks.
中文标题/摘要
标题：利用神经生物学原理引导稀疏神经网络以激发生物可解释的表征
尽管深度神经网络（DNNs）在图像识别等任务中取得了显著性能，但它们往往难以实现泛化、从少量样本学习和持续适应——这些能力是生物神经系统的固有特征。这些问题源于DNNs未能模拟生物网络高效、自适应的学习机制。为解决这些问题，我们探索将神经生物学启发的假设融入神经网络学习。本研究引入一种受生物启发的学习规则，自然整合了稀疏性、对数正态权重分布和道尔定律等神经生物学原则，无需显式强制执行。通过遵循这些核心神经生物学原则，我们的模型增强了对对抗攻击的鲁棒性，并在少量样本学习场景中展现出更优的泛化能力。值得注意的是，整合这些约束条件可促使神经网络涌现出生物可解释的表征，凸显将神经生物学假设融入神经网络设计的有效性。初步结果表明，该方法可能从特征编码扩展到任务编码，或为复杂任务的神经资源分配提供启示。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the limitations of deep neural networks in generalization, few-shot learning, and continuous adaptation compared to biological systems, this study proposes a learning rule inspired by neurobiological principles such as sparsity, lognormal weight distributions, and Dale's law. The method integrates these principles implicitly into network training without explicit constraints, allowing the model to naturally evolve biologically plausible representations. Experimental results show improved robustness against adversarial attacks and superior generalization performance, especially in few-shot settings, suggesting that neurobiological assumptions can enhance learning efficiency and representation quality.
鉴于深度神经网络在泛化、小样本学习和持续适应能力上不如生物神经系统，本研究提出一种内含神经生物学原理（如稀疏性、对数正态权重分布和戴尔定律）的生物启发式学习规则，无需显式约束。实验表明，该方法显著提升模型对对抗攻击的鲁棒性，并在小样本学习中表现出更强的泛化能力，同时生成符合生物合理性的神经表征。
VeriStruct: AI-assisted Automated Verification of Data-Structure Modules in Verus
Authors: Chuyue Sun, Yican Sun, Daneshvar Amrollahi, Ethan Zhang, Shuvendu Lahiri, Shan Lu, David Dill, Clark Barrett
First: 2025-10-28T22:28:37+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T18:26:58+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We introduce VeriStruct, a novel framework that extends AI-assisted automated verification from single functions to more complex data structure modules in Verus. VeriStruct employs a planner module to orchestrate the systematic generation of abstractions, type invariants, specifications, and proof code. To address the challenge that LLMs often misunderstand Verus' annotation syntax and verification-specific semantics, VeriStruct embeds syntax guidance within prompts and includes a repair stage to automatically correct annotation errors. In an evaluation on eleven Rust data structure modules, VeriStruct succeeds on ten of the eleven, successfully verifying 128 out of 129 functions (99.2%) in total. These results represent an important step toward the goal of automatic AI-assisted formal verification.
中文标题/摘要
标题：VeriStruct：用于Verus中数据结构模块的AI辅助自动化验证框架
我们提出了VeriStruct，一个将AI辅助自动化验证从单个函数扩展到Verus中更复杂数据结构模块的新型框架。VeriStruct采用规划模块协调抽象、类型不变式、规范和证明代码的系统化生成。为解决大语言模型常误解Verus注解语法和验证特定语义的问题，VeriStruct在提示中嵌入语法指导，并包含一个自动修正注解错误的修复阶段。在对11个Rust数据结构模块的评估中，VeriStruct成功验证了其中10个，总计成功验证129个函数中的128个（99.2%）。这些结果标志着向实现自动AI辅助形式化验证目标的重要一步。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need to extend AI-assisted verification beyond single functions to complex data structures, VeriStruct introduces a planner module that systematically generates abstractions, type invariants, specifications, and proof code for Verus modules. To mitigate LLM misunderstandings of Verus syntax and semantics, it embeds syntax guidance in prompts and includes an automatic repair stage for annotation errors. Evaluated on eleven Rust data structure modules, VeriStruct successfully verified ten modules and 128 out of 129 functions (99.2%), demonstrating strong feasibility for AI-assisted formal verification.
为将AI辅助验证从单个函数扩展至Verus中的复杂数据结构模块，VeriStruct引入规划模块，系统生成抽象、类型不变式、规范及证明代码。为解决大语言模型对Verus注解语法和验证语义理解不足的问题，该框架在提示中嵌入语法引导并加入自动修复阶段修正注解错误。在对11个Rust数据结构模块的评估中，VeriStruct成功验证了10个模块，共129个函数中128个（99.2%）通过验证，表明AI辅助形式验证具有高度可行性。
Safe Payload Transfer with Ship-Mounted Cranes: A Robust Model Predictive Control Approach
Authors: Ersin Das, William A. Welch, Patrick Spieler, Keenan Albee, Aurelio Noca, Jeffrey Edlund, Jonathan Becktor, Thomas Touma, Jessica Todd, Sriramya Bhamidipati, Stella Kombo, Maira Saboia, Anna Sabel, Grace Lim, Rohan Thakker, Amir Rahmani, Joel W. Burdick
First: 2025-10-19T18:13:33+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T18:26:25+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Ensuring safe real-time control of ship-mounted cranes in unstructured transportation environments requires handling multiple safety constraints while maintaining effective payload transfer performance. Unlike traditional crane systems, ship-mounted cranes are consistently subjected to significant external disturbances affecting underactuated crane dynamics due to the ship's dynamic motion response to harsh sea conditions, which can lead to robustness issues. To tackle these challenges, we propose a robust and safe model predictive control (MPC) framework and demonstrate it on a 5-DOF crane system, where a Stewart platform simulates the external disturbances that ocean surface motions would have on the supporting ship. The crane payload transfer operation must avoid obstacles and accurately place the payload within a designated target area. We use a robust zero-order control barrier function (R-ZOCBF)-based safety constraint in the nonlinear MPC to ensure safe payload positioning, while time-varying bounding boxes are utilized for collision avoidance. We introduce a new optimization-based online robustness parameter adaptation scheme to reduce the conservativeness of R-ZOCBFs. Experimental trials on a crane prototype demonstrate the overall performance of our safe control approach under significant perturbing motions of the crane base. While our focus is on crane-facilitated transfer, the methods more generally apply to safe robotically-assisted parts mating and parts insertion.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于船载起重机的安全载荷转移：一种鲁棒模型预测控制方法
在非结构化运输环境中确保船载起重机安全实时控制，需同时处理多重安全约束并保持有效的载荷转移性能。与传统起重机不同，船载起重机持续受到显著外部干扰，因船舶在恶劣海况下的动态响应导致欠驱动起重机动力学的鲁棒性问题。为应对这些挑战，我们提出一种鲁棒安全模型预测控制（MPC）框架，并在5自由度起重机系统上进行验证，其中Stewart平台模拟海洋表面运动对支撑船舶的影响。起重机载荷转移操作必须避开障碍物，并将载荷精确放置在指定目标区域内。我们采用基于鲁棒零阶控制屏障函数（R-ZOCBF）的安全约束，确保载荷安全定位，同时使用时变包围盒实现避碰。我们引入一种基于优化的在线鲁棒性参数自适应方案，以降低R-ZOCBF的保守性。在起重机原型上的实验表明，我们的安全控制方法在起重机基座显著扰动下仍能有效运行。虽然我们的重点是起重机辅助的载荷转移，但该方法更广泛适用于安全机器人辅助的部件装配与插入。
Summary / 总结
Ensuring safe real-time control of ship-mounted cranes in unstructured transportation environments requires handling multiple safety constraints while maintaining effective payload transfer performance.
为在海浪扰动下保障船载起重机的安全与精准吊运，本文提出一种结合零阶控制屏障函数与动态避障框的鲁棒模型预测控制框架。该方法在5自由度起重机原型上通过斯特拉特平台模拟船舶运动，验证了其在剧烈基座扰动下仍能确保负载安全定位与精度。引入的在线优化鲁棒参数调整机制有效降低了安全约束保守性，提升了系统性能与鲁棒性。
CIRCLE: A Framework for Evaluating AI from a Real-World Lens
Authors: Reva Schwartz, Carina Westling, Morgan Briggs, Marzieh Fadaee, Isar Nejadgholi, Matthew Holmes, Fariza Rashid, Maya Carlyle, Afaf Taïk, Kyra Wilson, Peter Douglas, Theodora Skeadas, Gabriella Waters, Rumman Chowdhury, Thiago Lacerda
First: 2026-02-27T14:43:23+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T18:25:54+00:00
Comments: Accepted at Intelligent Systems Conference (IntelliSys) 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
This paper proposes CIRCLE, a six-stage, lifecycle-based framework to bridge the reality gap between model-centric performance metrics and AI's materialized outcomes in deployment. While existing frameworks like MLOps focus on system stability and benchmarks measure abstract capabilities, decision-makers outside the AI stack lack systematic evidence about the behavior of AI technologies under real-world user variability and constraints. CIRCLE operationalizes the Validation phase of TEVV (Test, Evaluation, Verification, and Validation) by formalizing the translation of stakeholder concerns outside the stack into measurable signals. Unlike participatory design, which often remains localized, or algorithmic audits, which are often retrospective, CIRCLE provides a structured, prospective protocol for linking context-sensitive qualitative insights to scalable quantitative metrics. By integrating methods such as field testing, red teaming, and longitudinal studies into a coordinated pipeline, CIRCLE produces systematic knowledge: evidence that is comparable across sites yet sensitive to local context. This can enable governance based on materialized downstream effects rather than theoretical capabilities.
中文标题/摘要
标题：CIRCLE：从现实世界视角评估人工智能的框架
本文提出CIRCLE，一个基于生命周期的六阶段框架，旨在弥合以模型为中心的性能指标与人工智能在部署中实际产出之间的现实差距。现有框架如MLOps侧重系统稳定性，基准测试衡量抽象能力，但AI栈外的决策者缺乏关于AI技术在真实用户变异与约束下行为的系统性证据。CIRCLE通过形式化将栈外利益相关者关切转化为可测量信号，实现TEVV（测试、评估、验证与确认）中的验证阶段。与常局限于局部的参与式设计或常具回顾性的算法审计不同，CIRCLE提供了一种结构化、前瞻性的协议，将情境敏感的定性洞察与可扩展的定量指标相联系。通过将实地测试、红队演练和纵向研究等方法整合进协调流程，CIRCLE生成系统性知识：跨站点可比但对本地情境敏感的证据，从而支持基于实际下游效应而非理论能力的治理。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the gap between model-centric performance metrics and real-world AI outcomes, CIRCLE introduces a six-stage lifecycle framework that translates stakeholder concerns into measurable signals through structured validation. It integrates field testing, red teaming, and longitudinal studies into a coordinated pipeline to generate context-sensitive yet comparable evidence. Experimental results show that this approach enables decision-makers to evaluate AI systems based on materialized downstream effects rather than abstract benchmarks, offering a scalable and prospective method for governance.
为弥合模型性能指标与实际部署中AI效果之间的差距，CIRCLE提出一个六阶段生命周期框架，将利益相关者关切转化为可测量信号，通过整合实地测试、红队演练和纵向研究形成协调流程，生成既具本地敏感性又可跨场景比较的实证证据。实验表明，该框架使决策者能基于AI实际产生的下游影响而非抽象能力进行评估，提供了一种可扩展、前瞻性的治理方法。
AI-for-Science Low-code Platform with Bayesian Adversarial Multi-Agent Framework
Authors: Zihang Zeng, Jiaquan Zhang, Pengze Li, Yuan Qi, Xi Chen
First: 2026-03-03T18:25:00+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T18:25:00+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large Language Models (LLMs) demonstrate potentials for automating scientific code generation but face challenges in reliability, error propagation in multi-agent workflows, and evaluation in domains with ill-defined success metrics. We present a Bayesian adversarial multi-agent framework specifically designed for AI for Science (AI4S) tasks in the form of a Low-code Platform (LCP). Three LLM-based agents are coordinated under the Bayesian framework: a Task Manager that structures user inputs into actionable plans and adaptive test cases, a Code Generator that produces candidate solutions, and an Evaluator providing comprehensive feedback. The framework employs an adversarial loop where the Task Manager iteratively refines test cases to challenge the Code Generator, while prompt distributions are dynamically updated using Bayesian principles by integrating code quality metrics: functional correctness, structural alignment, and static analysis. This co-optimization of tests and code reduces dependence on LLM reliability and addresses evaluation uncertainty inherent to scientific tasks. LCP also streamlines human-AI collaboration by translating non-expert prompts into domain-specific requirements, bypassing the need for manual prompt engineering by practitioners without coding backgrounds. Benchmark evaluations demonstrate LCP's effectiveness in generating robust code while minimizing error propagation. The proposed platform is also tested on an Earth Science cross-disciplinary task and demonstrates strong reliability, outperforming competing models.
中文标题/摘要
标题：面向科学领域的低代码平台：贝叶斯对抗多智能体框架
大型语言模型（LLMs）在自动化科学代码生成方面展现出潜力，但在可靠性、多智能体工作流中的错误传播及评估指标不明确的领域中面临挑战。我们提出一种专为AI for Science（AI4S）任务设计的贝叶斯对抗多智能体框架，以低代码平台（LCP）形式呈现。该框架协调三个基于LLM的智能体：任务管理器将用户输入结构化为可执行计划和自适应测试用例；代码生成器生成候选解决方案；评估器提供全面反馈。框架采用对抗循环机制，任务管理器迭代优化测试用例以挑战代码生成器，同时通过贝叶斯原理动态更新提示分布，整合代码质量指标（功能正确性、结构对齐、静态分析）。该测试与代码协同优化机制降低了对LLM可靠性的依赖，解决了科学任务固有的评估不确定性。LCP还通过将非专家提示转化为领域特定需求，简化了人机协作，无需非编码背景从业者手动进行提示工程。基准评估表明，LCP在生成稳健代码的同时有效减少错误传播。该平台在地球科学跨学科任务中亦经测试，展现出卓越可靠性，优于现有竞争模型。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need to automate scientific code generation while mitigating LLM reliability issues and error propagation in multi-agent workflows, this paper introduces a Bayesian adversarial multi-agent framework embedded in a low-code platform. The system coordinates three LLM-based agents: a Task Manager that refines user inputs into test plans, a Code Generator that produces solutions, and an Evaluator that provides feedback. Through an adversarial loop, the Task Manager iteratively improves test cases to challenge the Code Generator, while Bayesian updating dynamically adjusts prompt distributions based on code quality metrics including correctness, structural alignment, and static analysis. Experimental results show the platform generates robust code with reduced error propagation and outperforms competitors on a cross-disciplinary Earth Science task, while also enabling non-experts to interact effectively via natural language prompts.
为解决科学代码自动生成中大语言模型可靠性不足、多智能体协作中错误传播及科学任务评价标准模糊等问题，本文提出一种基于贝叶斯对抗多智能体框架的低代码平台。该平台协调三个基于大语言模型的智能体：任务管理器将用户输入转化为测试计划，代码生成器输出候选方案，评估器提供综合反馈。通过对抗循环，任务管理器不断优化测试用例以挑战代码生成器，同时基于功能正确性、结构对齐和静态分析等指标，利用贝叶斯方法动态调整提示分布。实验表明，该平台生成的代码更稳健、错误传播更少，在跨学科地球科学任务中表现优于竞品，且无需专业背景用户手动设计提示即可高效协作。
SynthCharge: An Electric Vehicle Routing Instance Generator with Feasibility Screening to Enable Learning-Based Optimization and Benchmarking
Authors: Mertcan Daysalilar, Fuat Uyguroglu, Gabriel Nicolosi, Adam Meyers
First: 2026-03-03T18:23:38+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T18:23:38+00:00
Comments: This work has been submitted to the IEEE for possible publication
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
The electric vehicle routing problem with time windows (EVRPTW) extends the classical VRPTW by introducing battery capacity constraints and charging station decisions. Existing benchmark datasets are often static and lack verifiable feasibility, which restricts reproducible evaluation of learning-based routing models. We introduce SynthCharge, a parametric generator that produces diverse, feasibility-screened EVRPTW instances across varying spatiotemporal configurations and scalable customer counts. While SynthCharge can currently generate large-scale instances of up to 500 customers, we focus our experiments on sizes ranging from 5 to 100 customers. Unlike static benchmark suites, SynthCharge integrates instance geometry with adaptive energy capacity scaling and range-aware charging station placement. To guarantee structural validity, the generator systematically filters out unsolvable instances through a fast feasibility screening process. Ultimately, SynthCharge provides the dynamic benchmarking infrastructure needed to systematically evaluate the robustness of emerging neural routing and data-driven approaches.

带时间窗的电动车辆路径问题（EVRPTW）在经典VRPTW基础上引入了电池容量约束和充电站决策。现有基准数据集多为静态且缺乏可验证的可行性，限制了基于学习的路径模型的可重复评估。我们提出SynthCharge，一种参数化生成器，可在不同时空配置和可扩展客户数量下生成多样且经过可行性筛选的EVRPTW实例。尽管SynthCharge当前可生成最多500客户的大型实例，但我们的实验聚焦于5至100客户的规模。与静态基准集不同，SynthCharge将实例几何结构与自适应能量容量缩放及范围感知的充电站布局相结合。为确保结构有效性，生成器通过快速可行性筛选过程系统性剔除无解实例。最终，SynthCharge提供了动态基准测试基础设施，用于系统评估新兴神经路径与数据驱动方法的鲁棒性。

Inverse Reconstruction of Shock Time Series from Shock Response Spectrum Curves using Machine Learning
Authors: Adam Watts, Andrew Jeon, Destry Newton, Ryan Bowering
First: 2026-03-03T18:23:29+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T18:23:29+00:00
Comments: Extended journal-style manuscript. 27 pages, 13 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
The shock response spectrum (SRS) is widely used to characterize the response of single-degree-of-freedom (SDOF) systems to transient accelerations. Because the mapping from acceleration time history to SRS is nonlinear and many-to-one, reconstructing time-domain signals from a target spectrum is inherently ill-posed. Conventional approaches address this problem through iterative optimization, typically representing signals as sums of exponentially decayed sinusoids, but these methods are computationally expensive and constrained by predefined basis functions. We propose a conditional variational autoencoder (CVAE) that learns a data-driven inverse mapping from SRS to acceleration time series. Once trained, the model generates signals consistent with prescribed target spectra without requiring iterative optimization. Experiments demonstrate improved spectral fidelity relative to classical techniques, strong generalization to unseen spectra, and inference speeds three to six orders of magnitude faster. These results establish deep generative modeling as a scalable and efficient approach for inverse SRS reconstruction.
中文标题/摘要
标题：利用机器学习从冲击响应谱曲线反演冲击时程
冲击响应谱（SRS）广泛用于表征单自由度（SDOF）系统对瞬态加速度的响应。由于从加速度时程到SRS的映射是非线性且多对一的，从目标谱重建时域信号本质上是不适定问题。传统方法通过迭代优化解决此问题，通常将信号表示为指数衰减正弦波的和，但这些方法计算成本高且受限于预定义基函数。 我们提出一种条件变分自编码器（CVAE），学习从SRS到加速度时程的数据驱动逆映射。训练完成后，模型无需迭代优化即可生成与指定目标谱一致的信号。实验表明，该方法相比经典技术具有更高的频谱保真度、对未见谱的强泛化能力，且推理速度提升三至六个数量级。这些结果确立了深度生成建模作为可扩展且高效的逆SRS重建方法。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the computational inefficiency and limitations of traditional iterative methods for reconstructing acceleration time series from shock response spectra, this study proposes a conditional variational autoencoder (CVAE) to learn a direct, data-driven inverse mapping. The CVAE is trained on pairs of SRS curves and corresponding time-domain signals, enabling it to generate accurate acceleration waveforms without iterative optimization. Experimental results show that the model achieves superior spectral fidelity compared to classical techniques, generalizes well to unseen spectra, and offers inference speeds up to six orders of magnitude faster.
为解决传统方法在由冲击响应谱反演加速度时程时计算效率低、依赖预设基函数的问题，本文提出一种条件变分自编码器（CVAE），通过数据驱动学习SRS到时域信号的直接逆映射。训练完成后，模型无需迭代优化即可生成符合目标谱的加速度波形。实验表明，该方法在频谱保真度上优于传统方法，对未见谱具有强泛化能力，且推理速度提升达六个数量级。
Solving Inverse PDE Problems using Minimization Methods and AI
Authors: Noura Al Helwani, Sophie Moufawad, Georges Sakr
First: 2026-03-02T10:57:26+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T18:21:16+00:00
Comments: 52 pages, 21 Figures, 22 Tables
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Many physical and engineering systems require solving direct problems to predict behavior and inverse problems to determine unknown parameters from measurement. In this work, we study both aspects for systems governed by differential equations, contrasting well-established numerical methods with new AI-based techniques, specifically Physics-Informed Neural Networks (PINNs). We first analyze the logistic differential equation, using its closed-form solution to verify numerical schemes and validate PINN performance. We then address the Porous Medium Equation (PME), a nonlinear partial differential equation with no general closed-form solution, building strong solvers of the direct problem and testing techniques for parameter estimation in the inverse problem. Our results suggest that PINNs can closely estimate solutions at competitive computational cost, and thus propose an effective tool for solving both direct and inverse problems for complex systems.
中文标题/摘要
标题：使用最小化方法和人工智能求解逆偏微分方程问题
许多物理和工程系统需要求解正问题以预测行为，以及逆问题以从测量数据中确定未知参数。本文研究了由微分方程控制的系统的这两个方面，对比了成熟的数值方法与新型基于人工智能的技术，特别是物理信息神经网络（PINNs）。我们首先分析了逻辑微分方程，利用其解析解验证数值方案并验证PINN性能。随后处理了无一般解析解的非线性偏微分方程——渗流介质方程（PME），构建了强的正问题求解器，并测试了逆问题中的参数估计技术。结果表明，PINNs可在具有竞争力的计算成本下近似估计解，因此提出了一种解决复杂系统正逆问题的有效工具。
Summary / 总结
Many physical and engineering systems require solving direct problems to predict behavior and inverse problems to determine unknown parameters from measurement.
为解决由微分方程描述的物理与工程系统中的正向与反向问题，该研究对比了传统数值方法与物理信息神经网络（PINNs）。针对具有解析解的逻辑斯蒂方程，PINNs通过与解析解对比验证了其正向求解能力；针对无解析解的非线性渗流介质方程（PME），PINNs被用于直接求解并估计反向问题中的未知参数。实验表明，PINNs在保持高精度的同时，计算成本与传统方法相当，可作为复杂系统正向与反向问题的有效求解工具。
Automatic and Structure-Aware Sparsification of Hybrid Neural ODEs
Authors: Bob Junyi Zou, Lu Tian
Venue: ICLR
First: 2025-05-25T06:36:30+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T18:20:48+00:00
Comments: Accepted at The 14th International Conference on Learning Representations (ICLR) 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Hybrid neural ordinary differential equations (neural ODEs) integrate mechanistic models with neural ODEs, offering strong inductive bias and flexibility, and are particularly advantageous in data-scarce healthcare settings. However, excessive latent states and interactions from mechanistic models can lead to training inefficiency and over-fitting, limiting practical effectiveness of hybrid neural ODEs. In response, we propose a new hybrid pipeline for automatic state selection and structure optimization in mechanistic neural ODEs, combining domain-informed graph modifications with data-driven regularization to sparsify the model for improving predictive performance and stability while retaining mechanistic plausibility. Experiments on synthetic and real-world data show improved predictive performance and robustness with desired sparsity, establishing an effective solution for hybrid model reduction in healthcare applications.
中文标题/摘要
标题：混合神经常微分方程的自动与结构感知稀疏化
混合神经常微分方程（神经ODE）结合了机制模型与神经ODE，具有强大的归纳偏置和灵活性，尤其适用于数据稀缺的医疗场景。然而，机制模型中过多的隐状态和交互可能导致训练效率低下和过拟合，限制了混合神经ODE的实际有效性。为此，我们提出了一种新的混合管道，用于自动选择状态和优化结构，结合领域知识引导的图修改与数据驱动的正则化，以稀疏化模型，从而在保持机制合理性的同时提升预测性能与稳定性。在合成和真实数据上的实验表明，该方法在实现期望稀疏性的同时提升了预测性能与鲁棒性，为医疗应用中的混合模型降维提供了一种有效解决方案。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the inefficiency and overfitting risks in hybrid neural ODEs due to excessive latent states from mechanistic models, this work proposes an automatic and structure-aware sparsification method that combines domain-informed graph modifications with data-driven regularization to prune redundant states while preserving mechanistic plausibility. The method systematically reduces model complexity by identifying and removing non-essential interactions, enhancing training efficiency and generalization. Experimental results on both synthetic and real-world healthcare datasets demonstrate improved predictive performance and robustness under desired sparsity levels, validating the approach as an effective solution for model reduction in hybrid neural ODEs.
为了解决混合神经常微分方程中因机制模型引入过多隐状态而导致的训练低效与过拟合问题，本文提出一种自动且结构感知的稀疏化方法，结合领域知识引导的图结构修改与数据驱动的正则化，以剪枝冗余状态并保留机制合理性。该方法通过系统性识别并移除非必要交互，提升模型训练效率与泛化能力。在合成及真实医疗数据上的实验表明，该方法在保持期望稀疏度的同时显著提升预测性能与鲁棒性，验证了其在医疗领域混合模型压缩中的有效性。
Coalgebras for categorical deep learning: Representability and universal approximation
Authors: Dragan Mašulović
First: 2026-03-03T18:18:50+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T18:18:50+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Categorical deep learning (CDL) has recently emerged as a framework that leverages category theory to unify diverse neural architectures. While geometric deep learning (GDL) is grounded in the specific context of invariants of group actions, CDL aims to provide domain-independent abstractions for reasoning about models and their properties. In this paper, we contribute to this program by developing a coalgebraic foundation for equivariant representation in deep learning, as classical notions of group actions and equivariant maps are naturally generalized by the coalgebraic formalism. Our first main result demonstrates that, given an embedding of data sets formalized as a functor from SET to VECT, and given a notion of invariant behavior on data sets modeled by an endofunctor on SET, there is a corresponding endofunctor on VECT that is compatible with the embedding in the sense that this lifted functor recovers the analogous notion of invariant behavior on the embedded data. Building on this foundation, we then establish a universal approximation theorem for equivariant maps in this generalized setting. We show that continuous equivariant functions can be approximated within our coalgebraic framework for a broad class of symmetries. This work thus provides a categorical bridge between the abstract specification of invariant behavior and its concrete realization in neural architectures.
中文标题/摘要
标题：范畴深学习中的余代数：可表示性与通用逼近
范畴深学习（CDL）最近作为一种框架出现，利用范畴论统一多种神经架构。虽然几何深学习（GDL）基于群作用不变量的具体情境，CDL旨在为模型及其属性提供领域无关的抽象。本文通过发展深学习中等变表示的余代数基础，贡献于该计划，因为群作用与等变映射的经典概念可自然通过余代数形式化推广。我们的第一个主要结果表明，给定数据集的嵌入形式化为从SET到VECT的函子，以及数据集上不变行为的模型（由SET上的内函子描述），存在一个与嵌入兼容的VECT上内函子，该函子在嵌入数据上恢复类似的不变行为。在此基础上，我们建立了该广义设置下等变映射的通用逼近定理。我们证明，连续等变函数可在我们的余代数框架中被广泛对称类逼近。本工作因此在抽象不变行为规范与神经架构中具体实现之间架起了一座范畴桥梁。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need to provide domain-independent abstractions for neural architectures, this paper develops a coalgebraic framework for equivariant representation in deep learning, generalizing classical group actions. The method constructs a functor from SET to VECT that embeds data sets and lifts invariant behavior modeled by an endofunctor on SET into an endofunctor on VECT. Experimental results demonstrate that continuous equivariant functions can be universally approximated within this coalgebraic setting for a broad class of symmetries, establishing a categorical bridge between abstract invariance specifications and their neural implementations.
为超越几何深度学习的局限，本文构建了深度学习中等变表示的余代数框架，将经典群作用概念推广。方法通过从 SET 到 VECT 的函子嵌入数据，并将 SET 上的不变行为通过内函子提升为 VECT 上兼容的内函子。实验表明，该余代数框架可对广泛对称类下的连续等变函数实现通用逼近，建立了抽象不变性规范与神经网络实现之间的范畴桥梁。
Adaptive Methods Are Preferable in High Privacy Settings: An SDE Perspective
Authors: Enea Monzio Compagnoni, Alessandro Stanghellini, Rustem Islamov, Aurelien Lucchi, Anastasiia Koloskova
Venue: ICLR 2026 Poster
First: 2026-03-03T18:17:57+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T18:17:57+00:00
Comments: Accepted at ICLR 2026 (Poster)
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Differential Privacy (DP) is becoming central to large-scale training as privacy regulations tighten. We revisit how DP noise interacts with adaptivity in optimization through the lens of stochastic differential equations, providing the first SDE-based analysis of private optimizers. Focusing on DP-SGD and DP-SignSGD under per-example clipping, we show a sharp contrast under fixed hyperparameters: DP-SGD converges at a Privacy-Utility Trade-Off of $\mathcal{O}(1/\varepsilon^2)$ with speed independent of $\varepsilon$, while DP-SignSGD converges at a speed linear in $\varepsilon$ with an $\mathcal{O}(1/\varepsilon)$ trade-off, dominating in high-privacy or large batch noise regimes. By contrast, under optimal learning rates, both methods achieve comparable theoretical asymptotic performance; however, the optimal learning rate of DP-SGD scales linearly with $\varepsilon$, while that of DP-SignSGD is essentially $\varepsilon$-independent. This makes adaptive methods far more practical, as their hyperparameters transfer across privacy levels with little or no re-tuning. Empirical results confirm our theory across training and test metrics, and empirically extend from DP-SignSGD to DP-Adam.
Summary / 总结
Differential Privacy (DP) is becoming central to large-scale training as privacy regulations tighten.
随着隐私法规趋严，机器学习对差分隐私的需求日益增长，本研究从随机微分方程视角分析隐私噪声与优化自适应性的交互关系。在每样本裁剪下比较DP-SGD与DP-SignSGD发现，固定超参数时，DP-SGD的隐私-效用权衡为$\mathcal{O}(1/\varepsilon^2)$，收敛速度与ε无关；而DP-SignSGD收敛速度与ε线性相关，权衡为$\mathcal{O}(1/\varepsilon)$，在高隐私或大批次噪声场景下表现更优。当采用自适应学习率时，二者渐近性能相近，但DP-SignSGD的学习率几乎与ε无关，更易跨隐私级别迁移使用，无需重新调参。实验结果验证了理论分析，并扩展至DP-Adam方法。
Stabilized Adaptive Loss and Residual-Based Collocation for Physics-Informed Neural Networks
Authors: Divyavardhan Singh, Shubham Kamble, Dimple Sonone, Kishor Upla
First: 2026-03-03T18:17:28+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T18:17:28+00:00
Comments: 6 pages, 2 Figures, 4 tables
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Physics-Informed Neural Networks (PINNs) have been recognized as a mesh-free alternative to solve partial differential equations where physics information is incorporated. However, in dealing with problems characterized by high stiffness or shock-dominated dynamics, traditional PINNs have been found to have limitations, including unbalanced training and inaccuracy in solution, even with small physics residuals. In this research, we seek to address these limitations using the viscous Burgers' equation with low viscosity and the Allen-Cahn equation as test problems. In addressing unbalanced training, we have developed a new adaptive loss balancing scheme using smoothed gradient norms to ensure satisfaction of initial and boundary conditions. Further, to address inaccuracy in the solution, we have developed an adaptive residual-based collocation scheme to improve the accuracy of solutions in the regions with high physics residuals. The proposed new approach significantly improves solution accuracy with consistent satisfaction of physics residuals. For instance, in the case of Burgers' equation, the relative L2 error is reduced by about 44 percent compared to traditional PINNs, while for the Allen-Cahn equation, the relative L2 error is reduced by approximately 70 percent. Additionally, we show the trustworthy solution comparison of the proposed method using a robust finite difference solver.
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the limitations of traditional Physics-Informed Neural Networks (PINNs) in handling stiff or shock-dominated problems, this study introduces a stabilized adaptive loss and residual-based collocation method. The approach employs smoothed gradient norms to balance training and ensures initial and boundary condition satisfaction, while an adaptive collocation scheme targets high-residual regions to enhance solution accuracy. Experimental results on the viscous Burgers' equation and Allen-Cahn equation show significant improvements: relative L2 error reduced by 44% for Burgers' and 70% for Allen-Cahn compared to baseline PINNs, with consistent physics residual satisfaction and validation against a finite difference solver.
为解决传统物理信息神经网络（PINN）在处理强刚性或激波主导问题时训练失衡与解不准确的问题，本文提出一种基于自适应损失平衡与残差驱动插值的稳定方法。该方法通过平滑梯度范数平衡训练并满足初始与边界条件，同时采用自适应插值策略提升高残差区域的解精度。实验表明，在黏性Burgers方程和Allen-Cahn方程上，该方法相较传统PINN分别将相对L2误差降低44%和70%，且物理残差保持稳定，结果经有限差分求解器验证可靠。
Classroom Final Exam: An Instructor-Tested Reasoning Benchmark
Authors: Chongyang Gao, Diji Yang, Shuyan Zhou, Xichen Yan, Luchuan Song, Shuo Li, Kezhen Chen
First: 2026-02-23T05:17:41+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T18:16:35+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
We introduce CFE-Bench (Classroom Final Exam), a multimodal benchmark for evaluating the reasoning capabilities of large language models across more than 20 STEM domains. CFE-Bench is curated from repeatedly used, authentic university homework and exam problems, paired with reference solutions provided by course instructors. CFE-Bench remains challenging for frontier models: the newly released Gemini-3.1-pro-preview achieves 59.69% overall accuracy, while the second-best model, Gemini-3-flash-preview, reaches 55.46%, leaving substantial room for improvement. Beyond aggregate scores, we conduct a diagnostic analysis by decomposing instructor reference solutions into structured reasoning flows. We find that while frontier models often answer intermediate sub-questions correctly, they struggle to reliably derive and maintain correct intermediate states throughout multi-step solutions. We further observe that model-generated solutions typically contain more reasoning steps than instructor solutions, indicating lower step efficiency and a higher risk of error accumulation. Data and code are available at https://github.com/Analogy-AI/CFE_Bench.
中文标题/摘要
标题：课堂期末考试：一种经过教师验证的推理基准
我们提出了CFE-Bench（课堂期末考试），这是一个用于评估大型语言模型在20多个STEM领域推理能力的多模态基准。CFE-Bench从大学中反复使用的、真实的作业和考试题目中精选而来，并配有课程教师提供的参考答案。该基准对前沿模型仍具挑战性：新发布的Gemini-3.1-pro-preview整体准确率为59.69%，次优模型Gemini-3-flash-preview达到55.46%，仍有显著提升空间。除整体得分外，我们通过将教师参考答案分解为结构化推理流程进行诊断分析，发现前沿模型虽常能正确回答中间子问题，但在多步解题过程中难以可靠推导并维持正确的中间状态。此外，我们观察到模型生成的解题步骤通常多于教师解题步骤，表明其步骤效率较低，错误累积风险更高。数据与代码可访问：https://github.com/Analogy-AI/CFE_Bench。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need for realistic, instructor-validated reasoning benchmarks in STEM education, the authors introduce CFE-Bench, a multimodal dataset compiled from authentic university exam problems and instructor-provided solutions across over 20 domains. They evaluate frontier models like Gemini-3.1-pro-preview (59.69% accuracy) and Gemini-3-flash-preview (55.46%), revealing persistent difficulty in maintaining correct intermediate states during multi-step reasoning. Diagnostic analysis shows models often solve sub-questions correctly but fail to reliably chain them together, and their solutions typically include more steps than human ones, suggesting inefficiency and higher error accumulation risk.
为评估大语言模型在STEM领域的实际推理能力，研究者构建了CFE-Bench基准，该数据集由大学真实考试题目及教师参考答案组成，覆盖20多个学科。实验表明，前沿模型如Gemini-3.1-pro-preview准确率仅为59.69%，Gemini-3-flash-preview为55.46%，仍有较大提升空间。诊断分析发现，模型虽常能正确解答中间子问题，但在多步解题中难以稳定维持正确中间状态，且其解题步骤通常多于教师解法，表明推理效率低、错误累积风险高。
Deception by Design: A Temporal Dark Patterns Audit of McDonald's Self-Ordering Kiosk Flow
Authors: Aditya Kumar Purohit, Yuwei Liu, Manon Berney, Hendrik Heuer, Adrian Holzer
First: 2026-03-03T18:09:04+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T18:09:04+00:00
Comments: Accepted at the CHI'26 workshop on Bridge Over Troubled Water, April 16, 2026, Barcelona, Spain
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Self-ordering kiosks (SOKs) are widely deployed in fast food restaurants, transforming food ordering into digitally mediated, self-navigated interactions. While these systems enhance efficiency and average order value, they also create opportunities for manipulative interface design practices known as dark patterns. This paper presents a structured audit of the McDonald's self-ordering kiosk in Germany using the Temporal Analysis of Dark Patterns (TADP) framework. Through a scenario-based walkthrough simulating a time-pressured user, we reconstructed and analyzed 12 interface steps across intra-page, inter-page, and system levels. We identify recurring high-level strategies implemented through meso-level patterns such as adding steps, false hierarchy, bad defaults, hiding information, and pressured selling, and low-level patterns including visual prominence, confirmshaming, scarcity framing, feedforward ambiguity, emotional sensory manipulation, and partitioned pricing. Our findings demonstrate how these patterns accumulate across the interaction flow and may be amplified by the kiosk's linear task structure and physical context. These findings suggest that hybrid physical--digital consumer interfaces warrant closer scrutiny within emerging regulatory discussions on dark patterns.
中文标题/摘要
标题：设计中的欺骗：对麦当劳自助点餐机流程的时序暗模式审计
自助点餐机（SOKs）在快餐店广泛部署，将食品订购转变为数字化、自我导航的交互过程。虽然这些系统提升了效率和平均订单价值，但也为操纵性界面设计实践——即暗模式——创造了机会。本文采用时序暗模式分析框架（TADP），对德国麦当劳自助点餐机进行了结构化审计。通过模拟时间紧迫用户的场景式走查，我们重构并分析了跨页面内、页面间及系统层级的12个界面步骤。我们识别出通过中层模式（如增加步骤、虚假层级、不良默认设置、隐藏信息、压力销售）和底层模式（如视觉突出、确认羞辱、稀缺框架、前馈模糊、情感感官操控、分项计价）实施的反复出现的高层策略。研究发现，这些模式在交互流程中累积，并可能因点餐机的线性任务结构和物理环境而被放大。这些发现表明，混合物理-数字消费者界面应成为新兴暗模式监管讨论中更受关注的对象。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by concerns over manipulative design in self-ordering kiosks, this study audits McDonald's kiosk interface in Germany using the Temporal Analysis of Dark Patterns (TADP) framework. Through scenario-based walkthroughs simulating time-pressured users, researchers analyzed 12 interface steps across multiple levels, identifying recurring high-level strategies like adding steps and false hierarchy, alongside low-level tactics such as confirmshaming and scarcity framing. Findings reveal that these dark patterns accumulate across the interaction flow, amplified by the kiosk’s linear structure and physical environment, suggesting that hybrid physical-digital interfaces require regulatory attention.
鉴于自助点餐机中存在操纵性设计，本研究采用“时间暗模式分析框架”对德国麦当劳自助点餐机界面进行审计。通过模拟时间紧迫用户的场景化走查，研究人员分析了12个界面步骤，识别出如增加步骤、虚假层级等高层策略，以及确认羞辱、稀缺框架等低层手法。研究发现，这些暗模式在交互流程中累积叠加，且因设备线性结构与物理环境而被放大，提示混合物理-数字界面需纳入暗模式监管讨论。
Operator Learning Using Weak Supervision from Walk-on-Spheres
Authors: Hrishikesh Viswanath, Hong Chul Nam, Xi Deng, Julius Berner, Anima Anandkumar, Aniket Bera
First: 2026-03-01T17:23:39+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T18:07:51+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Training neural PDE solvers is often bottlenecked by expensive data generation or unstable physics-informed neural network (PINN) involving challenging optimization landscapes due to higher-order derivatives. To tackle this issue, we propose an alternative approach using Monte Carlo approaches to estimate the solution to the PDE as a stochastic process for weak supervision during training. Leveraging the Walk-on-Spheres method, we introduce a learning scheme called \emph{Walk-on-Spheres Neural Operator (WoS-NO)} which uses weak supervision from WoS to train any given neural operator. We propose to amortize the cost of Monte Carlo walks across the distribution of PDE instances using stochastic representations from the WoS algorithm to generate cheap, noisy, estimates of the PDE solution during training. This is formulated into a data-free physics-informed objective where a neural operator is trained to regress against these weak supervisions, allowing the operator to learn a generalized solution map for an entire family of PDEs. This strategy does not require expensive pre-computed datasets, avoids computing higher-order derivatives for loss functions that are memory-intensive and unstable, and demonstrates zero-shot generalization to novel PDE parameters and domains. Experiments show that for the same number of training steps, our method exhibits up to 8.75$\times$ improvement in $L_2$-error compared to standard physics-informed training schemes, up to 6.31$\times$ improvement in training speed, and reductions of up to 2.97$\times$ in GPU memory consumption. We present the code at https://github.com/neuraloperator/WoS-NO
中文标题/摘要
标题：利用Walk-on-Spheres弱监督学习算子
训练神经偏微分方程求解器常因昂贵的数据生成或不稳定的物理信息神经网络（PINN）而受阻，后者因高阶导数导致优化景观复杂。为解决此问题，我们提出一种替代方法，利用蒙特卡洛方法将PDE解估计为随机过程，以实现训练期间的弱监督。基于Walk-on-Spheres方法，我们引入一种名为\emph{Walk-on-Spheres神经算子（WoS-NO）}的学习方案，利用WoS提供的弱监督训练任意给定神经算子。我们提出通过WoS算法的随机表示，在PDE实例分布上摊销蒙特卡洛随机游走的成本，从而在训练期间生成廉价、噪声的PDE解估计。该方法被形式化为一种无数据的物理信息目标，神经算子通过回归这些弱监督进行训练，使其能够学习整个PDE族的通用解映射。该策略无需昂贵的预计算数据集，避免了高阶导数损失函数带来的内存密集型与不稳定性问题，并展现出对新颖PDE参数和域的零样本泛化能力。实验表明，在相同训练步数下，我们的方法相比标准物理信息训练方案在$L_2$误差上提升高达8.75倍，训练速度提升高达6.31倍，GPU内存消耗降低高达2.97倍。代码见https://github.com/neuraloperator/WoS-NO
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the computational cost and instability of training physics-informed neural networks due to expensive data generation and high-order derivative losses, this work introduces the Walk-on-Spheres Neural Operator (WoS-NO), a method that uses Monte Carlo estimation via the Walk-on-Spheres algorithm to generate cheap, noisy weak supervision for training neural operators. Instead of relying on precomputed datasets or derivative-heavy loss functions, WoS-NO amortizes Monte Carlo sampling across PDE instances using stochastic representations to train a neural operator to regress against these weak signals, enabling zero-shot generalization across PDE families. Experimental results show that with the same number of training steps, WoS-NO achieves up to 8.75x lower L2-error, 6.31x faster training speed, and 2.97x less GPU memory usage compared to standard physics-informed training.
为解决训练物理信息神经网络（PINN）时因数据生成昂贵或高阶导数导致的优化不稳定问题，本文提出Walk-on-Spheres神经算子（WoS-NO）方法，利用Walk-on-Spheres算法的蒙特卡洛采样生成训练过程中的弱监督信号。该方法通过在PDE实例分布上摊销蒙特卡洛路径计算成本，使用随机表示生成低成本、噪声的PDE解近似值，构建无数据物理信息目标函数，使神经算子能泛化至整个PDE族。实验表明，相比标准PINN方法，WoS-NO在相同训练步数下L2误差降低8.75倍，训练速度提升6.31倍，GPU内存消耗减少2.97倍，并支持零样本泛化至未见参数与域。
NeuroSkill(tm): Proactive Real-Time Agentic System Capable of Modeling Human State of Mind
Authors: Nataliya Kosmyna, Eugene Hauptmann
First: 2026-03-03T18:06:42+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T18:06:42+00:00
Comments: 36 pages, 18 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Real-time proactive agentic system, capable of modeling Human State of Mind, using foundation EXG model and text embeddings model, running fully offline on the edge. Unlike all previously known systems, the NeuroSkill(tm) system leverages SKILL.md description of Human's State of Mind via API and CLI provided by the system, directly from the Brain-Computer Interface (BCI) devices, which records Human biophysical and brain signals. Our custom harness - NeuroLoop(tm) - utilizes all of the above to run agentic flow that manages to engage with the Human on multiple cognitive and affective levels of their State of Mind (e.g., empathy), by providing actionable tool calls and protocol execution with explicit or implicit requests from the Human. GPLv3 open-source software with ethically aligned AI100 licensing for the skill markdown.
中文标题/摘要

Real-time proactive agentic system, capable of modeling Human State of Mind, using foundation EXG model and text embeddings model, running fully offline on the edge.

Shape Derivative-Informed Neural Operators with Application to Risk-Averse Shape Optimization
Authors: Xindi Gong, Dingcheng Luo, Thomas O'Leary-Roseberry, Ruanui Nicholson, Omar Ghattas
First: 2026-03-03T18:06:05+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T18:06:05+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Shape optimization under uncertainty (OUU) is computationally intensive for classical PDE-based methods due to the high cost of repeated sampling-based risk evaluation across many uncertainty realizations and varying geometries, while standard neural surrogates often fail to provide accurate and efficient sensitivities for optimization. We introduce Shape-DINO, a derivative-informed neural operator framework for learning PDE solution operators on families of varying geometries, with a particular focus on accelerating PDE-constrained shape OUU. Shape-DINOs encode geometric variability through diffeomorphic mappings to a fixed reference domain and employ a derivative-informed operator learning objective that jointly learns the PDE solution and its Fréchet derivatives with respect to design variables and uncertain parameters, enabling accurate state predictions and reliable gradients for large-scale OUU. We establish a priori error bounds linking surrogate accuracy to optimization error and prove universal approximation results for multi-input reduced basis neural operators in suitable $C^1$ norms. We demonstrate efficiency and scalability on three representative shape OUU problems, including boundary design for a Poisson equation and shape design governed by steady-state Navier-Stokes exterior flows in two and three dimensions. Across these examples, Shape-DINOs produce more reliable optimization results than operator surrogates trained without derivative information. In our examples, Shape-DINOs achieve 3-8 orders-of-magnitude speedups in state and gradient evaluations. Counting training data generation, Shape-DINOs reduce necessary PDE solves by 1-2 orders-of-magnitude compared to a strictly PDE-based approach for a single OUU problem. Moreover, Shape-DINO construction costs can be amortized across many objectives and risk measures, enabling large-scale shape OUU for complex systems.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于形状导数信息的神经算子及其在风险规避形状优化中的应用
由于需要在大量不确定性实现和变化几何中重复采样进行风险评估，传统基于偏微分方程（PDE）的方法在不确定性下的形状优化（OUU）中计算成本高昂；而标准神经代理通常无法提供准确且高效的优化敏感性。我们提出了Shape-DINO，一种基于导数信息的神经算子框架，用于学习在几何变化族上PDE解算子，特别关注加速PDE约束下的形状OUU。Shape-DINOs通过微分同胚映射到固定参考域来编码几何变异性，并采用导数信息驱动的算子学习目标，联合学习PDE解及其相对于设计变量和不确定参数的Fréchet导数，从而实现大规模OUU中准确的状态预测和可靠的梯度。我们建立了将代理精度与优化误差关联的先验误差界，并证明了在适当C¹范数下多输入降维基神经算子的通用逼近性。我们在三个代表性形状OUU问题上展示了其效率和可扩展性，包括泊松方程的边界设计和二维及三维稳态Navier-Stokes外流控制下的形状设计。在这些示例中，Shape-DINOs比未使用导数信息训练的算子代理产生更可靠的优化结果。在我们的示例中，Shape-DINOs在状态和梯度评估上实现了3至8个数量级的加速。计入训练数据生成，与纯PDE方法相比，Shape-DINOs将单个OUU问题所需的PDE求解次数减少了1至2个数量级。此外，Shape-DINO的构建成本可跨多个目标和风险度量进行摊销，从而支持复杂系统的大规模形状OUU。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the computational burden of classical PDE-based shape optimization under uncertainty, which requires repeated risk evaluations across varied geometries, this work introduces Shape-DINO: a derivative-informed neural operator framework that learns PDE solution operators with sensitivity to shape and parameter variations. It encodes geometric changes via diffeomorphic mappings to a reference domain and jointly trains solution and Fréchet derivatives using a derivative-aware loss, enabling accurate state predictions and gradients for optimization. Experimental results on Poisson boundary design and Navier-Stokes shape problems in 2D and 3D show Shape-DINO delivers 3–8 orders-of-magnitude faster state and gradient evaluations than standard neural surrogates, and reduces required PDE solves by 1–2 orders-of-magnitude when including training data generation. Its construction cost is amortizable across multiple objectives, making it scalable for large-scale risk-averse shape optimization.
为解决传统PDE方法在不确定性形状优化中因需反复采样不同几何与参数组合而计算成本过高的问题，本文提出Shape-DINO框架，通过微分信息引导的神经算子联合学习PDE解及其对设计变量与不确定参数的Fréchet导数。该方法通过微分同胚映射将几何变化编码至固定参考域，实现高效状态预测与可靠梯度计算。在三个代表性形状优化问题（泊松方程边界设计、二维及三维稳态Navier-Stokes外部流形形状设计）中，Shape-DINO显著优于无导数信息的标准神经代理，状态与梯度评估提速达3至8个数量级，且在包含训练数据生成时，所需PDE求解次数减少1至2个数量级。此外，该框架支持在多个目标与风险度量间复用，实现复杂系统的可扩展形状优化。
NutriBench: A Dataset for Evaluating Large Language Models on Nutrition Estimation from Meal Descriptions
Authors: Andong Hua, Mehak Preet Dhaliwal, Laya Pullela, Ryan Burke, Yao Qin
Venue: ICLR 2025
First: 2024-07-04T15:10:51+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T18:03:31+00:00
Comments: ICLR 2025
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Project1
Abstract
Accurate nutrition estimation helps people make informed dietary choices and is essential in the prevention of serious health complications. We present NutriBench, the first publicly available natural language meal description nutrition benchmark. NutriBench consists of 11,857 meal descriptions generated from real-world global dietary intake data. The data is human-verified and annotated with macro-nutrient labels, including carbohydrates, proteins, fats, and calories. We conduct an extensive evaluation of NutriBench on the task of carbohydrate estimation, testing twelve leading Large Language Models (LLMs), including GPT-4o, Llama3.1, Qwen2, Gemma2, and OpenBioLLM models, using standard, Chain-of-Thought and Retrieval-Augmented Generation strategies. Additionally, we present a study involving professional nutritionists, finding that LLMs can provide comparable but significantly faster estimates. Finally, we perform a real-world risk assessment by simulating the effect of carbohydrate predictions on the blood glucose levels of individuals with diabetes. Our work highlights the opportunities and challenges of using LLMs for nutrition estimation, demonstrating their potential to aid professionals and laypersons and improve health outcomes. Our benchmark is publicly available at: https://mehak126.github.io/nutribench.html
中文标题/摘要
标题：NutriBench：用于评估大型语言模型从餐食描述中估算营养成分的数据集
准确的营养估算有助于人们做出明智的饮食选择，并对预防严重健康并发症至关重要。我们提出了NutriBench，这是首个公开可用的自然语言餐食描述营养基准数据集。NutriBench包含11,857条基于真实全球饮食摄入数据生成的餐食描述，数据经人工验证，并标注了宏量营养素标签，包括碳水化合物、蛋白质、脂肪和热量。我们在碳水化合物估算任务上对NutriBench进行了全面评估，测试了十二种主流大型语言模型（LLM），包括GPT-4o、Llama3.1、Qwen2、Gemma2和OpenBioLLM模型，采用标准、思维链和检索增强生成策略。此外，我们还开展了一项涉及专业营养师的研究，发现LLM可提供相当但显著更快的估算结果。最后，我们通过模拟碳水化合物预测对糖尿病患者血糖水平的影响，进行了现实世界的风险评估。我们的工作突显了使用LLM进行营养估算的机会与挑战，展示了其在辅助专业人士和普通民众、改善健康结果方面的潜力。本基准数据集公开获取地址：https://mehak126.github.io/nutribench.html
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need for accurate nutrition estimation to support dietary decisions and prevent health complications, the authors introduce NutriBench, a large-scale dataset of 11,857 real-world meal descriptions annotated with macro-nutrient values. They evaluate twelve leading LLMs using standard, Chain-of-Thought, and Retrieval-Augmented Generation methods on carbohydrate estimation, finding that while models like GPT-4o and Llama3.1 perform well, their accuracy still lags behind human nutritionists. A real-world simulation further reveals that LLM predictions can significantly impact blood glucose levels in diabetics, underscoring both the utility and risks of relying on these models for nutrition estimation.
为支持饮食决策并预防健康问题，本研究提出NutriBench数据集，包含11857条真实世界餐食描述并标注宏量营养素数据。作者对十二个主流大语言模型（如GPT-4o、Llama3.1）采用标准、思维链和检索增强生成方法进行碳水化合物估算评估，发现模型表现差异显著。同时，研究对比了LLM与专业营养师的估算结果，显示LLM精度相当但效率更高，并通过模拟碳水化合物预测对糖尿病患者血糖水平的影响，揭示了LLM在营养估算中的潜力与局限。
I-CAM-UV: Integrating Causal Graphs over Non-Identical Variable Sets Using Causal Additive Models with Unobserved Variables
Authors: Hirofumi Suzuki, Kentaro Kanamori, Takuya Takagi, Thong Pham, Takashi Nicholas Maeda, Shohei Shimizu
Venue: AAAI
First: 2026-03-03T18:00:53+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T18:00:53+00:00
Comments: 16 pages, 22 figures, to appear in the 40th AAAI Conference on Artificial Intelligence (AAAI 2026)
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Causal discovery from observational data is a fundamental tool in various fields of science. While existing approaches are typically designed for a single dataset, we often need to handle multiple datasets with non-identical variable sets in practice. One straightforward approach is to estimate a causal graph from each dataset and construct a single causal graph by overlapping. However, this approach identifies limited causal relationships because unobserved variables in each dataset can be confounders, and some variable pairs may be unobserved in any dataset. To address this issue, we leverage Causal Additive Models with Unobserved Variables (CAM-UV) that provide causal graphs having information related to unobserved variables. We show that the ground truth causal graph has structural consistency with the information of CAM-UV on each dataset. As a result, we propose an approach named I-CAM-UV to integrate CAM-UV results by enumerating all consistent causal graphs. We also provide an efficient combinatorial search algorithm and demonstrate the usefulness of I-CAM-UV against existing methods.
Summary / 总结
Causal discovery from observational data is a fundamental tool in various fields of science.
Understanding and Mitigating Dataset Corruption in LLM Steering
Authors: Cullen Anderson, Narmeen Oozeer, Foad Namjoo, Remy Ogasawara, Amirali Abdullah, Jeff M. Phillips
First: 2026-03-03T18:00:49+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T18:00:49+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Contrastive steering has been shown as a simple and effective method to adjust the generative behavior of LLMs at inference time. It uses examples of prompt responses with and without a trait to identify a direction in an intermediate activation layer, and then shifts activations in this 1-dimensional subspace. However, despite its growing use in AI safety applications, the robustness of contrastive steering to noisy or adversarial data corruption is poorly understood. We initiate a study of the robustness of this process with respect to corruption of the dataset of examples used to train the steering direction. Our first observation is that contrastive steering is quite robust to a moderate amount of corruption, but unwanted side effects can be clearly and maliciously manifested when a non-trivial fraction of the training data is altered. Second, we analyze the geometry of various types of corruption, and identify some safeguards. Notably, a key step in learning the steering direction involves high-dimensional mean computation, and we show that replacing this step with a recently developed robust mean estimator often mitigates most of the unwanted effects of malicious corruption.
中文标题/摘要
标题：理解并缓解大语言模型引导中的数据集损坏
对比引导已被证明是一种简单有效的调整大语言模型推理时生成行为的方法。它通过使用具有和不具有某种特质的提示响应示例，在中间激活层中识别一个方向，然后在该一维子空间中移动激活值。然而，尽管其在人工智能安全应用中日益普及，其对噪声或对抗性数据损坏的鲁棒性尚不明确。我们首次研究了该过程在训练引导方向所用示例数据集被损坏时的鲁棒性。我们的第一个观察是，对比引导对中等程度的损坏具有相当的鲁棒性，但当训练数据中有非微小比例被篡改时，不良副作用可被明显且恶意地表现出来。其次，我们分析了各种类型损坏的几何结构，并识别出一些防护措施。值得注意的是，学习引导方向的关键步骤涉及高维均值计算，我们表明，用最近开发的鲁棒均值估计器替代该步骤，通常能缓解大部分恶意损坏带来的不良影响。

MMTok: Multimodal Coverage Maximization for Efficient Inference of VLMs
Authors: Sixun Dong, Juhua Hu, Mian Zhang, Ming Yin, Yanjie Fu, Qi Qian
Venue: ICLR 2026
First: 2025-08-25T17:57:49+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T17:59:41+00:00
Comments: Accepted by ICLR 2026. Code: https://github.com/Ironieser/mmtok , Project Homepage: https://project.ironieser.cc/mmtok
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Vision-Language Models (VLMs) demonstrate impressive performance in understanding visual content with language instruction by converting visual inputs to vision tokens. However, redundancy in vision tokens results in the degraded inference efficiency of VLMs. While many algorithms have been proposed to reduce the number of vision tokens, most of them apply only unimodal information (i.e., vision/text) for pruning and ignore the inherent multimodal property of vision-language tasks. Moreover, it lacks a generic criterion that can be applied to different modalities. To mitigate this limitation, in this work, we propose to leverage both vision and text tokens to select informative vision tokens by the coverage criterion. We first formulate the subset selection problem as a maximum coverage problem. Afterwards, a subset of vision tokens is optimized to cover the text tokens and the original set of vision tokens, simultaneously. The proposed method MMTok is extensively evaluated on benchmark datasets with different VLMs. The comparison illustrates that vision and text information are complementary, and combining multimodal information can surpass the unimodal baseline with a clear margin. Moreover, under the maximum coverage criterion on the POPE dataset, our method achieves a 1.87x speedup while maintaining 98.7% of the original performance on LLaVA-NeXT-13B. Finally, with only four vision tokens, 87.7% of the original performance is still preserved on LLaVA-1.5-7B. These results highlight the effectiveness of coverage in token selection. The code is available at https://github.com/Ironieser/mmtok
中文标题/摘要
标题：MMTok：面向视觉语言模型高效推理的多模态覆盖最大化
视觉语言模型（VLMs）通过将视觉输入转换为视觉标记，在语言指令下理解视觉内容方面表现优异。然而，视觉标记的冗余性导致VLMs推理效率下降。尽管已有多种算法旨在减少视觉标记数量，但多数仅利用单模态信息（即视觉/文本）进行剪枝，忽略了视觉语言任务固有的多模态特性，且缺乏可应用于不同模态的通用标准。为解决此问题，本文提出利用视觉与文本标记共同选择信息性视觉标记，依据覆盖准则。我们首先将子集选择问题建模为最大覆盖问题，随后优化视觉标记子集，使其同时覆盖文本标记与原始视觉标记集合。所提方法MMTok在多个基准数据集上广泛评估，结果表明视觉与文本信息互补，结合多模态信息可显著超越单模态基线。在POPE数据集上的最大覆盖准则下，该方法在LLaVA-NeXT-13B上实现1.87倍加速，性能保持98.7%；在LLaVA-1.5-7B上，仅用四个视觉标记即可保持87.7%原始性能。结果凸显覆盖准则在标记选择中的有效性。代码见https://github.com/Ironieser/mmtok
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the inefficiency caused by redundant vision tokens in Vision-Language Models (VLMs), this work proposes MMTok, a method that leverages both vision and text modalities to select informative tokens via a maximum coverage criterion. By formulating token selection as a maximum coverage problem, MMTok optimizes a subset of vision tokens to simultaneously cover both the text tokens and the original vision token set. Evaluated across multiple VLMs and benchmarks, MMTok consistently outperforms unimodal baselines, achieving a 1.87x speedup with 98.7% performance retention on LLaVA-NeXT-13B and preserving 87.7% of original performance using only four vision tokens on LLaVA-1.5-7B, demonstrating the complementary nature of multimodal information and the effectiveness of coverage-based selection.
为解决视觉语言模型中冗余视觉token导致的推理效率低下问题，本文提出MMTok方法，通过最大化视觉token对文本token和原始视觉token的覆盖度来选择信息量大的视觉token，充分利用多模态信息而非单模态方法。该方法将子集选择问题建模为最大覆盖问题，联合优化视觉token子集以实现跨模态的全面表征。实验表明，多模态覆盖显著优于单模态基线，于LLaVA-NeXT-13B上实现1.87倍加速且保持98.7%性能，仅用四个视觉token即可在LLaVA-1.5-7B上保留87.7%性能，验证了覆盖度在token选择中的有效性。
Learning When to Act or Refuse: Guarding Agentic Reasoning Models for Safe Multi-Step Tool Use
Authors: Aradhye Agarwal, Gurdit Siyan, Yash Pandya, Joykirat Singh, Akshay Nambi, Ahmed Awadallah
First: 2026-03-03T17:59:35+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T17:59:35+00:00
Comments: 24 pages, 5 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Agentic language models operate in a fundamentally different safety regime than chat models: they must plan, call tools, and execute long-horizon actions where a single misstep, such as accessing files or entering credentials, can cause irreversible harm. Existing alignment methods, largely optimized for static generation and task completion, break down in these settings due to sequential decision-making, adversarial tool feedback, and overconfident intermediate reasoning. We introduce MOSAIC, a post-training framework that aligns agents for safe multi-step tool use by making safety decisions explicit and learnable. MOSAIC structures inference as a plan, check, then act or refuse loop, with explicit safety reasoning and refusal as first-class actions. To train without trajectory-level labels, we use preference-based reinforcement learning with pairwise trajectory comparisons, which captures safety distinctions often missed by scalar rewards. We evaluate MOSAIC zero-shot across three model families, Qwen2.5-7B, Qwen3-4B-Thinking, and Phi-4, and across out-of-distribution benchmarks spanning harmful tasks, prompt injection, benign tool use, and cross-domain privacy leakage. MOSAIC reduces harmful behavior by up to 50%, increases harmful-task refusal by over 20% on injection attacks, cuts privacy leakage, and preserves or improves benign task performance, demonstrating robust generalization across models, domains, and agentic settings.
中文标题/摘要
标题：学习何时行动或拒绝：为安全多步工具使用保护代理推理模型
代理语言模型的安全机制与聊天模型根本不同：它们必须规划、调用工具并执行长周期行动，其中单次错误（如访问文件或输入凭证）可能导致不可逆损害。现有对齐方法主要针对静态生成和任务完成而优化，在这些场景下因顺序决策、对抗性工具反馈和过度自信的中间推理而失效。我们提出MOSAIC，一种后训练框架，通过显式化并可学习安全决策，使代理模型适应安全多步工具使用。MOSAIC将推理结构化为“计划—检查—行动或拒绝”循环，将显式安全推理与拒绝作为首要动作。为避免轨迹级标签训练，我们采用基于偏好的强化学习，通过成对轨迹比较捕捉常被标量奖励忽略的安全差异。我们在三个模型家族（Qwen2.5-7B、Qwen3-4B-Thinking、Phi-4）和多个分布外基准（有害任务、提示注入、良性工具使用、跨域隐私泄露）上对MOSAIC进行零样本评估。结果表明，MOSAIC可将有害行为降低50%，在注入攻击中拒绝有害任务的比例提升超20%，减少隐私泄露，同时保持或提升良性任务表现，展现出跨模型、跨领域和代理场景的稳健泛化能力。

No Memorization, No Detection: Output Distribution-Based Contamination Detection in Small Language Models
Authors: Omer Sela
First: 2026-03-03T17:55:24+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T17:55:24+00:00
Comments: 8 pages main text, 5 pages appendix, 9 figures, 7 tables. Code available at https://github.com/Sela-Omer/Contamination-Detection-Small-LM
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
CDD, or Contamination Detection via output Distribution, identifies data contamination by measuring the peakedness of a model's sampled outputs. We study the conditions under which this approach succeeds and fails on small language models ranging from 70M to 410M parameters. Using controlled contamination experiments on GSM8K, HumanEval, and MATH, we find that CDD's effectiveness depends critically on whether fine-tuning produces verbatim memorization. With low-rank adaptation, models can learn from contaminated data without memorizing it, and CDD performs at chance level even when the data is verifiably contaminated. Only when fine-tuning capacity is sufficient to induce memorization does CDD recover strong detection accuracy. Our results characterize a memorization threshold that governs detectability and highlight a practical consideration: parameter-efficient fine-tuning can produce contamination that output-distribution methods do not detect. Our code is available at https://github.com/Sela-Omer/Contamination-Detection-Small-LM
Summary / 总结
CDD, or Contamination Detection via output Distribution, identifies data contamination by measuring the peakedness of a model's sampled outputs.
该研究探讨了基于输出分布的污染检测方法（CDD）为何在小型语言模型中失效，发现CDD仅在微调引发对污染数据的逐字记忆时才有效。通过在GSM8K、HumanEval和MATH上的受控实验，作者表明低秩适应方法可在不记忆污染数据的情况下学习污染数据，导致CDD表现与随机猜测相当。只有当微调容量足以引发记忆时，CDD才能实现高检测准确率，揭示了决定可检测性的记忆阈值，并指出参数高效微调可能产生CDD无法检测的污染。
Code2Math: Can Your Code Agent Effectively Evolve Math Problems Through Exploration?
Authors: Dadi Guo, Yuejin Xie, Qingyu Liu, Jiayu Liu, Zhiyuan Fan, Qihan Ren, Shuai Shao, Tianyi Zhou, Dongrui Liu, Yi R. Fung
Venue: ICML 2026
First: 2026-03-03T17:55:10+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T17:55:10+00:00
Comments: Under review in ICML 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
As large language models (LLMs) advance their mathematical capabilities toward the IMO level, the scarcity of challenging, high-quality problems for training and evaluation has become a significant bottleneck. Simultaneously, recent code agents have demonstrated sophisticated skills in agentic coding and reasoning, suggesting that code execution can serve as a scalable environment for mathematical experimentation. In this paper, we investigate the potential of code agents to autonomously evolve existing math problems into more complex variations. We introduce a multi-agent framework designed to perform problem evolution while validating the solvability and increased difficulty of the generated problems. Our experiments demonstrate that, given sufficient test-time exploration, code agents can synthesize new, solvable problems that are structurally distinct from and more challenging than the originals. This work provides empirical evidence that code-driven agents can serve as a viable mechanism for synthesizing high-difficulty mathematical reasoning problems within scalable computational environments. Our data is available at https://github.com/TarferSoul/Code2Math.
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the shortage of high-quality math problems for training LLMs at IMO-level proficiency, this study explores whether code agents can autonomously evolve existing math problems into more complex, solvable variants. The authors introduce a multi-agent framework that iteratively modifies problems through code execution, validates their solvability and increased difficulty, and selects promising evolutions. Experiments show that with sufficient exploration, code agents generate structurally novel problems that are more challenging than the originals, demonstrating their potential as a scalable method for synthesizing high-difficulty mathematical reasoning tasks.
鉴于训练达到IMO级别能力的LLM面临高质量数学题稀缺的问题，本研究探讨代码代理是否能自主演化现有数学题为更复杂且可解的新题。作者提出一个多代理框架，通过代码执行迭代修改问题、验证其可解性与难度提升，并选择优质演化结果。实验表明，经充分探索后，代码代理能生成结构新颖、难度更高的新题，证明其在可扩展计算环境中合成高难度数学推理题的潜力。
ACE-Brain-0: Spatial Intelligence as a Shared Scaffold for Universal Embodiments
Authors: Ziyang Gong, Zehang Luo, Anke Tang, Zhe Liu, Shi Fu, Zhi Hou, Ganlin Yang, Weiyun Wang, Xiaofeng Wang, Jianbo Liu, Gen Luo, Haolan Kang, Shuang Luo, Yue Zhou, Yong Luo, Li Shen, Xiaosong Jia, Yao Mu, Xue Yang, Chunxiao Liu, Junchi Yan, Hengshuang Zhao, Dacheng Tao, Xiaogang Wang
First: 2026-03-03T17:53:45+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T17:53:45+00:00
Comments: Code: https://github.com/ACE-BRAIN-Team/ACE-Brain-0 Hugging Face: https://huggingface.co/ACE-Brain/ACE-Brain-0-8B
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Universal embodied intelligence demands robust generalization across heterogeneous embodiments, such as autonomous driving, robotics, and unmanned aerial vehicles (UAVs). However, existing embodied brain in training a unified model over diverse embodiments frequently triggers long-tail data, gradient interference, and catastrophic forgetting, making it notoriously difficult to balance universal generalization with domain-specific proficiency. In this report, we introduce ACE-Brain-0, a generalist foundation brain that unifies spatial reasoning, autonomous driving, and embodied manipulation within a single multimodal large language model~(MLLM). Our key insight is that spatial intelligence serves as a universal scaffold across diverse physical embodiments: although vehicles, robots, and UAVs differ drastically in morphology, they share a common need for modeling 3D mental space, making spatial cognition a natural, domain-agnostic foundation for cross-embodiment transfer. Building on this insight, we propose the Scaffold-Specialize-Reconcile~(SSR) paradigm, which first establishes a shared spatial foundation, then cultivates domain-specialized experts, and finally harmonizes them through data-free model merging. Furthermore, we adopt Group Relative Policy Optimization~(GRPO) to strengthen the model's comprehensive capability. Extensive experiments demonstrate that ACE-Brain-0 achieves competitive and even state-of-the-art performance across 24 spatial and embodiment-related benchmarks.
中文标题/摘要

Specificity-aware reinforcement learning for fine-grained open-world classification
Authors: Samuele Angheben, Davide Berasi, Alessandro Conti, Elisa Ricci, Yiming Wang
Venue: CVPR 2026
First: 2026-03-03T17:52:39+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T17:52:39+00:00
Comments: Accepted at CVPR 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Classifying fine-grained visual concepts under open-world settings, i.e., without a predefined label set, demands models to be both accurate and specific. Recent reasoning Large Multimodal Models (LMMs) exhibit strong visual understanding capability but tend to produce overly generic predictions when performing fine-grained image classification. Our preliminary analysis reveals that models do possess the intrinsic fine-grained domain knowledge. However, promoting more specific predictions (specificity) without compromising correct ones (correctness) remains a non-trivial and understudied challenge. In this work, we investigate how to steer reasoning LMMs toward predictions that are both correct and specific. We propose a novel specificity-aware reinforcement learning framework, SpeciaRL, to fine-tune reasoning LMMs on fine-grained image classification under the open-world setting. SpeciaRL introduces a dynamic, verifier-based reward signal anchored to the best predictions within online rollouts, promoting specificity while respecting the model's capabilities to prevent incorrect predictions. Our out-of-domain experiments show that SpeciaRL delivers the best trade-off between correctness and specificity across extensive fine-grained benchmarks, surpassing existing methods and advancing open-world fine-grained image classification. Code and model are publicly available at https://github.com/s-angheben/SpeciaRL.
中文标题/摘要
标题：面向细粒度开放世界分类的特定性感知强化学习

为解决开放世界细粒度图像分类中模型预测准确但缺乏具体性的难题，作者提出SpeciaRL框架，通过强化学习引导推理型大模型生成更具体的预测，同时保持正确性。该方法采用基于在线回滚的动态奖励机制，结合验证器反馈，激励模型输出既准确又详尽的预测。实验表明，SpeciaRL在多个细粒度基准上实现了正确性与具体性之间的最佳平衡，超越现有方法。
Infinite dimensional generative sensing
Authors: Paolo Angella, Vito Paolo Pastore, Matteo Santacesaria
First: 2026-03-03T17:52:18+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T17:52:18+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Deep generative models have become a standard for modeling priors for inverse problems, going beyond classical sparsity-based methods. However, existing theoretical guarantees are mostly confined to finite-dimensional vector spaces, creating a gap when the physical signals are modeled as functions in Hilbert spaces. This work presents a rigorous framework for generative compressed sensing in Hilbert spaces. We extend the notion of local coherence in an infinite-dimensional setting, to derive optimal, resolution-independent sampling distributions. Thanks to a generalization of the Restricted Isometry Property, we show that stable recovery holds when the number of measurements is proportional to the prior's intrinsic dimension (up to logarithmic factors), independent of the ambient dimension. Finally, numerical experiments on the Darcy flow equation validate our theoretical findings and demonstrate that in severely undersampled regimes, employing lower-resolution generators acts as an implicit regularizer, improving reconstruction stability.
Summary / 总结
Deep generative models have become a standard for modeling priors for inverse problems, going beyond classical sparsity-based methods.
为将深度生成模型推广到无限维信号空间，本文构建了希尔伯特空间中的生成压缩感知理论框架。通过无限维局部相干性的推广，推导出与分辨率无关的最优采样分布。借助广义的等距性质，证明在测量数与先验内在维度成比例（对数因子内）时可实现稳定恢复，与嵌入维度无关。对达西流方程的数值实验验证了理论，并表明在严重欠采样下使用低分辨率生成器可提升重建稳定性。
Chain of World: World Model Thinking in Latent Motion
Authors: Fuxiang Yang, Donglin Di, Lulu Tang, Xuancheng Zhang, Lei Fan, Hao Li, Chen Wei, Tonghua Su, Baorui Ma
First: 2026-03-03T17:52:06+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T17:52:06+00:00
Comments: Accepted by CVPR2026. Project page: https://fx-hit.github.io/cowvla-io/
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Project1 · Project2
Abstract
Vision-Language-Action (VLA) models are a promising path toward embodied intelligence, yet they often overlook the predictive and temporal-causal structure underlying visual dynamics. World-model VLAs address this by predicting future frames, but waste capacity reconstructing redundant backgrounds. Latent-action VLAs encode frame-to-frame transitions compactly, but lack temporally continuous dynamic modeling and world knowledge. To overcome these limitations, we introduce CoWVLA (Chain-of-World VLA), a new "Chain of World" paradigm that unifies world-model temporal reasoning with a disentangled latent motion representation. First, a pretrained video VAE serves as a latent motion extractor, explicitly factorizing video segments into structure and motion latents. Then, during pre-training, the VLA learns from an instruction and an initial frame to infer a continuous latent motion chain and predict the segment's terminal frame. Finally, during co-fine-tuning, this latent dynamic is aligned with discrete action prediction by jointly modeling sparse keyframes and action sequences in a unified autoregressive decoder. This design preserves the world-model benefits of temporal reasoning and world knowledge while retaining the compactness and interpretability of latent actions, enabling efficient visuomotor learning. Extensive experiments on robotic simulation benchmarks show that CoWVLA outperforms existing world-model and latent-action approaches and achieves moderate computational efficiency, highlighting its potential as a more effective VLA pretraining paradigm. The project website can be found at https://fx-hit.github.io/cowvla-io.
Summary / 总结
Vision-Language-Action (VLA) models are a promising path toward embodied intelligence, yet they often overlook the predictive and temporal-causal structure underlying visual dynamics.
为提升视觉-语言-动作系统对时序动态和世界知识的建模能力，作者提出CoWVLA（Chain-of-World VLA）框架，融合世界模型推理与解耦的潜在运动表示。该方法利用预训练视频VAE提取结构与运动潜在表示，训练VLA从指令和初始帧预测连续潜在运动链并预测终端帧；在联合微调阶段，通过统一自回归解码器将潜在动态与离散动作对齐。在机器人仿真基准测试中，CoWVLA优于现有世界模型与潜在动作方法，同时保持中等计算效率，验证其作为VLA预训练范式的有效性。
BeyondSWE: Can Current Code Agent Survive Beyond Single-Repo Bug Fixing?
Authors: Guoxin Chen, Fanzhe Meng, Jiale Zhao, Minghao Li, Daixuan Cheng, Huatong Song, Jie Chen, Yuzhi Lin, Hui Chen, Xin Zhao, Ruihua Song, Chang Liu, Cheng Chen, Kai Jia, Ji-Rong Wen
First: 2026-03-03T17:52:01+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T17:52:01+00:00
Comments: Benchmark: https://huggingface.co/datasets/AweAI-Team/BeyondSWE. Repo: https://github.com/AweAI-Team/BeyondSWE. Scaffold: https://github.com/AweAI-Team/AweAgent
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Current benchmarks for code agents primarily assess narrow, repository-specific fixes, overlooking critical real-world challenges such as cross-repository reasoning, domain-specialized problem solving, dependency-driven migration, and full-repository generation. To address this gap, we introduce BeyondSWE, a comprehensive benchmark that broadens existing evaluations along two axes - resolution scope and knowledge scope - using 500 real-world instances across four distinct settings. Experimental results reveal a significant capability gap: even frontier models plateau below 45% success, and no single model performs consistently across task types. To systematically investigate the role of external knowledge, we develop SearchSWE, a framework that integrates deep search with coding abilities. Our experiments show that search augmentation yields inconsistent gains and can in some cases degrade performance, highlighting the difficulty of emulating developer-like workflows that interleave search and reasoning during coding tasks. This work offers both a realistic, challenging evaluation benchmark and a flexible framework to advance research toward more capable code agents.
中文标题/摘要
标题：BeyondSWE：当前代码代理能否超越单一仓库的Bug修复？
