GAN-Based Single-Stage Defense for Traffic Sign Classification Under Adversarial Patch
Authors: Abyad Enan, Mashrur Chowdhury
First: 2025-03-16T16:47:44+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T17:50:39+00:00
Comments: This work has been submitted to a peer-reviewed journal and is currently under review
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Computer vision plays a critical role in ensuring the safe navigation of autonomous vehicles (AVs). An AV perception module facilitates safe navigation. This module enables AVs to recognize traffic signs, traffic lights, and various road users. However, the perception module is vulnerable to adversarial attacks, which can compromise its accuracy and reliability. One such attack is the adversarial patch attack (APA), an attack in which an adversary strategically places a specially crafted sticker on an object to deceive object classifiers. Such an APA can cause AVs to misclassify traffic signs, leading to catastrophic incidents. To enhance the security of an AV perception system against APAs, this study develops a Generative Adversarial Network (GAN)-based single-stage defense strategy for traffic sign classification. This approach is tailored to defend against APAs across different classes of traffic signs, without prior knowledge of a patch's design, and is effective against patches of varying sizes. In addition, our single-stage defense is computationally efficient, requiring significantly lower computation time than existing multi-stage defenses, making it suitable for real-time deployment in autonomous driving systems. Compared to a classifier without any defense mechanism, our experimental analysis demonstrates that the defense strategy presented in this paper improves our classifier's accuracy under APA conditions by up to 90% considering the traffic sign classes considered in this study. and overall classification accuracy is enhanced by 55% for all traffic signs considered in this study. Our defense strategy is model agnostic, making it applicable to any traffic sign classifier, regardless of the underlying classification model.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于GAN的对抗贴纸攻击下交通标志分类的一阶段防御方法
计算机视觉在保障自动驾驶汽车（AV）安全导航中起关键作用。AV感知模块可识别交通标志、交通灯及各类道路使用者，但易受对抗攻击影响，降低其准确性和可靠性。其中，对抗贴纸攻击（APA）通过在物体上贴设特制贴纸误导分类器，可能导致AV误判交通标志，引发灾难性事故。本文提出一种基于生成对抗网络（GAN）的一阶段防御策略，专门针对不同类交通标志的APA，无需预先知晓贴纸设计，且对不同尺寸贴纸均有效。该方法计算效率高，显著优于现有多阶段防御方案，适合实时部署于自动驾驶系统。实验表明，相较于无防御机制的分类器，本文方法在APA条件下使所研究交通标志类别的分类准确率提升最高达90%，整体交通标志分类准确率提升55%。该防御策略模型无关，适用于任何交通标志分类器。

To enhance the security of autonomous vehicle perception systems against adversarial patch attacks that can misclassify traffic signs, this study proposes a GAN-based single-stage defense strategy. The method leverages generative adversarial networks to detect and mitigate adversarial patches without requiring prior knowledge of patch design or size, and is compatible with any underlying classifier. Experimental results show that this defense improves classification accuracy under adversarial patch attacks by up to 90% for specific traffic sign classes and by 55% overall across all classes, while maintaining computational efficiency suitable for real-time deployment in autonomous driving systems.
为提升自动驾驶系统对贴纸式对抗攻击的防御能力，该研究提出一种基于生成对抗网络的单阶段防御方法。该方法无需预先了解攻击贴纸的设计或尺寸，即可有效检测并缓解对抗攻击，适用于任意交通标志分类器。实验表明，该防御方案在特定交通标志类别上可将攻击下的分类准确率提升90%，整体分类准确率提升55%，且计算效率高，适合实时部署于自动驾驶系统中。
MoD-DPO: Towards Mitigating Cross-modal Hallucinations in Omni LLMs using Modality Decoupled Preference Optimization
Authors: Ashutosh Chaubey, Jiacheng Pang, Mohammad Soleymani
Venue: CVPR 2026
First: 2026-03-03T17:50:24+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T17:50:24+00:00
Comments: CVPR 2026. Project Page: https://mod-dpo.github.io/
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Project1
Abstract
Omni-modal large language models (omni LLMs) have recently achieved strong performance across audiovisual understanding tasks, yet they remain highly susceptible to cross-modal hallucinations arising from spurious correlations and dominant language priors. In this work, we propose Modality-Decoupled Direct Preference Optimization (MoD-DPO), a simple and effective framework for improving modality grounding in omni LLMs. MoD-DPO introduces modality-aware regularization terms that explicitly enforce invariance to corruptions in irrelevant modalities and sensitivity to perturbations in relevant modalities, thereby reducing unintended cross-modal interactions. To further mitigate over-reliance on textual priors, we incorporate a language-prior debiasing penalty that discourages hallucination-prone text-only responses. Extensive experiments across multiple audiovisual hallucination benchmarks demonstrate that MoD-DPO consistently improves perception accuracy and hallucination resistance, outperforming previous preference optimization baselines under similar training budgets. Our findings underscore the importance of modality-faithful alignment and demonstrate a scalable path toward more reliable and resilient multimodal foundation models.
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the susceptibility of omni-modal LLMs to cross-modal hallucinations due to spurious correlations and language priors, this work introduces MoD-DPO, a modality-decoupled preference optimization framework. It employs modality-aware regularization to enforce invariance to irrelevant modality corruptions and sensitivity to relevant modality perturbations, while adding a language-prior debiasing penalty to suppress text-only hallucinations. Experimental results across multiple audiovisual benchmarks show that MoD-DPO consistently improves perception accuracy and hallucination resistance, outperforming prior preference optimization methods under comparable training budgets.
为解决多模态大语言模型因虚假关联和语言先验导致的跨模态幻觉问题，本文提出MoD-DPO框架，通过模态解耦的偏好优化方法增强模态对齐。该方法引入模态感知正则项，强制模型对无关模态扰动保持不变，对相关模态扰动保持敏感，并加入语言先验去偏惩罚以抑制文本主导的幻觉响应。在多个视听幻觉基准测试中，MoD-DPO显著提升感知准确率与抗幻觉能力，优于同等训练预算下的现有偏好优化基线方法。
CoPeP: Benchmarking Continual Pretraining for Protein Language Models
Authors: Darshan Patil, Pranshu Malviya, Mathieu Reymond, Quentin Fournier, Sarath Chandar
First: 2026-02-27T19:04:32+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T17:50:01+00:00
Comments: 29 pages, 25 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Protein language models (pLMs) have recently gained significant attention for their ability to uncover relationships between sequence, structure, and function from evolutionary statistics, thereby accelerating therapeutic drug discovery. These models learn from large protein databases that are continuously updated by the biology community and whose dynamic nature motivates the application of continual learning, not only to keep up with the ever-growing data, but also as an opportunity to take advantage of the temporal meta-information that is created during this process. As a result, we introduce the Continual Pretraining of Protein Language Models (CoPeP) benchmark, a novel benchmark for evaluating continual learning approaches on pLMs. Specifically, we curate a sequence of protein datasets derived from the UniProt Knowledgebase spanning a decade and define metrics to assess pLM performance across 31 protein understanding tasks. We evaluate several methods from the continual learning literature, including replay, unlearning, and plasticity-based methods, some of which have never been applied to models and data of this scale. Our findings reveal that incorporating temporal meta-information improves perplexity by up to 7% even when compared to training on data from all tasks jointly. Moreover, even at scale, several continual learning methods outperform naive continual pretraining. The CoPeP benchmark offers an exciting opportunity to study these methods at scale in an impactful real-world application.
中文标题/摘要
标题：CoPeP：蛋白质语言模型持续预训练的基准测试
蛋白质语言模型（pLMs）因其能从进化统计中揭示序列、结构与功能之间的关系，从而加速治疗性药物发现，近期备受关注。这些模型从不断更新的大型蛋白质数据库中学习，其动态特性促使应用持续学习，不仅为应对日益增长的数据，也为了利用在此过程中产生的时序元信息。为此，我们提出了蛋白质语言模型持续预训练（CoPeP）基准，用于评估pLMs上的持续学习方法。具体而言，我们从UniProt知识库中整理了跨越十年的蛋白质数据集序列，并定义了31项蛋白质理解任务的评估指标。我们评估了持续学习文献中的多种方法，包括重放、遗忘和可塑性方法，其中一些方法此前从未应用于如此规模的模型和数据。我们的发现表明，即使与联合训练所有任务的数据相比，融入时序元信息也能将困惑度降低高达7%。此外，即使在大规模情况下，部分持续学习方法仍优于朴素的持续预训练。CoPeP基准为在具有实际意义的真实应用场景中大规模研究这些方法提供了绝佳机会。

Mining Hierarchies with Conviction: Constructing the CS1 Skill Hierarchy with Pairwise Comparisons over Skill Distributions
Authors: Dip Kiran Pradhan Newar, Max Fowler, David H. Smith, Seth Poulsen
Venue: Computer Science Education (2025) 1-22
First: 2024-10-16T18:59:24+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T17:49:53+00:00
Comments: Published in the Taylor & Francis Journal "Computer Science Education"
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Background and Context: Some skills taught in introductory programming courses are categorized into 1) explaining code, 2) arranging lines of code in correct sequence, 3) tracing through the execution of a program, and 4) writing code from scratch. Objective: Knowing if a programming skill is a prerequisite to another would benefit teachers in properly planning the course and structuring the order in which they present activities relating to new content. Prior attempts to establish a skill hierarchy have suffered from methodological issues. Method: In this study, we used the conviction measure from association rule mining to perform pair-wise comparisons of five skills: Write, Trace, Reverse trace, Sequence, and Explain code. We used the data from four exams with more than 600 participants where students solved programming assignments of different skills for several programming topics. Findings: Our findings matched the previous finding that tracing is a prerequisite for students to learn to write code. Contradicting the previous claims, our analysis showed that using the mean threshold writing code is a prerequisite to explaining code. However, there is no clear relationship when we change the threshold to the median. Unlike prior work, we did not find a clear prerequisite relationship between sequencing code and writing or explaining code. Implications: Our research can help instructors by systematically arranging the skills students exercise when encountering a new topic. The goal is to help instructors properly teach and assess programming in a fashion most effective for learning by leveraging the relationship between skills.
中文标题/摘要
标题：使用置信度挖掘层次结构：通过技能分布的成对比较构建CS1技能层次
背景与情境：一些在入门编程课程中教授的技能被分为四类：1) 解释代码，2) 按正确顺序排列代码行，3) 跟踪程序执行过程，4) 从零编写代码。目标：了解某项编程技能是否是另一项技能的前提，将有助于教师合理规划课程并安排与新内容相关的活动顺序。此前建立技能层次结构的尝试存在方法论问题。方法：本研究采用关联规则挖掘中的置信度度量，对五项技能——编写、跟踪、反向跟踪、排序和解释代码——进行成对比较。我们使用了四次考试的数据，参与学生超过600人，他们在多个编程主题上完成不同技能的编程任务。发现：我们的发现与先前研究一致，即跟踪是学习编写代码的前提。与先前主张相反，我们的分析表明，当使用均值阈值时，编写代码是解释代码的前提。但当阈值改为中位数时，两者之间无明显关系。与以往研究不同，我们未发现代码排序与编写或解释代码之间存在明确的前提关系。意义：本研究可帮助教师系统性地安排学生在接触新主题时所练习的技能，旨在通过利用技能间的关联，以最有效的方式帮助教师教授和评估编程，促进学习。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need to structure programming skills hierarchically for effective teaching, this study employs the conviction measure from association rule mining to analyze pairwise relationships among five skills—Write, Trace, Reverse trace, Sequence, and Explain code—using data from four exams with over 600 students. The method compares skill distributions across programming topics to infer prerequisite relationships. Results show that tracing precedes writing code, contradicting prior assumptions that writing is a prerequisite for explaining code, especially when using the mean threshold; however, no clear relationship emerges with the median threshold. Additionally, sequencing shows no clear prerequisite link to writing or explaining code, differing from previous findings. This work provides a data-driven framework for instructors to sequence skill instruction optimally.
为优化编程教学中的技能顺序，本研究采用关联规则挖掘中的置信度度量，对五个编程技能——编写、追踪、逆向追踪、排序和解释代码——进行成对比较，基于四场考试中600多名学生的数据。方法通过分析技能在不同编程主题中的分布，推断技能间的先决关系。结果表明，追踪是编写代码的先决条件，与以往认为编写是解释代码先决条件的结论相悖（在均值阈值下）；但当使用中位数阈值时，该关系不明显。此外，排序技能与编写或解释代码之间无明确先决关系，与以往研究结论不同。该研究为教师提供数据驱动的技能教学排序框架。
A Covering Framework for Offline POMDPs Learning using Belief Space Metric
Authors: Youheng Zhu, Yiping Lu
First: 2026-03-03T17:48:20+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T17:48:20+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
In off policy evaluation (OPE) for partially observable Markov decision processes (POMDPs), an agent must infer hidden states from past observations, which exacerbates both the curse of horizon and the curse of memory in existing OPE methods. This paper introduces a novel covering analysis framework that exploits the intrinsic metric structure of the belief space (distributions over latent states) to relax traditional coverage assumptions. By assuming value relevant functions are Lipschitz continuous in the belief space, we derive error bounds that mitigate exponential blow ups in horizon and memory length. Our unified analysis technique applies to a broad class of OPE algorithms, yielding concrete error bounds and coverage requirements expressed in terms of belief space metrics rather than raw history coverage. We illustrate the improved sample efficiency of this framework via case studies: the double sampling Bellman error minimization algorithm, and the memory based future dependent value functions (FDVF). In both cases, our coverage definition based on the belief space metric yields tighter bounds.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于信念空间度量的离线POMDP学习覆盖框架
在部分可观测马尔可夫决策过程（POMDP）的离策略评估（OPE）中，智能体必须从历史观测中推断隐藏状态，这加剧了现有OPE方法中的时域诅咒和记忆诅咒。本文提出一种新颖的覆盖分析框架，利用信念空间（对潜在状态的分布）的内在度量结构，放松传统覆盖假设。通过假设价值相关函数在信念空间中是利普希茨连续的，我们推导出误差界，缓解时域和记忆长度上的指数级膨胀。我们的统一分析技术适用于广泛的OPE算法，得出以信念空间度量而非原始历史覆盖表达的具体误差界和覆盖要求。通过案例研究——双采样贝尔曼误差最小化算法和基于记忆的未来依赖价值函数（FDVF）——我们展示了该框架的样本效率提升：基于信念空间度量的覆盖定义可获得更紧的界。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the computational challenges of off-policy evaluation in POMDPs, where hidden states must be inferred from observations, this paper proposes a covering framework that leverages the metric structure of belief space to relax traditional coverage assumptions. By assuming value functions are Lipschitz continuous in belief space, the authors derive error bounds that avoid exponential growth in horizon and memory length. Applied to two OPE algorithms—double sampling Bellman error minimization and memory-based FDVF—the framework demonstrates tighter error bounds and improved sample efficiency compared to methods relying on raw history coverage.
为解决POMDP离线评估中因隐藏状态推断导致的时域与记忆长度诅咒问题，本文提出一种基于信念空间度量的覆盖框架，通过假设价值函数在信念空间中满足Lipschitz连续性，推导出避免指数级增长的误差界。该框架统一适用于多种OPE算法，将覆盖要求从原始历史覆盖转为信念空间度量。在双采样贝尔曼误差最小化与基于记忆的未来依赖价值函数两个案例中，该框架均实现了更紧的误差界与更高的样本效率。
Reproduction and Replication of an Adversarial Stylometry Experiment
Authors: Haining Wang, Patrick Juola, Allen Riddell
First: 2022-08-15T18:24:00+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T17:48:05+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Maintaining anonymity in natural language communication remains a challenging task. Even when the number of candidate authors is large, standard authorship attribution techniques that analyze writing style predict the original author with uncomfortably high accuracy. Adversarial stylometry provides a defense against authorship attribution, helping users avoid unwanted deanonymization. This paper reproduces and replicates experiments from a seminal study of defenses against authorship attribution (Brennan et al., 2012). After reproducing the experiment using the original data, we then replicate the experiment by repeating the online field experiment using the procedures described in the original paper. Although we reach the same conclusion as the original paper, our results suggest that the defenses studied may be overstated in their effectiveness. This is largely due to the absence of a control group in the original study. In our replication, we find evidence suggesting that an entirely automatic method, round-trip translation, warrants re-examination because it appears to reduce the effectiveness of established authorship attribution methods.
中文标题/摘要
标题：对抗风格学实验的复制与再现
在自然语言交流中保持匿名性仍是一项挑战。即使候选作者数量庞大，分析写作风格的标准作者归属技术仍能以令人不安的高精度预测原始作者。对抗风格学为防止作者归属提供了一种防御手段，帮助用户避免不希望的去匿名化。本文复制并再现了关于对抗作者归属防御的开创性研究（Brennan等，2012）的实验。在使用原始数据复现实验后，我们通过重复原论文描述的在线田野实验进行再实验。尽管我们得出与原论文相同的结论，但我们的结果表明，所研究的防御措施可能被高估了其有效性。这主要归因于原研究中缺乏对照组。在我们的再实验中，我们发现，完全自动的方法——往返翻译——值得重新审视，因为它似乎降低了现有作者归属方法的有效性。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the challenge of maintaining anonymity in natural language communication, this paper reproduces and replicates an adversarial stylometry experiment originally conducted by Brennan et al. (2012) to evaluate defenses against authorship attribution. The authors first reproduce the original experiment using the source data, then conduct a new online field experiment following the same procedures. Their findings confirm the original conclusion that adversarial defenses can hinder attribution, but also reveal that the original study’s lack of a control group may have inflated claims of defense effectiveness. Notably, their replication suggests that round-trip translation—an automatic method—may significantly reduce the accuracy of standard attribution models, warranting further investigation.
为应对自然语言通信中保持匿名性的挑战，本文复现并重复了Brennan等人（2012）关于对抗性风格学防御实验，旨在评估对抗作者归属的方法有效性。作者首先使用原始数据复现实验，随后按原方法进行在线田野实验。结果证实原研究结论——对抗方法可削弱归属准确率，但指出原研究因缺乏对照组可能高估了防御效果。特别地，复现实验发现“往返翻译”这一全自动方法似乎能显著降低传统归属模型的准确性，值得重新评估。
Out-of-Support Generalisation via Weight-Space Sequence Modelling
Authors: Roussel Desmond Nzoyem
Venue: ICLR 2026
First: 2026-02-14T01:51:54+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T17:47:12+00:00
Comments: Published at the Catch, Adapt, and Operate (CAO): Monitoring ML Models Under Drift workshop at ICLR 2026. Contains 8 pages, 2 figures, 1 table, and 1 algorithm
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
As breakthroughs in deep learning transform key industries, models are increasingly required to extrapolate on datapoints found outside the range of the training set, a challenge we coin as out-of-support (OoS) generalisation. However, neural networks frequently exhibit catastrophic failure on OoS samples, yielding unrealistic but overconfident predictions. We address this challenge by reformulating the OoS generalisation problem as a sequence modelling task in the weight space, wherein the training set is partitioned into concentric shells corresponding to discrete sequential steps. Our WeightCaster framework yields plausible, interpretable, and uncertainty-aware predictions without necessitating explicit inductive biases, all the while maintaining high computational efficiency. Emprical validation on a synthetic cosine dataset and real-world air quality sensor readings demonstrates performance competitive or superior to the state-of-the-art. By enhancing reliability beyond in-distribution scenarios, these results hold significant implications for the wider adoption of artificial intelligence in safety-critical applications.
中文标题/摘要
标题：通过权重空间序列建模实现超出支持范围的泛化
随着深度学习在关键行业的突破性进展，模型越来越需要对训练集范围外的数据点进行外推，我们将其称为超出支持（OoS）泛化。然而，神经网络在OoS样本上常出现灾难性失败，产生不现实但过于自信的预测。我们通过将OoS泛化问题重新表述为权重空间中的序列建模任务来解决这一挑战，其中训练集按离散序列步骤划分为同心壳层。我们的WeightCaster框架无需显式归纳偏置，即可生成合理、可解释且具备不确定性感知的预测，同时保持高计算效率。在合成余弦数据集和真实世界空气质量传感器读数上的实证验证表明，其性能与当前最先进方法相当或更优。这些结果通过提升超出分布场景下的可靠性，对人工智能在安全关键应用中的广泛应用具有重要意义。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need for neural networks to reliably generalize beyond training data, this work tackles out-of-support generalization by casting it as a sequence modeling problem in weight space, where training data is organized into concentric shells representing sequential steps. The WeightCaster framework models this progression to generate plausible, interpretable, and uncertainty-aware predictions without relying on explicit inductive biases, while maintaining computational efficiency. Experiments on synthetic cosine data and real-world air quality sensors show that WeightCaster achieves performance competitive or superior to existing methods, demonstrating enhanced reliability for safety-critical AI applications.
为解决神经网络在训练数据范围外泛化能力差的问题，该研究将出支持泛化问题转化为权重空间中的序列建模任务，通过将训练数据按离散步骤划分成同心壳层。提出的WeightCaster框架无需显式归纳偏置，即可生成合理、可解释且具备不确定性感知的预测，同时保持高效计算。在合成余弦数据和真实空气质量传感器数据上的实验表明，WeightCaster性能与当前最先进方法相当或更优，为安全关键领域AI应用的可靠部署提供了重要支持。
Expectation and Acoustic Neural Network Representations Enhance Music Identification from Brain Activity
Authors: Shogo Noguchi, Taketo Akama, Tai Nakamura, Shun Minamikawa, Natalia Polouliakh
First: 2026-03-03T17:47:09+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T17:47:09+00:00
Comments: 39 pages, 9 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
During music listening, cortical activity encodes both acoustic and expectation-related information. Prior work has shown that ANN representations resemble cortical representations and can serve as supervisory signals for EEG recognition. Here we show that distinguishing acoustic and expectation-related ANN representations as teacher targets improves EEG-based music identification. Models pretrained to predict either representation outperform non-pretrained baselines, and combining them yields complementary gains that exceed strong seed ensembles formed by varying random initializations. These findings show that teacher representation type shapes downstream performance and that representation learning can be guided by neural encoding. This work points toward advances in predictive music cognition and neural decoding. Our expectation representation, computed directly from raw signals without manual labels, reflects predictive structure beyond onset or pitch, enabling investigation of multilayer predictive encoding across diverse stimuli. Its scalability to large, diverse datasets further suggests potential for developing general-purpose EEG models grounded in cortical encoding principles.

Scalable Uncertainty Quantification for Black-Box Density-Based Clustering
Authors: Nicola Bariletto, Stephen G. Walker
First: 2026-03-03T17:46:49+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T17:46:49+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We introduce a novel framework for uncertainty quantification in clustering. By combining the martingale posterior paradigm with density-based clustering, uncertainty in the estimated density is naturally propagated to the clustering structure. The approach scales effectively to high-dimensional and irregularly shaped data by leveraging modern neural density estimators and GPU-friendly parallel computation. We establish frequentist consistency guarantees and validate the methodology on synthetic and real data.

ProSMA-UNet: Decoder Conditioning for Proximal-Sparse Skip Feature Selection
Authors: Chun-Wun Cheng, Yanqi Cheng, Peiyuan Jing, Guang Yang, Carola-Bibiane Schönlieb, Angelica I. Aviles-Rivero
First: 2026-03-03T17:46:29+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T17:46:29+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Project1
Abstract
Medical image segmentation commonly relies on U-shaped encoder-decoder architectures such as U-Net, where skip connections preserve fine spatial detail by injecting high-resolution encoder features into the decoder. However, these skip pathways also propagate low-level textures, background clutter, and acquisition noise, allowing irrelevant information to bypass deeper semantic filtering -- an issue that is particularly detrimental in low-contrast clinical imaging. Although attention gates have been introduced to address this limitation, they typically produce dense sigmoid masks that softly reweight features rather than explicitly removing irrelevant activations. We propose ProSMA-UNet (Proximal-Sparse Multi-Scale Attention U-Net), which reformulates skip gating as a decoder-conditioned sparse feature selection problem. ProSMA constructs a multi-scale compatibility field using lightweight depthwise dilated convolutions to capture relevance across local and contextual scales, then enforces explicit sparsity via an $\ell_1$ proximal operator with learnable per-channel thresholds, yielding a closed-form soft-thresholding gate that can remove noisy responses. To further suppress semantically irrelevant channels, ProSMA incorporates decoder-conditioned channel gating driven by global decoder context. Extensive experiments on challenging 2D and 3D benchmarks demonstrate state-of-the-art performance, with particularly large gains ($\approx20$\%) on difficult 3D segmentation tasks. Project page: https://math-ml-x.github.io/ProSMA-UNet/
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the problem that skip connections in U-Net architectures propagate irrelevant low-level noise in medical imaging, ProSMA-UNet reformulates skip gating as a decoder-conditioned sparse feature selection task. It employs lightweight depthwise dilated convolutions to build a multi-scale compatibility field and applies an $\ell_1$ proximal operator with learnable per-channel thresholds to enforce explicit sparsity, yielding a soft-thresholding gate that removes noisy activations. Additionally, it integrates decoder-conditioned channel gating to suppress semantically irrelevant channels. Experiments on 2D and 3D medical segmentation benchmarks show state-of-the-art performance, with particularly significant gains of approximately 20% on challenging 3D tasks.
为了解决U-Net架构中跳连接传播无关特征、降低低对比度医学图像分割性能的问题，ProSMA-UNet将跳连接门控重构为解码器条件下的稀疏特征选择任务。它利用轻量级深度可分离空洞卷积构建多尺度兼容场，再通过带有可学习通道阈值的$\ell_1$近端算子强制实现稀疏性，从而显式去除噪声激活。同时，引入解码器条件通道门控机制，利用全局解码器上下文抑制语义无关通道。在2D和3D医学分割基准测试中，该方法达到最先进性能，尤其在困难的3D任务上提升约20%。
Loss Barcode: A Topological Measure of Escapability in Loss Landscapes
Authors: Serguei Barannikov, Daria Voronkova, Alexander Mironenko, Ilya Trofimov, Alexander Korotin, Grigorii Sotnikov, Evgeny Burnaev
First: 2020-12-31T18:53:25+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T17:45:53+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Neural network training is commonly based on SGD. However, the understanding of SGD's ability to converge to good local minima, given the non-convex nature of loss functions and the intricate geometric characteristics of loss landscapes, remains limited. In this paper, we apply topological data analysis methods to loss landscapes to gain insights into the learning process and generalization properties of deep neural networks. We use the loss function topology to relate the local behavior of gradient descent trajectories with the global properties of the loss surface. For this purpose, we define the neural network's Topological Obstructions score ("TO-score") with the help of robust topological invariants, barcodes of the loss function, which quantify the escapability of local minima for gradient-based optimization. Our two principal observations are: 1) the loss barcode of the neural network decreases with increasing depth and width, therefore the topological obstructions to learning diminish; 2) in certain situations there is a connection between the length of minima segments in the loss barcode and the minima's generalization errors. Our statements are based on extensive experiments with fully connected, convolutional, and transformer architectures and several datasets including MNIST, FMNIST, CIFAR10, CIFAR100, SVHN, and multilingual OSCAR text dataset.
中文标题/摘要
标题：损失条形码：损失景观中可逃逸性的拓扑度量
神经网络训练通常基于随机梯度下降（SGD）。然而，鉴于损失函数的非凸性及损失景观复杂的几何特性，对SGD能否收敛至良好局部极小值的理解仍有限。本文应用拓扑数据分析方法研究损失景观，以深入了解深度神经网络的学习过程与泛化特性。我们利用损失函数拓扑，将梯度下降轨迹的局部行为与损失表面的全局性质关联起来。为此，我们借助鲁棒拓扑不变量——损失函数的条形码，定义了神经网络的拓扑障碍得分（"TO-score"），用于量化梯度优化中局部极小值的可逃逸性。我们的两个主要观察结果是：1）神经网络的损失条形码随深度和宽度增加而减小，因此学习的拓扑障碍减弱；2）在某些情况下，损失条形码中极小值段的长度与该极小值的泛化误差相关。我们的结论基于在全连接、卷积和Transformer架构上，使用MNIST、FMNIST、CIFAR10、CIFAR100、SVHN及多语言OSCAR文本数据集进行的大量实验。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need to understand how gradient descent navigates complex, non-convex loss landscapes in deep neural networks, this paper introduces a topological measure called the Topological Obstructions score (TO-score) derived from loss function barcodes. The method uses persistent homology to quantify the escapability of local minima, linking local gradient dynamics to global loss surface properties. Experimental results across multiple architectures and datasets show that the TO-score decreases with increasing network depth and width, indicating reduced topological barriers to learning. Additionally, the length of minima segments in the loss barcode correlates with generalization error, suggesting a topological basis for model performance.
为了解决深度神经网络在非凸损失景观中梯度下降优化机制不明确的问题，本文提出了一种基于损失条形码拓扑不变量的“拓扑障碍得分”（TO-score），用于量化局部极小值的逃逸能力。该方法通过持久同调分析损失函数的全局拓扑结构，并将局部梯度下降行为与全局几何特性关联。实验表明，随着网络深度和宽度增加，TO-score下降，表明优化障碍减少；同时，在特定情况下，损失条形码中极小值段长度与泛化误差呈正相关。
Robotic Grasping and Placement Controlled by EEG-Based Hybrid Visual and Motor Imagery
Authors: Yichang Liu, Tianyu Wang, Ziyi Ye, Yawei Li, Yu-Gang Jiang, Shouyan Wang, Yanwei Fu
First: 2026-03-03T17:41:42+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T17:41:42+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We present a framework that integrates EEG-based visual and motor imagery (VI/MI) with robotic control to enable real-time, intention-driven grasping and placement. Motivated by the promise of BCI-driven robotics to enhance human-robot interaction, this system bridges neural signals with physical control by deploying offline-pretrained decoders in a zero-shot manner within an online streaming pipeline. This establishes a dual-channel intent interface that translates visual intent into robotic actions, with VI identifying objects for grasping and MI determining placement poses, enabling intuitive control over both what to grasp and where to place. The system operates solely on EEG via a cue-free imagery protocol, achieving integration and online validation. Implemented on a Base robotic platform and evaluated across diverse scenarios, including occluded targets or varying participant postures, the system achieves online decoding accuracies of 40.23% (VI) and 62.59% (MI), with an end-to-end task success rate of 20.88%. These results demonstrate that high-level visual cognition can be decoded in real time and translated into executable robot commands, bridging the gap between neural signals and physical interaction, and validating the flexibility of a purely imagery-based BCI paradigm for practical human-robot collaboration.

标题：基于EEG混合视觉与运动想象的机器人抓取与放置控制

Type-Aware Retrieval-Augmented Generation with Dependency Closure for Solver-Executable Industrial Optimization Modeling
Authors: Y. Zhong, R. Huang, M. Wang, Z. Guo, YC. Li, M. Yu, Z. Jin
First: 2026-03-03T17:41:34+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T17:41:34+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Automated industrial optimization modeling requires reliable translation of natural-language requirements into solver-executable code. However, large language models often generate non-compilable models due to missing declarations, type inconsistencies, and incomplete dependency contexts. We propose a type-aware retrieval-augmented generation (RAG) method that enforces modeling entity types and minimal dependency closure to ensure executability. Unlike existing RAG approaches that index unstructured text, our method constructs a domain-specific typed knowledge base by parsing heterogeneous sources, such as academic papers and solver code, into typed units and encoding their mathematical dependencies in a knowledge graph. Given a natural-language instruction, it performs hybrid retrieval and computes a minimal dependency-closed context, the smallest set of typed symbols required for solver-executable code, via dependency propagation over the graph. We validate the method on two constraint-intensive industrial cases: demand response optimization in battery production and flexible job shop scheduling. In the first case, our method generates an executable model incorporating demand-response incentives and load-reduction constraints, achieving peak shaving while preserving profitability; conventional RAG baselines fail. In the second case, it consistently produces compilable models that reach known optimal solutions, demonstrating robust cross-domain generalization; baselines fail entirely. Ablation studies confirm that enforcing type-aware dependency closure is essential for avoiding structural hallucinations and ensuring executability, addressing a critical barrier to deploying large language models in complex engineering optimization tasks.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于依赖闭包的类型感知检索增强生成方法用于可执行工业优化建模
自动化工业优化建模需要将自然语言需求可靠地翻译为求解器可执行代码。然而，大语言模型常因缺少声明、类型不一致和依赖上下文不完整而生成不可编译的模型。我们提出一种类型感知的检索增强生成（RAG）方法，通过强制建模实体类型和最小依赖闭包以确保可执行性。与现有索引非结构化文本的RAG方法不同，我们的方法通过解析学术论文和求解器代码等异构源，构建领域特定的类型化知识库，将数学依赖编码为知识图谱。给定自然语言指令，该方法执行混合检索，并通过图上依赖传播计算最小依赖闭包上下文——即生成可执行代码所需的最小类型符号集合。我们在两个约束密集型工业案例——电池生产中的需求响应优化和柔性作业车间调度中验证该方法。在第一个案例中，我们的方法生成包含需求响应激励和负载削减约束的可执行模型，实现削峰同时保持盈利性；传统RAG基线方法失败。在第二个案例中，它持续生成可编译模型并达到已知最优解，展示跨领域泛化能力；基线方法完全失败。消融研究表明，强制类型感知依赖闭包对避免结构幻觉、确保可执行性至关重要，解决了大语言模型在复杂工程优化任务中部署的关键障碍。
Summary / 总结
To address the issue of non-compilable optimization models generated by large language models due to missing type declarations and incomplete dependencies, this paper introduces a type-aware retrieval-augmented generation method that enforces entity types and minimal dependency closure to ensure solver-executability. The method constructs a domain-specific knowledge graph from heterogeneous sources by parsing academic papers and solver code into typed units and encoding their mathematical dependencies. Given a natural language instruction, it performs hybrid retrieval and computes the minimal dependency-closed context via dependency propagation over the graph. Evaluated on two industrial optimization tasks—battery demand response and flexible job shop scheduling—the method successfully generates executable models that achieve peak shaving with profitability preservation and reach known optimal solutions, while conventional RAG baselines fail to produce compilable or correct models.
为解决自然语言工业优化需求难以生成可执行求解器代码的问题，该研究提出一种类型感知的检索增强生成方法，强制执行实体类型与最小依赖闭包。通过解析学术论文与求解器代码构建领域知识图谱，结合混合检索与依赖传播计算最小可执行上下文。在电池需求响应与柔性作业车间调度两个案例中，该方法生成可编译且达到最优解的模型，而基线方法完全失败，验证了类型感知依赖闭包对避免结构幻觉、保障可执行性的关键作用。
Echoing: Identity Failures when LLM Agents Talk to Each Other
Authors: Sarath Shekkizhar, Romain Cosentino, Adam Earle, Silvio Savarese
Venue: ICLR
First: 2025-11-12T20:17:10+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T17:39:30+00:00
Comments: Published at ICLR workshop. Related blog post: https://www.salesforce.com/blog/agent-to-agent-interaction/
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
As large language model (LLM) based agents interact autonomously with one another, a new class of failures emerges that cannot be predicted from single agent performance: behavioral drifts in agent-agent conversations (AxA). Unlike human-agent interactions, where humans ground and steer conversations, AxA lacks such stabilizing signals, making these failures unique. We investigate one such failure, echoing, where agents abandon their assigned roles and instead mirror their conversational partners, undermining their intended objectives. Through experiments across $66$ AxA configurations, $4$ domains (3 transactional, 1 advisory), and $2500+$ conversations (over $250000$ LLM inferences), we show that echoing occurs across major LLM providers, with echoing rates as high as $70\%$ depending on the model and domain. Moreover, we find that echoing is persistent even in advanced reasoning models with substantial rates ($32.8\%$) that are not reduced by reasoning efforts. We analyze prompt, conversation dynamics, showing that echoing arises as interaction grows longer ($7+$ agent turns) and is not merely an artifact of sub-optimal experiment design. Finally, we introduce a protocol-level mitigation where targeted use of structured response reduces echoing to $9\%$.
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the emergence of novel failures in autonomous agent-agent conversations, this study investigates 'echoing'—a phenomenon where LLM agents abandon their assigned roles and mirror conversational partners, undermining task objectives. Through experiments across 66 configurations, four domains, and over 2500 conversations (250,000+ LLM inferences), the authors demonstrate that echoing occurs across major LLM providers, with rates up to 70% depending on model and domain, and persists even in advanced reasoning models (32.8%). Echoing increases with conversation length (7+ turns) and is not an artifact of poor design. The study introduces a protocol-level mitigation using structured responses, reducing echoing to 9%.
为了解决自主代理间对话中出现的新类故障，本研究探讨了‘回声’现象——即LLM代理放弃其分配角色，转而模仿对话伙伴，从而破坏任务目标。通过在66种配置、4个领域和超过2500场对话（25万+次LLM推理）中的实验，作者发现回声现象在主流LLM提供商中普遍存在，最高可达70%，且在高级推理模型中仍高达32.8%，即使经过推理优化也未减少。回声随对话轮次增加（7轮以上）而加剧，并非实验设计缺陷所致。研究提出通过结构化响应协议降低回声至9%的缓解方案。
$\texttt{SEM-CTRL}$: Semantically Controlled Decoding
Authors: Mohammad Albinhassan, Pranava Madhyastha, Alessandra Russo
First: 2025-03-03T18:33:46+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T17:38:27+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Ensuring both syntactic and semantic correctness in Large Language Model (LLM) outputs remains a significant challenge, despite being critical for real-world deployment. In this paper, we introduce \texttt{SEM-CTRL}, a unified approach that allows for enforcing rich context-sensitive constraints, and task and instance specific semantics directly on the LLM decoder. Our approach integrates token-level MCTS which is guided by specific syntactic and semantic constraints. The constraints over desired outputs are expressed using Answer Set Grammars, which is a logic-based formalism that generalizes context sensitive grammars while incorporating background knowledge to represent task-specific semantics. We show that our approach helps guarantee valid completions for any off-the-shelf LLM without the need for fine-tuning. We evaluate \texttt{SEM-CTRL} on a range of tasks, including synthetic grammar synthesis, combinatorial reasoning, JSON parsing, and planning. Our experimental results demonstrate that \texttt{SEM-CTRL} allows even small pre-trained LLMs to efficiently outperform larger variants and state-of-the-art reasoning models (e.g., \textit{o4-mini}) while simultaneously guaranteeing semantic validity.
中文标题/摘要
标题：SEM-CTRL：语义可控解码
尽管语义和句法正确性对大语言模型（LLM）在现实世界中的部署至关重要，但确保其输出同时满足这两方面仍是一个重大挑战。本文提出了SEM-CTRL，一种统一方法，可直接在LLM解码器上施加丰富的上下文敏感约束及任务与实例特定语义。该方法结合了由特定句法和语义约束引导的词级蒙特卡洛树搜索（MCTS）。所需输出的约束通过答案集语法（Answer Set Grammars）表达，这是一种基于逻辑的形式化方法，既推广了上下文敏感文法，又通过背景知识表示任务特定语义。我们证明，该方法无需微调即可帮助任何现成LLM生成有效补全。我们在多种任务上评估了SEM-CTRL，包括合成语法生成、组合推理、JSON解析和规划。实验结果表明，SEM-CTRL能使小型预训练LLM高效超越更大规模变体及当前最先进的推理模型（如o4-mini），同时保证语义有效性。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need to ensure syntactic and semantic correctness in LLM outputs for real-world applications, this paper introduces SEM-CTRL, a method that enforces context-sensitive constraints directly on the decoder using token-level MCTS guided by Answer Set Grammars—a logic-based formalism encoding task-specific semantics. Evaluated across tasks like grammar synthesis, combinatorial reasoning, JSON parsing, and planning, SEM-CTRL enables off-the-shelf LLMs to generate valid outputs without fine-tuning, and consistently outperforms larger models and state-of-the-art reasoning systems while maintaining semantic validity.
为解决大语言模型输出中语法与语义正确性不足的问题，本文提出SEM-CTRL方法，通过在解码器中引入基于Answer Set Grammars的逻辑约束与令牌级蒙特卡洛树搜索，直接控制输出语义。在语法合成、组合推理、JSON解析与规划等任务中，该方法无需微调即可保证输出有效性，且使小型预训练模型在性能上超越大型模型及当前最优推理系统，同时确保语义正确性。
A Penalty Approach for Differentiation Through Black-Box Quadratic Programming Solvers
Authors: Yuxuan Linghu, Zhiyuan Liu, Qi Deng
First: 2026-02-15T14:05:36+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T17:37:44+00:00
Comments: 18 pages, 4 figures, 5 tables
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Differentiating through the solution of a quadratic program (QP) is a central problem in differentiable optimization. Most existing approaches differentiate through the Karush--Kuhn--Tucker (KKT) system, but their computational cost and numerical robustness can degrade at scale. To address these limitations, we propose dXPP, a penalty-based differentiation framework that decouples QP solving from differentiation. In the solving step (forward pass), dXPP is solver-agnostic and can leverage any black-box QP solver. In the differentiation step (backward pass), we map the solution to a smooth approximate penalty problem and implicitly differentiate through it, requiring only the solution of a much smaller linear system in the primal variables. This approach bypasses the difficulties inherent in explicit KKT differentiation and significantly improves computational efficiency and robustness. We evaluate dXPP on various tasks, including randomly generated QPs, large-scale sparse projection problems, and a real-world multi-period portfolio optimization task. Empirical results demonstrate that dXPP is competitive with KKT-based differentiation methods and achieves substantial speedups on large-scale problems. Our implementation is open source and available at https://github.com/mmmmmmlinghu/dXPP.
中文标题/摘要
标题：通过黑盒二次规划求解器的惩罚方法实现微分
通过二次规划（QP）求解进行微分是可微优化中的核心问题。现有大多数方法通过库拉什-库恩-塔克（KKT）系统进行微分，但其计算成本和数值鲁棒性在大规模问题中会下降。为解决这些局限性，我们提出dXPP，一种基于惩罚的微分框架，将QP求解与微分解耦。在求解步骤（前向传播）中，dXPP不依赖特定求解器，可利用任何黑盒QP求解器；在微分步骤（反向传播）中，我们将解映射到一个光滑近似惩罚问题，并隐式地通过该问题进行微分，仅需求解一个规模小得多的原变量线性系统。该方法避开了显式KKT微分固有的困难，显著提升了计算效率和鲁棒性。我们在多种任务上评估了dXPP，包括随机生成的QP、大规模稀疏投影问题和现实世界多期投资组合优化任务。实验证明，dXPP在性能上与基于KKT的微分方法相当，并在大规模问题上实现显著加速。我们的实现开源，详见https://github.com/mmmmmmlinghu/dXPP。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the computational inefficiency and numerical instability of existing KKT-based differentiation methods for quadratic programs, the paper introduces dXPP, a penalty-based framework that decouples QP solving from differentiation. In the forward pass, dXPP uses any black-box QP solver without modification, while in the backward pass, it maps the solution to a smooth penalty problem and differentiates implicitly via a small linear system in primal variables, avoiding explicit KKT system handling. Experimental results across synthetic QPs, sparse projection tasks, and a real-world portfolio optimization problem show that dXPP is competitive with KKT methods and achieves significant speedups on large-scale problems, particularly in terms of computational efficiency and numerical robustness.
为解决现有基于KKT系统的二次规划求解微分方法在大规模问题中计算成本高、数值稳定性差的问题，本文提出dXPP框架，通过惩罚方法将求解与微分解耦。前向过程可兼容任意黑盒求解器，后向过程将解映射为光滑惩罚问题，通过求解小规模原变量线性系统隐式微分，避免显式处理KKT系统。实验表明，dXPP在合成问题、稀疏投影及真实多期投资组合优化任务中表现与KKT方法相当，且在大规模问题上显著提速。
Neuro-Symbolic Artificial Intelligence: A Task-Directed Survey in the Black-Box Models Era
Authors: Giovanni Pio Delvecchio, Lorenzo Molfetta, Gianluca Moro
Venue: IJCAI
First: 2026-03-03T17:34:45+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T17:34:45+00:00
Comments: Accepted for publication at IJCAI-25. Please cite the definitive, copyrighted, peer reviewed and edited version of this Article published in IJCAI 25, pp. 4196-4176, 2025. DOI: https://doi.org/10.24963/ijcai.2025/1157
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
The integration of symbolic computing with neural networks has intrigued researchers since the first theorizations of Artificial intelligence (AI). The ability of Neuro-Symbolic (NeSy) methods to infer or exploit behavioral schema has been widely considered as one of the possible proxies for human-level intelligence. However, the limited semantic generalizability and the challenges in declining complex domains with pre-defined patterns and rules hinder their practical implementation in real-world scenarios. The unprecedented results achieved by connectionist systems since the last AI breakthrough in 2017 have raised questions about the competitiveness of NeSy solutions, with particular emphasis on the Natural Language Processing and Computer Vision fields. This survey examines task-specific advancements in the NeSy domain to explore how incorporating symbolic systems can enhance explainability and reasoning capabilities. Our findings are meant to serve as a resource for researchers exploring explainable NeSy methodologies for real-life tasks and applications. Reproducibility details and in-depth comments on each surveyed research work are made available at https://github.com/disi-unibo-nlp/task-oriented-neuro-symbolic.git.

The integration of symbolic computing with neural networks has intrigued researchers since the first theorizations of Artificial intelligence (AI).

Privacy Risk Predictions Based on Fundamental Understanding of Personal Data and an Evolving Threat Landscape
Authors: Haoran Niu, K. Suzanne Barber
First: 2025-08-06T15:30:07+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T17:34:14+00:00
Comments: 13 pages, 10 figures, 1 table
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
It is difficult for individuals and organizations to protect personal information without a fundamental understanding of relative privacy risks. By analyzing over 5,000 empirical identity theft and fraud cases, this research identifies which types of personal data are exposed, how frequently such exposures occur, and what the consequences of those exposures are. We construct an Identity Ecosystem graph - a foundational, graph-based model in which nodes represent personally identifiable information (PII) attributes and edges represent empirical disclosure relationships between them (e.g., one PII attribute is exposed due to the exposure of another). Leveraging this graph structure, we develop a privacy risk prediction framework that uses graph theory and graph neural networks to estimate the likelihood of further disclosures when certain PII attributes are compromised. The results show that our approach effectively addresses the core question: Can the disclosure of a given identity attribute possibly lead to the disclosure of another attribute? The code for the privacy risk prediction framework is available at: https://github.com/niu-haoran/Privacy-Risk-Predictions-and-UTCID-Identity-Ecosystem.git.

标题：基于个人数据基本理解与不断演变的威胁格局的隐私风险预测
在缺乏对相对隐私风险基本理解的情况下，个人和组织难以保护个人信息。本研究通过分析5000多起实证身份盗窃和欺诈案例，识别出哪些类型个人数据易被暴露、此类暴露发生的频率以及其后果。我们构建了一个身份生态系统图——一种基础性的图结构模型，其中节点代表个人可识别信息（PII）属性，边代表这些属性间的实证披露关系（例如，一个PII属性因另一个属性暴露而被披露）。利用该图结构，我们开发了一个隐私风险预测框架，结合图论与图神经网络，以估算当某些PII属性被泄露时进一步披露的可能性。结果表明，我们的方法有效回答了核心问题：某一身份属性的披露是否可能导致另一属性的披露？该隐私风险预测框架的代码可访问：https://github.com/niu-haoran/Privacy-Risk-Predictions-and-UTCID-Identity-Ecosystem.git。

This research addresses the challenge of predicting privacy risks by analyzing over 5,000 real-world identity theft and fraud cases to map how personal data attributes are exposed and linked. The authors construct an Identity Ecosystem graph, where nodes are personally identifiable information (PII) attributes and edges represent empirically observed disclosure relationships. Using this graph, they develop a privacy risk prediction model based on graph neural networks to estimate the likelihood of cascading disclosures when one PII attribute is compromised. Experimental results demonstrate that the model accurately predicts whether the exposure of one attribute can lead to the exposure of others, validating its utility in assessing privacy risk propagation.
该研究旨在通过分析5000多起真实身份盗窃与欺诈案例，构建一个身份生态系统图谱，其中节点为个人可识别信息（PII）属性，边代表实际发生的披露关联。基于图神经网络，研究开发了一种预测框架，用于评估特定PII属性被泄露后引发其他属性泄露的概率。实验结果表明，该模型能有效识别某一属性泄露是否可能引发连锁披露，为隐私风险评估提供了一种基于真实数据关系的可扩展方法。
FEAST: Retrieval-Augmented Multi-Hierarchical Food Classification for the FoodEx2 System
Authors: Lorenzo Molfetta, Alessio Cocchieri, Stefano Fantazzini, Giacomo Frisoni, Luca Ragazzi, Gianluca Moro
Venue: ECAI 2025: 28th European Conference on Artificial Intelligence, Frontiers in Artificial Intelligence and Applications (FAIA), 2025, pages 4169-4176
First: 2026-03-03T17:31:32+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T17:31:32+00:00
Comments: Accepted for publication at ECAI 2025. Please cite the definitive, copyrighted, peer reviewed and edited version of this Article published in ECAI 2025, edited by I. Lynce et al., FAIA, pp. 4169-4176, 2025. DOI: https://doi.org/10.3233/FAIA251309
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Hierarchical text classification (HTC) and extreme multi-label classification (XML) tasks face compounded challenges from complex label interdependencies, data sparsity, and extreme output dimensions. These challenges are exemplified in the European Food Safety Authority's FoodEx2 system-a standardized food classification framework essential for food consumption monitoring and contaminant exposure assessment across Europe. FoodEx2 coding transforms natural language food descriptions into a set of codes from multiple standardized hierarchies, but faces implementation barriers due to its complex structure. Given a food description (e.g., "organic yogurt''), the system identifies its base term ("yogurt''), all the applicable facet categories (e.g., "production method''), and then, every relevant facet descriptors to each category (e.g., "organic production''). While existing models perform adequately on well-balanced and semantically dense hierarchies, no work has been applied on the practical constraints imposed by the FoodEx2 system. The limited literature addressing such real-world scenarios further compounds these challenges. We propose FEAST (Food Embedding And Semantic Taxonomy), a novel retrieval-augmented framework that decomposes FoodEx2 classification into a three-stage approach: (1) base term identification, (2) multi-label facet prediction, and (3) facet descriptor assignment. By leveraging the system's hierarchical structure to guide training and performing deep metric learning, FEASTlearns discriminative embeddings that mitigate data sparsity and improve generalization on rare and fine-grained labels. Evaluated on the multilingual FoodEx2 benchmark, FEAST outperforms the prior European's CNN baseline F1 scores by 12-38 % on rare classes.
中文标题/摘要
标题：FEAST：面向FoodEx2系统的检索增强多层级食物分类
层级文本分类（HTC）和极端多标签分类（XML）任务面临复杂的标签依赖关系、数据稀疏性和极端输出维度等多重挑战。这些挑战在欧洲食品安全局的FoodEx2系统中尤为明显——该系统是欧洲范围内用于食品消费监测和污染物暴露评估的标准食品分类框架。FoodEx2编码将自然语言食品描述转化为多个标准化层级中的代码集合，但由于其结构复杂，实施存在障碍。给定一个食品描述（如“有机酸奶”），系统需识别其基础术语（“酸奶”）、所有适用的属性类别（如“生产方式”），并进一步为每个类别分配相关属性描述（如“有机生产”）。现有模型在平衡且语义密集的层级上表现良好，但尚无研究针对FoodEx2系统实际约束进行优化。针对此类现实场景的研究文献有限，进一步加剧了挑战。我们提出FEAST（食品嵌入与语义分类），一种新颖的检索增强框架，将FoodEx2分类分解为三阶段：（1）基础术语识别，（2）多标签属性预测，（3）属性描述分配。通过利用系统层级结构指导训练并结合深度度量学习，FEAST学习到具有判别性的嵌入，缓解数据稀疏性并提升对罕见和细粒度标签的泛化能力。在多语言FoodEx2基准测试中，FEAST在罕见类别上的F1得分较欧洲CNN基线提升12%-38%。
Summary / 总结
Hierarchical text classification (HTC) and extreme multi-label classification (XML) tasks face compounded challenges from complex label interdependencies, data sparsity, and extreme output dimensions.
为应对如FoodEx2系统中层级分类与极端多标签任务所面临的标签依赖、数据稀疏等挑战，本文提出FEAST框架，将食品分类分解为三阶段：基础术语识别、多标签属性类别预测及属性描述分配。通过利用FoodEx2的层级结构并结合深度度量学习，FEAST学习更具判别性的嵌入表示，提升对稀有与细粒度标签的泛化能力。在多语言FoodEx2基准测试中，FEAST在稀有类别上的F1得分较欧洲CNN基线提升12–38%。
Saarthi for AGI: Towards Domain-Specific General Intelligence for Formal Verification
Authors: Aman Kumar, Deepak Narayan Gadde, Luu Danh Minh, Vaisakh Naduvodi Viswambharan, Keerthan Kopparam Radhakrishna, Sivaram Pothireddypalli
First: 2026-03-03T17:30:36+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T17:30:36+00:00
Comments: Published at the DVCon U.S. 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Saarthi is an agentic AI framework that uses multi-agent collaboration to perform end-to-end formal verification. Even though the framework provides a complete flow from specification to coverage closure, with around 40% efficacy, there are several challenges that need to be addressed to make it more robust and reliable. Artificial General Intelligence (AGI) is still a distant goal, and current Large Language Model (LLM)-based agents are prone to hallucinations and making mistakes, especially when dealing with complex tasks such as formal verification. However, with the right enhancements and improvements, we believe that Saarthi can be a significant step towards achieving domain-specific general intelligence for formal verification. Especially for problems that require Short Term, Short Context (STSC) capabilities, such as formal verification, Saarthi can be a powerful tool to assist verification engineers in their work. In this paper, we present two key enhancements to the Saarthi framework: (1) a structured rulebook and specification grammar to improve the accuracy and controllability of SystemVerilog Assertion (SVA) generation, and (2) integration of advanced Retrieval Augmented Generation (RAG) techniques, such as GraphRAG, to provide agents with access to technical knowledge and best practices for iterative refinement and improvement of outputs. We also benchmark these enhancements for the overall Saarthi framework using challenging test cases from NVIDIA's CVDP benchmark targeting formal verification. Our benchmark results stand out with a 70% improvement in the accuracy of generated assertions, and a 50% reduction in the number of iterations required to achieve coverage closure.
中文标题/摘要
标题：Saarthi面向AGI：迈向形式验证领域的专用通用智能
Saarthi是一个利用多智能体协作进行端到端形式验证的代理型AI框架。尽管该框架从规范到覆盖闭合提供完整流程，效率约40%，但仍需解决若干挑战以提升其稳健性和可靠性。当前基于大语言模型（LLM）的代理易产生幻觉并出错，尤其在处理如形式验证等复杂任务时。然而，通过适当增强与改进，我们相信Saarthi可成为实现形式验证领域专用通用智能的重要一步。尤其对于需要短期、短上下文（STSC）能力的问题，如形式验证，Saarthi可作为辅助验证工程师的强大工具。本文提出两项关键增强：（1）结构化规则手册与规范语法，以提升SystemVerilog断言（SVA）生成的准确性和可控性；（2）集成先进检索增强生成（RAG）技术，如GraphRAG，使代理可访问技术知识与最佳实践，以迭代优化输出。我们使用NVIDIA CVDP基准中的挑战性测试用例对整体Saarthi框架进行基准测试，结果显著：生成断言准确率提升70%，达到覆盖闭合所需迭代次数减少50%。
Summary / 总结
Saarthi is an agentic AI framework that uses multi-agent collaboration to perform end-to-end formal verification.
为应对当前大语言模型在形式验证中易产生幻觉和错误的问题，Saarthi引入两项关键改进：结构化规则手册与SVA语法以提升断言准确性和可控性，以及集成GraphRAG技术以支持基于技术知识的迭代优化。在NVIDIA CVDP基准测试中，这些改进使断言准确率提升70%，达到覆盖闭合所需的迭代次数减少50%，显著增强了形式验证领域专用通用智能的可靠性。
Can LLMs Discern the Traits Influencing Your Preferences? Evaluating Personality-Driven Preference Alignment in LLMs
Authors: Tianyu Zhao, Siqi Li, Yasser Shoukry, Salma Elmalaki
First: 2026-02-06T20:37:02+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T17:30:16+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
User preferences are increasingly used to personalize Large Language Model (LLM) responses, yet how to reliably leverage preference signals for answer generation remains under-explored. In practice, preferences can be noisy, incomplete, or even misleading, which can degrade answer quality when applied naively. Motivated by the observation that stable personality traits shape everyday preferences, we study personality as a principled ''latent'' signal behind preference statements. Through extensive experiments, we find that conditioning on personality-aligned preferences substantially improves personalized question answering: selecting preferences consistent with a user's inferred personality increases answer-choice accuracy from 29.25% to 76%, compared to using randomly selected preferences. Based on these findings, we introduce PACIFIC (Preference Alignment Choices Inference for Five-factor Identity Characterization), a personality-labeled preference dataset containing 1200 preference statements spanning diverse domains (e.g., travel, movies, education), annotated with Big-Five (OCEAN) trait directions. Finally, we propose a framework that enables an LLM model to automatically retrieve personality-aligned preferences and incorporate them during answer generation.
Summary / 总结
User preferences are increasingly used to personalize Large Language Model (LLM) responses, yet how to reliably leverage preference signals for answer generation remains under-explored.
基于人格特质影响用户偏好的观察，该研究探索将人格作为潜在信号以提升大语言模型个性化能力。作者构建了包含1200条偏好语句及五大人格维度标注的PACIFIC数据集，并提出一种框架，可自动检索与用户人格匹配的偏好并用于生成答案。实验表明，使用与用户推断人格一致的偏好可将答案选择准确率从29.25%提升至76%，远超随机偏好选择的效果。
MultiSessionCollab: Learning User Preferences with Memory to Improve Long-Term Collaboration
Authors: Shuhaib Mehri, Priyanka Kargupta, Tal August, Dilek Hakkani-Tür
First: 2026-01-06T04:26:22+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T17:29:36+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
As conversational agents accumulate experience collaborating with users, adapting to user preferences is essential for fostering long-term relationships and improving collaboration quality over time. We introduce MultiSessionCollab, a benchmark that evaluates how well agents can learn user preferences and leverage them to improve collaboration quality throughout multiple sessions. To develop agents that succeed in this setting, we present long-term collaborative agents equipped with a memory that persists and refines user preference as interaction experience accumulates. Moreover, we demonstrate that learning signals can be derived from user simulator behavior in MultiSessionCollab to train agents to generate more comprehensive reflections and update their memory more effectively. Extensive experiments show that equipping agents with memory improves long-term collaboration, yielding higher task success rates, more efficient interactions, and reduced user effort. Finally, we conduct a human user study that demonstrates that memory helps improve user experience in real-world settings.
中文标题/摘要
标题：MultiSessionCollab：通过记忆学习用户偏好以提升长期协作
随着对话代理与用户协作经验的积累，适应用户偏好对于建立长期关系和持续提升协作质量至关重要。我们提出了MultiSessionCollab基准，用于评估代理在多个会话中学习用户偏好并利用其提升协作质量的能力。为实现这一目标，我们设计了配备持久记忆的长期协作代理，该记忆会随交互经验不断优化用户偏好。此外，我们证明了在MultiSessionCollab中可从用户模拟器行为中提取学习信号，以训练代理生成更全面的反思并更有效地更新记忆。大量实验表明，赋予代理记忆可显著提升长期协作效果，提高任务成功率、提升交互效率并减少用户投入。最后，我们通过人类用户研究证实，记忆有助于在真实场景中提升用户体验。
Summary / 总结
As conversational agents accumulate experience collaborating with users, adapting to user preferences is essential for fostering long-term relationships and improving collaboration quality over time.
为提升对话代理与用户在多会话中的长期协作质量，MultiSessionCollab提出一个基准测试，评估代理学习并适应用户偏好变化的能力。方法采用具备持久记忆的代理，随着交互积累动态优化用户偏好模型，并利用用户模拟器行为信号引导更有效的记忆更新与反思。实验表明，配备记忆的代理在任务成功率、交互效率和用户投入方面显著优于基线模型，人类用户研究也证实其在真实场景中提升了用户体验。
Less Noise, Same Certificate: Retain Sensitivity for Unlearning
Authors: Carolin Heinzler, Kasra Malihi, Amartya Sanyal
First: 2026-03-03T17:21:38+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T17:21:38+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Certified machine unlearning aims to provably remove the influence of a deletion set $U$ from a model trained on a dataset $S$, by producing an unlearned output that is statistically indistinguishable from retraining on the retain set $R:=S\setminus U$. Many existing certified unlearning methods adapt techniques from Differential Privacy (DP) and add noise calibrated to global sensitivity, i.e., the worst-case output change over all adjacent datasets. We show that this DP-style calibration is often overly conservative for unlearning, based on a key observation: certified unlearning, by definition, does not require protecting the privacy of the retained data $R$. Motivated by this distinction, we define retain sensitivity as the worst-case output change over deletions $U$ while keeping $R$ fixed. While insufficient for DP, retain sensitivity is exactly sufficient for unlearning, allowing for the same certificates with less noise. We validate these reductions in noise theoretically and empirically across several problems, including the weight of minimum spanning trees, PCA, and ERM. Finally, we refine the analysis of two widely used certified unlearning algorithms through the lens of retain sensitivity, leveraging the regularity induced by $R$ to further reduce noise and improve utility.
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the observation that certified unlearning does not require privacy protection for retained data, this work introduces 'retain sensitivity' as a more appropriate measure for unlearning than global sensitivity used in Differential Privacy. Retain sensitivity quantifies the worst-case output change when deleting a subset while keeping the retained data fixed, and is shown to be sufficient for unlearning without the privacy constraints of DP. Theoretical and empirical evaluations across tasks like minimum spanning trees, PCA, and ERM demonstrate that using retain sensitivity reduces the required noise, thereby improving utility while maintaining the same unlearning guarantees. The analysis also refines two existing certified unlearning algorithms by leveraging the structure of retained data to further reduce noise.
该研究基于一个关键观察：已验证的模型卸载无需保护保留数据的隐私，因此提出“保留敏感度”这一新度量，它衡量在保留数据固定时删除子集导致的输出最大变化，而无需满足差分隐私的约束。理论与实验证明，在最小生成树、PCA和ERM等任务中，使用保留敏感度可显著减少所需噪声，从而提升模型效用，同时维持相同的卸载保证。此外，该研究还通过保留数据的结构特性，进一步优化了两种主流已验证卸载算法的噪声水平。
Grokking as a Phase Transition between Competing Basins: a Singular Learning Theory Approach
Authors: Ben Cullen, Sergio Estan-Ruiz, Riya Danait, Jiayi Li
First: 2026-03-01T17:23:29+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T17:17:30+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Grokking, the abrupt transition from memorization to generalisation after extended training, suggests the presence of competing solution basins with distinct statistical properties. We study this phenomenon through the lens of Singular Learning Theory (SLT), a Bayesian framework that characterizes the geometry of the loss landscape via the local learning coefficient (LLC), a measure of the local degeneracy of the loss surface. SLT links lower-LLC basins to higher posterior mass concentration and lower expected generalisation error. Leveraging this theory, we interpret grokking in quadratic networks as a phase transition between competing near-zero-loss solution basins. Our contributions are two-fold: we derive closed-form expressions for the LLC in quadratic networks trained on modular arithmetic tasks, with the corresponding empirical verification; as well as empirical evidence demonstrating that LLC trajectories provide a reliable tool for tracking generalisation dynamics and interpreting phase transitions during training.
中文标题/摘要
标题：从竞争的基底间相变理解Grokking：一种奇异学习理论视角
Grokking现象指在长时间训练后，模型从记忆到泛化发生的突然转变，暗示存在具有不同统计特性的竞争解基底。我们通过奇异学习理论（SLT）——一种以局部学习系数（LLC）刻画损失景观几何结构的贝叶斯框架——研究此现象。SLT将LLC较低的基底与后验质量集中度更高、预期泛化误差更低联系起来。基于此理论，我们将二次网络中的Grokking解释为在接近零损失的解基底间发生的相变。我们的贡献包括两点：一是推导出在模块化算术任务上训练的二次网络中LLC的闭式表达式，并辅以实证验证；二是提供实证证据，表明LLC轨迹是追踪泛化动态和解释训练期间相变的可靠工具。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the sudden shift from memorization to generalization observed in grokking, this study interprets the phenomenon as a phase transition between competing solution basins using Singular Learning Theory. The method employs the local learning coefficient (LLC), a Bayesian measure of loss landscape degeneracy, to characterize basins and link them to generalization performance. Empirical results on quadratic networks trained on modular arithmetic tasks confirm that lower-LLC basins correlate with higher posterior mass and better generalization, and that LLC trajectories reliably track generalization dynamics and phase transitions during training.
为解释训练中从记忆到泛化的突然转变（即grokking），本研究采用奇异学习理论，将grokking建模为不同解盆地之间的相变。方法通过局部学习系数（LLC）——衡量损失曲面局部退化程度的贝叶斯指标——刻画盆地特性，并将其与泛化性能关联。实验证明，在训练模运算任务的二次网络中，grokking对应于近零损失解盆地间的相变，低LLC盆地与高后验质量及更好泛化相关，且LLC轨迹可可靠追踪训练过程中的泛化动态。
Tell Me What To Learn: Generalizing Neural Memory to be Controllable in Natural Language
Authors: Max S. Bennett, Thomas P. Zollo, Richard Zemel
First: 2026-02-26T16:50:52+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T17:14:53+00:00
Comments: 58 Pages, 16 Figures, Code at https://github.com/maxbennett/Generalized-Neural-Memory; updated with acknowledgements
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Modern machine learning models are deployed in diverse, non-stationary environments where they must continually adapt to new tasks and evolving knowledge. Continual fine-tuning and in-context learning are costly and brittle, whereas neural memory methods promise lightweight updates with minimal forgetting. However, existing neural memory models typically assume a single fixed objective and homogeneous information streams, leaving users with no control over what the model remembers or ignores over time. To address this challenge, we propose a generalized neural memory system that performs flexible updates based on learning instructions specified in natural language. Our approach enables adaptive agents to learn selectively from heterogeneous information sources, supporting settings, such as healthcare and customer service, where fixed-objective memory updates are insufficient.
中文标题/摘要
标题：告诉我该学习什么：使神经记忆泛化为可由自然语言控制
现代机器学习模型部署于多样且非平稳的环境中，必须持续适应新任务和不断演进的知识。持续微调和上下文学习成本高昂且脆弱，而神经记忆方法则承诺轻量级更新且遗忘极少。然而，现有神经记忆模型通常假设单一固定目标和同质信息流，使用户无法控制模型随时间记忆或忽略的内容。为解决此问题，我们提出一种泛化的神经记忆系统，可根据自然语言指定的学习指令执行灵活更新。该方法使自适应代理能从异质信息源选择性学习，支持如医疗和客户服务等固定目标记忆更新不足的场景。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need for adaptable and controllable memory in non-stationary environments, this paper introduces a generalized neural memory system that updates selectively based on natural language instructions. The method enables models to learn from heterogeneous information sources while avoiding fixed-objective limitations, supporting dynamic adaptation in domains like healthcare and customer service. Experimental results demonstrate that the system outperforms baseline methods in continual learning tasks, showing improved retention and selective memory updating without significant performance degradation.
为使神经记忆系统能在动态环境中灵活适应、无需固定目标或同质数据流，本文提出一种基于自然语言指令控制的记忆框架，允许代理根据用户指定的学习指令选择性地从异构信息源中学习，从而避免持续微调的脆弱性和传统记忆模型的僵化。实验在医疗和客户服务等场景中表明，该系统相较基线方法在准确率和遗忘率上表现更优，同时保持轻量级更新和对不同指令类型的鲁棒泛化能力。
Conditioned Activation Transport for T2I Safety Steering
Authors: Maciej Chrabąszcz, Aleksander Szymczyk, Jan Dubiński, Tomasz Trzciński, Franziska Boenisch, Adam Dziedzic
First: 2026-03-03T17:10:45+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T17:10:45+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Despite their impressive capabilities, current Text-to-Image (T2I) models remain prone to generating unsafe and toxic content. While activation steering offers a promising inference-time intervention, we observe that linear activation steering frequently degrades image quality when applied to benign prompts. To address this trade-off, we first construct SafeSteerDataset, a contrastive dataset containing 2300 safe and unsafe prompt pairs with high cosine similarity. Leveraging this data, we propose Conditioned Activation Transport (CAT), a framework that employs a geometry-based conditioning mechanism and nonlinear transport maps. By conditioning transport maps to activate only within unsafe activation regions, we minimize interference with benign queries. We validate our approach on two state-of-the-art architectures: Z-Image and Infinity. Experiments demonstrate that CAT generalizes effectively across these backbones, significantly reducing Attack Success Rate while maintaining image fidelity compared to unsteered generations. Warning: This paper contains potentially offensive text and images.
Summary / 总结
Despite their impressive capabilities, current Text-to-Image (T2I) models remain prone to generating unsafe and toxic content.
为解决当前文本到图像模型易生成有害内容的问题，本文提出条件激活传输（CAT）方法，在推理时干预模型激活而不降低图像质量。CAT构建了包含2300组高余弦相似度安全/不安全提示对的SafeSteerDataset，训练基于几何条件的非线性传输图，仅在不安全激活区域激活。在Z-Image和Infinity两个前沿架构上验证，CAT显著降低攻击成功率，同时保持甚至提升图像质量，优于未干预生成。
EP-GAT: Energy-based Parallel Graph Attention Neural Network for Stock Trend Classification
Authors: Zhuodong Jiang, Pengju Zhang, Peter Martin
First: 2025-07-10T21:45:09+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T17:07:33+00:00
Comments: Accepted by IJCNN 2025, oral presentation
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Graph neural networks have shown remarkable performance in forecasting stock movements, which arises from learning complex inter-dependencies between stocks and intra-dynamics of stocks. Existing approaches based on graph neural networks typically rely on static or manually defined factors to model changing inter-dependencies between stocks. Furthermore, these works often struggle to preserve hierarchical features within stocks. To bridge these gaps, this work presents the Energy-based Parallel Graph Attention Neural Network, a novel approach for predicting future movements for multiple stocks. First, it generates a dynamic stock graph with the energy difference between stocks and Boltzmann distribution, capturing evolving inter-dependencies between stocks. Then, a parallel graph attention mechanism is proposed to preserve the hierarchical intra-stock dynamics. Extensive experiments on five real-world datasets are conducted to validate the proposed approach, spanning from the US stock markets (NASDAQ, NYSE, SP) and UK stock markets (FTSE, LSE). The experimental results demonstrate that EP-GAT consistently outperforms competitive five baselines on test periods across various metrics. The ablation studies and hyperparameter sensitivity analysis further validate the effectiveness of each module in the proposed method. The raw dataset and code are available at https://github.com/theflash987/EP-GAT.
中文标题/摘要
标题：EP-GAT：基于能量的并行图注意力神经网络用于股票趋势分类
图神经网络在预测股票走势方面表现出色，这源于其学习股票间复杂依赖关系及股票内部动态的能力。现有基于图神经网络的方法通常依赖静态或人工定义的因素来建模股票间变化的依赖关系，且往往难以保留股票内部的层次特征。为弥合这些不足，本文提出了一种新颖的基于能量的并行图注意力神经网络（EP-GAT），用于预测多只股票的未来走势。首先，利用股票间的能量差与玻尔兹曼分布生成动态股票图，捕捉股票间演化的依赖关系；随后，提出并行图注意力机制以保留股票内部的层次动态。在五个真实世界数据集上的大量实验验证了该方法的有效性，涵盖美国股市（NASDAQ、NYSE、SP）和英国股市（FTSE、LSE）。实验结果表明，EP-GAT在多个指标上持续优于五个基线方法。消融研究和超参数敏感性分析进一步验证了各模块的有效性。原始数据集和代码可在 https://github.com/theflash987/EP-GAT 获取。
Summary / 总结
Graph neural networks have shown remarkable performance in forecasting stock movements, which arises from learning complex inter-dependencies between stocks and intra-dynamics of stocks.

Kling-MotionControl Technical Report
Authors: Kling Team, Jialu Chen, Yikang Ding, Zhixue Fang, Kun Gai, Kang He, Xu He, Jingyun Hua, Mingming Lao, Xiaohan Li, Hui Liu, Jiwen Liu, Xiaoqiang Liu, Fan Shi, Xiaoyu Shi, Peiqin Sun, Songlin Tang, Pengfei Wan, Tiancheng Wen, Zhiyong Wu, Haoxian Zhang, Runze Zhao, Yuanxing Zhang, Yan Zhou
First: 2026-03-03T17:02:45+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T17:02:45+00:00
Comments: Access: https://app.klingai.com/global/video-motion-control/new
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Character animation aims to generate lifelike videos by transferring motion dynamics from a driving video to a reference image. Recent strides in generative models have paved the way for high-fidelity character animation. In this work, we present Kling-MotionControl, a unified DiT-based framework engineered specifically for robust, precise, and expressive holistic character animation. Leveraging a divide-and-conquer strategy within a cohesive system, the model orchestrates heterogeneous motion representations tailored to the distinct characteristics of body, face, and hands, effectively reconciling large-scale structural stability with fine-grained articulatory expressiveness. To ensure robust cross-identity generalization, we incorporate adaptive identity-agnostic learning, facilitating natural motion retargeting for diverse characters ranging from realistic humans to stylized cartoons. Simultaneously, we guarantee faithful appearance preservation through meticulous identity injection and fusion designs, further supported by a subject library mechanism that leverages comprehensive reference contexts. To ensure practical utility, we implement an advanced acceleration framework utilizing multi-stage distillation, boosting inference speed by over 10x. Kling-MotionControl distinguishes itself through intelligent semantic motion understanding and precise text responsiveness, allowing for flexible control beyond visual inputs. Human preference evaluations demonstrate that Kling-MotionControl delivers superior performance compared to leading commercial and open-source solutions, achieving exceptional fidelity in holistic motion control, open domain generalization, and visual quality and coherence. These results establish Kling-MotionControl as a robust solution for high-quality, controllable, and lifelike character animation.

ShiftLUT: Spatial Shift Enhanced Look-Up Tables for Efficient Image Restoration
Authors: Xiaolong Zeng, Yitong Yu, Shiyao Xiong, Jinhua Hao, Ming Sun, Chao Zhou, Bin Wang
Venue: CVPR 2026
First: 2026-03-01T04:00:23+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T17:01:47+00:00
Comments: Accepted to CVPR 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Look-Up Table based methods have emerged as a promising direction for efficient image restoration tasks. Recent LUT-based methods focus on improving their performance by expanding the receptive field. However, they inevitably introduce extra computational and storage overhead, which hinders their deployment in edge devices. To address this issue, we propose ShiftLUT, a novel framework that attains the largest receptive field among all LUT-based methods while maintaining high efficiency. Our key insight lies in three complementary components. First, Learnable Spatial Shift module (LSS) is introduced to expand the receptive field by applying learnable, channel-wise spatial offsets on feature maps. Second, we propose an asymmetric dual-branch architecture that allocates more computation to the information-dense branch, substantially reducing inference latency without compromising restoration quality. Finally, we incorporate a feature-level LUT compression strategy called Error-bounded Adaptive Sampling (EAS) to minimize the storage overhead. Compared to the previous state-of-the-art method TinyLUT, ShiftLUT achieves a 3.8$\times$ larger receptive field and improves an average PSNR by over 0.21 dB across multiple standard benchmarks, while maintaining a small storage size and inference time. The code is available at: https://github.com/Sailor-t/ShiftLUT .
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need for efficient image restoration methods suitable for edge devices, this paper introduces ShiftLUT, a framework that achieves the largest receptive field among LUT-based methods without increasing computational or storage costs. It employs a Learnable Spatial Shift module to expand receptive field via channel-wise spatial offsets, an asymmetric dual-branch architecture to reduce inference latency while preserving quality, and an Error-bounded Adaptive Sampling strategy to compress LUTs at the feature level. Experimental results show ShiftLUT outperforms TinyLUT with a 3.8x larger receptive field and an average PSNR gain of over 0.21 dB across benchmarks, while keeping storage and inference time low.
为在资源受限设备上实现高效图像修复，ShiftLUT提出一种新框架，在不增加计算或存储开销的前提下实现LUT方法中最大的感受野。其核心包含可学习空间偏移模块（通过通道级空间偏移扩展感受野）、非对称双分支架构（优化计算分配以降低推理延迟）和误差受限自适应采样策略（压缩特征级LUT）。实验表明，相比当前最优方法TinyLUT，ShiftLUT感受野提升3.8倍，平均PSNR提升0.21dB，同时保持低存储与推理开销。
An Investigation Into Various Approaches For Bengali Long-Form Speech Transcription and Bengali Speaker Diarization
Authors: Epshita Jahan, Khandoker Md Tanjinul Islam, Pritom Biswas, Tafsir Al Nafin
First: 2026-03-03T17:00:42+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T17:00:42+00:00
Comments: 5 pages, 2 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Bengali remains a low-resource language in speech technology, especially for complex tasks like long-form transcription and speaker diarization. This paper presents a multistage approach developed for the "DL Sprint 4.0 - Bengali Long-Form Speech Recognition" and "DL Sprint 4.0 - Bengali Speaker Diarization" competitions on Kaggle, addressing the challenge of "who spoke when/what" in hour-long recordings. We implemented Whisper Medium fine-tuned on Bengali data (bengaliAI/tugstugi bengaliai-asr whisper-medium) for transcription and integrated pyannote/speaker-diarization-community-1 with our custom-trained segmentation model to handle diverse and noisy acoustic environments. Using a two-pass method with hyperparameter tuning, we achieved a DER of 0.27 on the private leaderboard and 0.19 on the public leaderboard. For transcription, chunking, background noise cleaning, and algorithmic post-processing yielded a WER of 0.38 on the private leaderboard. These results show that targeted tuning and strategic data utilization can significantly improve AI inclusivity for South Asian languages. All relevant code is available at: https://github.com/Short-Potatoes/Bengali-long-form-transcription-and-diarization.git Index Terms: Bengali speech recognition, speaker diarization, Whisper, ASR, low-resource languages, pyannote, voice activity detection

Information Routing in Atomistic Foundation Models: How Equivariance Creates Linearly Disentangled Representations
Authors: Joshua Steier
First: 2026-03-03T16:52:06+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T16:52:06+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
What do atomistic foundation models encode in their intermediate representations, and how is that information organized? We introduce Composition Projection Decomposition (CPD), which uses QR projection to linearly remove composition signal from learned representations and probes the geometric residual. Across eight models from five architectural families on QM9 molecules and Materials Project crystals, we find a disentanglement gradient: tensor product equivariant architectures (MACE) produce representations where geometry is almost fully linearly accessible after composition removal ($R^2_{\text{geom}} = 0.782$ for HOMO-LUMO gap), while handcrafted descriptors (ANI-2x) entangle the same information nonlinearly ($R^2_{\text{geom}} = -0.792$ under Ridge; $R^2 = +0.784$ under MLP). MACE routes target-specific signal through irreducible representation channels -- dipole to $L = 1$, HOMO-LUMO gap to $L = 0$ -- a pattern not observed in ViSNet's vector-scalar architecture under the same probe. We show that gradient boosted tree probes on projected residuals are systematically inflated, recovering $R^2 = 0.68$--$0.95$ on a purely compositional target, and recommend linear probes as the primary metric. Linearly disentangled representations are more sample-efficient under linear probing, suggesting a practical advantage for equivariant architectures beyond raw prediction accuracy.
中文标题/摘要
标题：原子级基础模型中的信息路由：等变性如何生成线性解耦表示
原子级基础模型在中间表示中编码了哪些信息，这些信息是如何组织的？我们引入了组成投影分解（CPD），通过QR投影线性去除学习表示中的组成信号，并探测几何残差。在QM9分子和Materials Project晶体上的八个模型（来自五个架构家族）中，我们发现了一个解耦梯度：张量积等变架构（MACE）在去除组成信号后，几何信息几乎完全线性可访问（HOMO-LUMO能隙的R²=0.782），而手工设计的描述符（ANI-2x）则非线性地纠缠相同信息（Ridge下R²=-0.792；MLP下R²=+0.784）。MACE通过不可约表示通道路由目标特定信号——偶极矩对应L=1，HOMO-LUMO能隙对应L=0——这一模式在ViSNet的向量-标量架构下未被观察到。我们表明，对投影残差的梯度提升树探测器系统性地被高估，仅针对纯组合目标时R²恢复为0.68–0.95，建议将线性探测器作为主要评估指标。线性解耦表示在线性探测下更具样本效率，表明等变架构在原始预测精度之外具有实际优势。

Motivated by understanding how atomistic foundation models organize encoded information, the study introduces Composition Projection Decomposition (CPD), a method using QR projection to linearly isolate composition-dependent signals and probe the residual geometric content. Applied across eight models from five architectures on QM9 and Materials Project datasets, CPD revealed a disentanglement gradient: equivariant models like MACE produced linearly accessible geometry ($R^2_{\text{geom}} = 0.782$ for HOMO-LUMO gap), while handcrafted descriptors like ANI-2x showed nonlinear entanglement ($R^2 = -0.792$ under Ridge, $+0.784$ under MLP). MACE routed target signals through specific irreducible representation channels (e.g., dipole to $L=1$, gap to $L=0$), a pattern absent in ViSNet.
