Linear Model Extraction via Factual and Counterfactual Queries
Authors: Daan Otto, Jannis Kurtz, Dick den Hertog, Ilker Birbil
First: 2026-02-10T12:57:53+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T16:49:24+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
In model extraction attacks, the goal is to reveal the parameters of a black-box machine learning model by querying the model for a selected set of data points. Due to an increasing demand for explanations, this may involve counterfactual queries besides the typically considered factual queries. In this work, we consider linear models and three types of queries: factual, counterfactual, and robust counterfactual. First, for an arbitrary set of queries, we derive novel mathematical formulations for the classification regions for which the decision of the unknown model is known, without recovering any of the model parameters. Second, we derive bounds on the number of queries needed to extract the model's parameters for (robust) counterfactual queries under arbitrary norm-based distances. We show that the full model can be recovered using just a single counterfactual query when differentiable distance measures are employed. In contrast, when using polyhedral distances for instance, the number of required queries grows linearly with the dimension of the data space. For robust counterfactuals, the latter number of queries doubles. Consequently, the applied distance function and robustness of counterfactuals have a significant impact on the model's security.
中文标题/摘要
标题：通过事实与反事实查询进行线性模型提取
在模型提取攻击中，目标是通过查询黑盒机器学习模型选定的数据点，揭示模型参数。由于对解释需求的增加，此类攻击可能涉及除通常考虑的事实查询外的反事实查询。本文考虑线性模型和三类查询：事实查询、反事实查询和鲁棒反事实查询。首先，对于任意一组查询，我们推导出新颖的数学公式，用于描述决策未知模型的分类区域，而无需恢复任何模型参数。其次，我们推导出在任意基于范数的距离下，提取模型参数所需查询数量的界限。我们证明，当使用可微距离度量时，仅需一个反事实查询即可恢复完整模型。相比之下，当使用多面体距离时，所需查询数量随数据空间维度线性增长；对于鲁棒反事实查询，该数量翻倍。因此，所应用的距离函数和反事实查询的鲁棒性对模型安全性有显著影响。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the rising need for model explanations, this work investigates model extraction attacks on linear models using factual, counterfactual, and robust counterfactual queries. It derives mathematical formulations to determine classification regions without recovering model parameters, and establishes query bounds for parameter extraction under norm-based distances. Key results show that a single differentiable-distance-based counterfactual query suffices to fully recover the model, whereas polyhedral distances require linearly increasing queries with data dimension, and robust counterfactuals double that number, highlighting the critical role of distance metrics and robustness in model security.
鉴于对模型解释需求的增长，本研究探讨了针对线性模型的模型提取攻击，使用事实、反事实和鲁棒反事实查询。它推导出无需恢复模型参数即可确定分类区域的数学公式，并建立了在范数距离下提取参数所需的查询数量界限。主要发现表明，仅需一个基于可微距离的反事实查询即可完全恢复模型，而使用多面体距离时查询数随数据维度线性增长，鲁棒反事实则使查询数翻倍，凸显距离度量和鲁棒性对模型安全性的关键影响。
PROFusion: Robust and Accurate Dense Reconstruction via Camera Pose Regression and Optimization
Authors: Siyan Dong, Zijun Wang, Lulu Cai, Yi Ma, Yanchao Yang
Venue: ICRA 2026
First: 2025-09-29T03:20:49+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T16:49:04+00:00
Comments: ICRA 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Real-time dense scene reconstruction during unstable camera motions is crucial for robotics, yet current RGB-D SLAM systems fail when cameras experience large viewpoint changes, fast motions, or sudden shaking. Classical optimization-based methods deliver high accuracy but fail with poor initialization during large motions, while learning-based approaches provide robustness but lack sufficient accuracy for dense reconstruction. We address this challenge through a combination of learning-based initialization with optimization-based refinement. Our method employs a camera pose regression network to predict metric-aware relative poses from consecutive RGB-D frames, which serve as reliable starting points for a randomized optimization algorithm that further aligns depth images with the scene geometry. Extensive experiments demonstrate promising results: our approach outperforms the best competitor on challenging benchmarks, while maintaining comparable accuracy on stable motion sequences. The system operates in real-time, showcasing that combining simple and principled techniques can achieve both robustness for unstable motions and accuracy for dense reconstruction. Code released: https://github.com/siyandong/PROFusion.
中文标题/摘要
标题：PROFusion：通过相机位姿回归与优化实现鲁棒且精确的稠密重建
在不稳定相机运动期间进行实时稠密场景重建对机器人至关重要，但当前RGB-D SLAM系统在相机经历大幅视角变化、快速运动或突然抖动时失效。经典基于优化的方法虽精度高，但在大幅运动时因初始化不良而失败；而基于学习的方法虽具鲁棒性，但稠密重建精度不足。我们通过结合学习初始化与优化精炼解决此问题：方法采用相机位姿回归网络，从连续RGB-D帧预测具有度量感知的相对位姿，作为随机优化算法的可靠起点，进一步对齐深度图像与场景几何。大量实验表明：在挑战性基准上超越最佳竞争方法，稳定运动序列中保持相近精度。系统实时运行，证明简单而严谨的技术结合可同时实现不稳定运动下的鲁棒性与稠密重建的高精度。代码开源：https://github.com/siyandong/PROFusion。
Summary / 总结
To address the challenge of real-time dense scene reconstruction under unstable camera motion, where traditional RGB-D SLAM systems fail due to large viewpoint changes or fast movements, the paper proposes PROFusion: a hybrid method combining a learning-based camera pose regression network with optimization-based refinement. The pose regressor predicts metric-aware relative poses from consecutive RGB-D frames, which are then used as initialization for a randomized optimization algorithm to align depth images with scene geometry. Experimental results show that PROFusion outperforms state-of-the-art methods on challenging benchmarks while maintaining comparable accuracy on stable motion sequences, and it achieves real-time performance, demonstrating that principled techniques can yield both robustness and accuracy.
为解决在不稳定相机运动下实时稠密场景重建的难题——传统RGB-D SLAM系统在大视角变化或快速运动时失效——本文提出PROFusion方法，结合学习驱动的相机位姿回归网络与优化驱动的精炼模块。位姿回归器从连续RGB-D帧中预测具有度量感知的相对位姿，作为随机优化算法的可靠初始化，用于对齐深度图像与场景几何结构。实验表明，该方法在具有挑战性的基准测试中优于当前最优方法，同时在稳定运动序列上保持相近精度，并实现实时运行，证明了简洁而严谨的方法可同时实现鲁棒性和高精度重建。
A medical coding language model trained on clinical narratives from a population-wide cohort of 1.8 million patients
Authors: Joakim Edin, Sedrah Butt Balaganeshan, Annike Kjølby Kristensen, Lars Maaløe, Ioannis Louloudis, Søren Brunak
First: 2026-02-27T18:54:43+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T16:48:38+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Medical coding translates clinical documentation into standardized codes for billing, research, and public health, but manual coding is time-consuming and error-prone. Existing automation efforts rely on small datasets that poorly represent real-world patient heterogeneity. We trained a language model on 5.8 million electronic health records from 1.8 million patients across nearly all specialties in Eastern Denmark (2006--2016) to predict ICD-10 codes from clinical notes, medications, and laboratory results. Evaluated on 270,000 held-out patients, the model achieved a micro F1 of 71.8% and a top-10 recall of 95.5%. Performance varied by specialty (F1: 53--91%), with higher scores in specialties with well-defined diagnostic criteria. Codes appearing predominantly as secondary diagnoses had markedly lower F1 scores. For three such codes (suicide-related behaviors, weight disorders, and hypertension), the model identified thousands of uncoded cases, of which 76-86% were confirmed valid upon manual review, suggesting systematic under-coding rather than model error. These findings suggest under-coding of secondary diagnoses in Eastern Denmark during this period, with potential implications for epidemiological research, public health surveillance, and understanding of multimorbidity. Similar time constraints and reimbursement structures in other healthcare systems suggest this may not be isolated to this dataset. The model can automate coding for approximately 50% of cases and provide accurate suggestions for most others, and may offer a practical solution to help capture missed secondary conditions.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于180万患者人群临床记录训练的医学编码语言模型
医学编码将临床记录转化为标准化代码，用于计费、研究和公共卫生，但人工编码耗时且易出错。现有自动化方法依赖小规模数据集，难以反映真实世界患者异质性。我们基于丹麦东部近所有专科（2006-2016年）180万患者580万份电子健康记录，训练语言模型预测ICD-10编码，输入为临床记录、药物和实验室结果。在27万例验证患者上评估，模型微F1为71.8%，前10名召回率95.5%。不同专科表现差异显著（F1：53%-91%），诊断标准明确的专科表现更优。主要作为次要诊断出现的编码F1显著偏低。对三类此类编码（自杀相关行为、体重障碍、高血压），模型识别出数千例未编码病例，经人工复核76%-86%确认有效，提示系统性漏编码而非模型错误。这表明丹麦东部该时期存在次要诊断漏编码，可能影响流行病学研究、公共卫生监测及多病共存理解。其他医疗体系存在类似时间压力和报销结构，提示该问题或非孤立现象。模型可自动化处理约50%病例，其余病例亦能提供准确建议，或为捕捉漏诊次要疾病提供实用方案。
Summary / 总结
To address the inefficiency and inaccuracies of manual medical coding, researchers trained a language model on 5.8 million electronic health records from 1.8 million patients in Eastern Denmark to predict ICD-10 codes from clinical narratives, medications, and lab results. Evaluated on 270,000 unseen patients, the model achieved a micro F1 score of 71.8% and a top-10 recall of 95.5%, though performance varied by specialty (53–91%) and was notably lower for secondary diagnoses. The model uncovered thousands of previously uncoded cases for three such diagnoses—suicide-related behaviors, weight disorders, and hypertension—with 76–86% confirmed valid upon manual review, indicating systemic under-coding rather than model failure. This suggests widespread under-recording of secondary conditions in the dataset, with potential implications for epidemiology and public health, and implies similar issues may exist in other healthcare systems with comparable reimbursement structures.
为解决人工医疗编码效率低、易出错的问题，研究人员基于丹麦近180万患者580万份电子健康记录训练了一个语言模型，用于从临床记录、药物和实验室数据中预测ICD-10编码。在27万份未见患者数据上评估，模型达到71.8%的微F1值和95.5%的前10召回率，不同专科表现差异显著（53–91%），且次要诊断编码准确率明显偏低。模型识别出数千例此前未编码的病例，涉及自杀相关行为、体重障碍和高血压三类疾病，经人工复核76–86%被确认有效，表明是系统性漏编码而非模型错误。这提示该地区在2006–2016年间存在次要诊断普遍漏记现象，可能影响流行病学和公共卫生监测，并暗示其他医疗体系可能面临类似问题。
MLV-Edit: Towards Consistent and Highly Efficient Editing for Minute-Level Videos
Authors: Yangyi Cao, Yuanhang Li, Lan Chen, Qi Mao
First: 2026-02-02T14:07:00+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T16:46:06+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We propose MLV-Edit, a training-free, flow-based framework that address the unique challenges of minute-level video editing. While existing techniques excel in short-form video manipulation, scaling them to long-duration videos remains challenging due to prohibitive computational overhead and the difficulty of maintaining global temporal consistency across thousands of frames. To address this, MLV-Edit employs a divide-and-conquer strategy for segment-wise editing, facilitated by two core modules: Velocity Blend rectifies motion inconsistencies at segment boundaries by aligning the flow fields of adjacent chunks, eliminating flickering and boundary artifacts commonly observed in fragmented video processing; and Attention Sink anchors local segment features to global reference frames, effectively suppressing cumulative structural drift. Extensive quantitative and qualitative experiments demonstrate that MLV-Edit consistently outperforms state-of-the-art methods in terms of temporal stability and semantic fidelity.
Summary / 总结
We propose MLV-Edit, a training-free, flow-based framework that address the unique challenges of minute-level video editing.
为解决长时长分钟级视频编辑中的计算开销大和时间一致性差的问题，MLV-Edit 提出一种无需训练的基于流的框架，采用分段处理策略，通过 Velocity Blend 对齐相邻片段的运动场以消除闪烁和边界伪影，通过 Attention Sink 将局部特征锚定到全局参考帧以抑制结构漂移。实验表明，该方法在时间稳定性和语义保真度上显著优于现有方法。
Entropy Sentinel: Continuous LLM Accuracy Monitoring from Decoding Entropy Traces in STEM
Authors: Pedro Memoli Buffa, Luciano Del Corro
First: 2026-01-13T21:54:38+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T16:43:33+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Deploying LLMs raises two coupled challenges: (1) monitoring--estimating where a model underperforms as traffic and domains drift--and (2) improvement--prioritizing data acquisition to close the largest performance gaps. We test whether an inference-time signal can estimate slice-level accuracy under domain shift. For each response, we compute an output-entropy profile from final-layer next-token probabilities (from top-$k$ logprobs) and summarize it with different statistics. A lightweight classifier predicts instance correctness, and averaging predicted probabilities yields a domain-level accuracy estimate. We evaluate on ten STEM reasoning benchmarks with exhaustive train/test compositions ($k\in\{1,2,3,4\}$; all $\binom{10}{k}$ combinations), on different classifier models and features across nine LLMs from six families (3B--20B). Estimates often track held-out benchmark accuracy, and several models show near-monotonic ordering of domains, providing evidence for output-entropy profiles being an accessible signal for scalable monitoring and for targeted data acquisition.
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need to monitor and improve LLM performance under shifting domains, this study investigates whether decoding entropy traces can serve as a reliable signal for estimating slice-level accuracy. The method computes output-entropy profiles from final-layer next-token probabilities (top-k logprobs) for each response, summarizes them with various statistics, and feeds them into a lightweight classifier to predict instance correctness. Averaging these predictions yields a domain-level accuracy estimate. Evaluated across ten STEM reasoning benchmarks with all possible train/test splits (k=1 to 4) and nine LLMs from six families, the approach consistently tracked held-out benchmark accuracy, with several models showing near-monotonic domain ordering, suggesting entropy-based signals are viable for scalable monitoring and targeted data acquisition.
为应对大语言模型在领域漂移下监控与改进性能的挑战，本研究探索解码熵迹是否可作为推理时信号以估计切片级准确率。方法从最后一层下一词概率（top-k logprobs）计算输出熵分布，并用不同统计量进行摘要，输入轻量级分类器预测实例正确性，其预测概率平均值即为领域级准确率估计。在十项STEM推理基准上，对所有可能的训练/测试组合（k=1至4）及九个来自六家厂商的模型进行评估，结果表明该方法常能跟踪验证集准确率，并在多个模型中呈现近单调的领域排序，证明熵迹信号适用于可扩展监控与定向数据采集。
From Language to Action: Can LLM-Based Agents Be Used for Embodied Robot Cognition?
Authors: Shinas Shaji, Fabian Huppertz, Alex Mitrevski, Sebastian Houben
Venue: ICRA
First: 2026-03-03T16:36:06+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T16:36:06+00:00
Comments: Accepted for publication at the 2026 IEEE International Conference on Robotics and Automation (ICRA)
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
In order to flexibly act in an everyday environment, a robotic agent needs a variety of cognitive capabilities that enable it to reason about plans and perform execution recovery. Large language models (LLMs) have been shown to demonstrate emergent cognitive aspects, such as reasoning and language understanding; however, the ability to control embodied robotic agents requires reliably bridging high-level language to low-level functionalities for perception and control. In this paper, we investigate the extent to which an LLM can serve as a core component for planning and execution reasoning in a cognitive robot architecture. For this purpose, we propose a cognitive architecture in which an agentic LLM serves as the core component for planning and reasoning, while components for working and episodic memories support learning from experience and adaptation. An instance of the architecture is then used to control a mobile manipulator in a simulated household environment, where environment interaction is done through a set of high-level tools for perception, reasoning, navigation, grasping, and placement, all of which are made available to the LLM-based agent. We evaluate our proposed system on two household tasks (object placement and object swapping), which evaluate the agent's reasoning, planning, and memory utilisation. The results demonstrate that the LLM-driven agent can complete structured tasks and exhibits emergent adaptation and memory-guided planning, but also reveal significant limitations, such as hallucinations about the task success and poor instruction following by refusing to acknowledge and complete sequential tasks. These findings highlight both the potential and challenges of employing LLMs as embodied cognitive controllers for autonomous robots.
中文标题/摘要
标题：从语言到行动：基于大语言模型的代理能否用于具身机器人认知？
为了在日常环境中灵活行动，机器人代理需要多种认知能力，使其能够规划并执行恢复。大语言模型（LLMs）已被证明展现出涌现的认知能力，如推理和语言理解；然而，控制具身机器人代理需要可靠地将高层语言与感知和控制的底层功能连接起来。本文研究了LLM在认知机器人架构中作为规划和执行推理核心组件的程度。为此，我们提出了一种认知架构，其中具身LLM作为规划和推理的核心组件，而工作记忆和情景记忆组件支持从经验中学习和适应。该架构的一个实例被用于控制一个移动操作机器人在模拟家庭环境中的行为，环境交互通过一组高层工具实现，包括感知、推理、导航、抓取和放置，这些工具均对基于LLM的代理开放。我们在两个家庭任务（物体放置和物体交换）上评估了该系统，以检验代理的推理、规划和记忆利用能力。结果表明，LLM驱动的代理能够完成结构化任务，并展现出涌现的适应性和记忆引导的规划能力，但也揭示了显著的局限性，如对任务成功的幻觉和拒绝承认并完成顺序任务的指令遵循能力。这些发现突显了将LLM作为自主机器人具身认知控制器的潜力与挑战。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need for robots to reason and adapt in dynamic environments, this study explores whether large language models (LLMs) can serve as core cognitive planners for embodied robotic agents. The authors propose a cognitive architecture where an LLM handles planning and reasoning, supported by memory components for learning and adaptation, and integrate it with high-level robotic tools for perception and manipulation in a simulated home. Evaluated on object placement and swapping tasks, the LLM agent successfully completed structured tasks and showed emergent memory-guided planning, but also exhibited significant flaws including hallucinations about task success and failure to follow multi-step instructions. These results indicate LLMs hold promise for embodied cognition but face critical limitations in reliability and task compliance.
本文探讨大型语言模型（LLM）能否作为具身机器人认知的核心组件，动机在于机器人需在动态环境中进行推理与适应。作者提出一种认知架构，其中LLM负责规划与推理，辅以工作记忆与情景记忆模块支持学习与适应，并与高阶机器人工具（如感知、导航、抓取与放置）集成。在两项家庭任务（物体放置与交换）中，LLM驱动的代理能完成结构化任务并展现适应性与记忆引导规划，但也存在明显缺陷，如任务成功幻觉及拒绝执行多步指令。
Agentic AI-based Coverage Closure for Formal Verification
Authors: Sivaram Pothireddypalli, Ashish Raman, Deepak Narayan Gadde, Aman Kumar
First: 2026-03-03T16:35:03+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T16:35:03+00:00
Comments: Published at IEEE International Conference on Intelligent Processing, Hardware, Electronics, and Radio Systems 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Coverage closure is a critical requirement in Integrated Chip (IC) development process and key metric for verification sign-off. However, traditional exhaustive approaches often fail to achieve full coverage within project timelines. This study presents an agentic AI-driven workflow that utilizes Large Language Model (LLM)-enabled Generative AI (GenAI) to automate coverage analysis for formal verification, identify coverage gaps, and generate the required formal properties. The framework accelerates verification efficiency by systematically addressing coverage holes. Benchmarking open-source and internal designs reveals a measurable increase in coverage metrics, with improvements correlated to the complexity of the design. Comparative analysis validates the effectiveness of this approach. These results highlight the potential of agentic AI-based techniques to improve formal verification productivity and support comprehensive coverage closure.

标题：基于代理人工智能的正式验证覆盖闭合
覆盖闭合是集成电路（IC）开发流程中的关键要求，也是验证签核的核心指标。然而，传统穷举方法往往无法在项目周期内实现全面覆盖。本研究提出一种基于代理人工智能的工作流，利用大型语言模型（LLM）赋能的生成式人工智能（GenAI）自动化正式验证的覆盖分析，识别覆盖缺口，并生成所需的形式化属性。该框架通过系统性解决覆盖漏洞，提升验证效率。对开源及内部设计的基准测试显示，覆盖指标显著提升，且改进程度与设计复杂度相关。对比分析验证了该方法的有效性。结果凸显了基于代理人工智能技术在提升正式验证生产力和实现全面覆盖闭合方面的潜力。

Nano-EmoX: Unifying Multimodal Emotional Intelligence from Perception to Empathy
Authors: Jiahao Huang, Fengyan Lin, Xuechao Yang, Chen Feng, Kexin Zhu, Xu Yang, Zhide Chen
First: 2026-03-02T17:42:33+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T16:34:24+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
The development of affective multimodal language models (MLMs) has long been constrained by a gap between low-level perception and high-level interaction, leading to fragmented affective capabilities and limited generalization. To bridge this gap, we propose a cognitively inspired three-level hierarchy that organizes affective tasks according to their cognitive depth-perception, understanding, and interaction-and provides a unified conceptual foundation for advancing affective modeling. Guided by this hierarchy, we introduce Nano-EmoX, a small-scale multitask MLM, and P2E (Perception-to-Empathy), a curriculum-based training framework. Nano-EmoX integrates a suite of omni-modal encoders, including an enhanced facial encoder and a fusion encoder, to capture key multimodal affective cues and improve cross-task transferability. The outputs are projected into a unified language space via heterogeneous adapters, empowering a lightweight language model to tackle diverse affective tasks. Concurrently, P2E progressively cultivates emotional intelligence by aligning rapid perception with chain-of-thought-driven empathy. To the best of our knowledge, Nano-EmoX is the first compact MLM (2.2B) to unify six core affective tasks across all three hierarchy levels, achieving state-of-the-art or highly competitive performance across multiple benchmarks, demonstrating excellent efficiency and generalization.
中文标题/摘要
标题：Nano-EmoX：从感知到共情的多模态情感智能统一框架
情感多模态语言模型（MLM）的发展长期受限于低层感知与高层交互之间的鸿沟，导致情感能力碎片化且泛化能力有限。为弥合此差距，我们提出一种受认知启发的三级层次结构，按认知深度（感知、理解、交互）组织情感任务，并提供统一的概念基础以推进情感建模。基于此框架，我们提出Nano-EmoX——一种小型多任务MLM，以及P2E（感知到共情）课程式训练框架。Nano-EmoX整合了多种全模态编码器（含增强型面部编码器与融合编码器），以捕捉关键多模态情感线索并提升跨任务迁移能力；其输出通过异构适配器投影至统一语言空间，使轻量级语言模型可处理多样情感任务。同时，P2E通过将快速感知与思维链驱动的共情对齐，逐步培养情感智能。据我们所知，Nano-EmoX是首个统一涵盖三级层次结构六大核心情感任务的紧凑型MLM（2.2B参数），在多个基准测试中达到最先进或高度竞争力的性能，展现出卓越的效率与泛化能力。
Summary / 总结
The development of affective multimodal language models (MLMs) has long been constrained by a gap between low-level perception and high-level interaction, leading to fragmented affective capabilities and limited generalization.
为弥合多模态语言模型在感知与高级交互间的能力断层，作者提出Nano-EmoX小规模多任务模型与P2E课程训练框架，统一构建从感知、理解到交互的情感智能层级。Nano-EmoX融合增强型面部编码器与融合编码器，并通过异构适配器将多模态情感线索映射至统一语言空间，实现高效跨任务迁移。在六个核心情感任务上，该2.2B参数模型达到多项基准的最先进或竞争力强的结果，展现出优异的泛化能力与效率。
Channel-Adaptive Edge AI: Maximizing Inference Throughput by Adapting Computational Complexity to Channel States
Authors: Jierui Zhang, Jianhao Huang, Kaibin Huang
First: 2026-03-03T16:33:29+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T16:33:29+00:00
Comments: 14 pages, 14 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
\emph{Integrated communication and computation} (IC$^2$) has emerged as a new paradigm for enabling efficient edge inference in sixth-generation (6G) networks. However, the design of IC$^2$ technologies is hindered by the lack of a tractable theoretical framework for characterizing \emph{end-to-end} (E2E) inference performance. The metric is highly complicated as it needs to account for both channel distortion and artificial intelligence (AI) model architecture and computational complexity. In this work, we address this challenge by developing a tractable analytical model for E2E inference accuracy and leveraging it to design a \emph{channel-adaptive AI} algorithm that maximizes inference throughput, referred to as the edge processing rate (EPR), under latency and accuracy constraints. Specifically, we consider an edge inference system in which a server deploys a backbone model with early exit, which enables flexible computational complexity, to perform inference on data features transmitted by a mobile device. The proposed accuracy model characterizes high-dimensional feature distributions in the angular domain using a Mixture of von Mises (MvM) distribution. This leads to a desired closed-form expression for inference accuracy as a function of quantization bit-width and model traversal depth, which represents channel distortion and computational complexity, respectively. Building upon this accuracy model, we formulate and solve the EPR maximization problem under joint latency and accuracy constraints, leading to a channel-adaptive AI algorithm that achieves full IC$^2$ integration. The proposed algorithm jointly adapts transmit-side feature compression and receive-side model complexity according to channel conditions to maximize overall efficiency and inference throughput. Experimental results demonstrate its superior performance as compared with fixed-complexity counterparts.
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need for efficient edge inference in 6G networks, this work develops a channel-adaptive AI algorithm to maximize inference throughput under latency and accuracy constraints. It introduces a tractable analytical model for end-to-end inference accuracy using a Mixture of von Mises distribution to characterize high-dimensional feature distributions in the angular domain, enabling closed-form expressions for accuracy based on quantization bit-width and model traversal depth. The algorithm jointly adapts feature compression at the transmitter and model complexity at the receiver to match channel conditions, optimizing the edge processing rate. Experimental results show that this adaptive approach outperforms fixed-complexity methods in terms of throughput while maintaining accuracy.
为提升6G网络边缘推理效率，本文提出一种基于信道自适应的AI算法，旨在满足延迟与精度约束下最大化推理吞吐量。该算法构建了一个可解析的端到端推理精度模型，利用混合von Mises分布刻画高维特征在角域的分布，推导出精度与量化比特宽、模型遍历深度（分别对应信道失真与计算复杂度）的闭式表达式。算法联合调整发送端特征压缩与接收端模型复杂度以匹配信道状态，从而优化边缘处理率。实验表明，该自适应方法在保持精度的同时，显著优于固定复杂度方案的吞吐量表现。
Geometry-Guided Reinforcement Learning for Multi-view Consistent 3D Scene Editing
Authors: Jiyuan Wang, Chunyu Lin, Lei Sun, Zhi Cao, Yuyang Yin, Lang Nie, Zhenlong Yuan, Xiangxiang Chu, Yunchao Wei, Kang Liao, Guosheng Lin
First: 2026-03-03T16:31:10+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T16:31:10+00:00
Comments: 18 pages, 8 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Leveraging the priors of 2D diffusion models for 3D editing has emerged as a promising paradigm. However, maintaining multi-view consistency in edited results remains challenging, and the extreme scarcity of 3D-consistent editing paired data renders supervised fine-tuning (SFT), the most effective training strategy for editing tasks, infeasible. In this paper, we observe that, while generating multi-view consistent 3D content is highly challenging, verifying 3D consistency is tractable, naturally positioning reinforcement learning (RL) as a feasible solution. Motivated by this, we propose \textbf{RL3DEdit}, a single-pass framework driven by RL optimization with novel rewards derived from the 3D foundation model, VGGT. Specifically, we leverage VGGT's robust priors learned from massive real-world data, feed the edited images, and utilize the output confidence maps and pose estimation errors as reward signals, effectively anchoring the 2D editing priors onto a 3D-consistent manifold via RL. Extensive experiments demonstrate that RL3DEdit achieves stable multi-view consistency and outperforms state-of-the-art methods in editing quality with high efficiency. To promote the development of 3D editing, we will release the code and model.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于几何引导的强化学习用于多视角一致的3D场景编辑
利用2D扩散模型的先验知识进行3D编辑已成为一种有前景的范式。然而，编辑结果保持多视角一致性仍具挑战性，且3D一致编辑配对数据极度稀缺，使得监督微调（SFT）——编辑任务中最有效的训练策略——不可行。本文观察到，虽然生成多视角一致的3D内容极具挑战，但验证3D一致性是可行的，这自然将强化学习（RL）定位为可行方案。受此启发，我们提出\textbf{RL3DEdit}，一种基于RL优化的单次通过框架，其奖励信号源自3D基础模型VGGT。具体而言，我们利用VGGT从海量真实数据中学习到的鲁棒先验，输入编辑后的图像，并利用输出置信度图和姿态估计误差作为奖励信号，通过RL将2D编辑先验锚定在3D一致流形上。大量实验表明，RL3DEdit实现了稳定的多视角一致性，并在编辑质量上高效超越现有最先进方法。为促进3D编辑发展，我们将开源代码与模型。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the challenge of maintaining multi-view consistency in 3D scene editing despite the scarcity of paired training data, this paper proposes RL3DEdit, a reinforcement learning framework that leverages 3D foundation model VGGT to derive reward signals from confidence maps and pose estimation errors. By anchoring 2D diffusion model priors onto a 3D-consistent manifold through RL optimization, the method enables single-pass editing with stable multi-view consistency. Experimental results show RL3DEdit outperforms existing methods in editing quality and efficiency, validating its effectiveness for 3D scene editing.
为解决3D场景编辑中多视角一致性难以维持且配对数据稀缺的问题，本文提出RL3DEdit框架，利用3D基础模型VGGT生成置信度图与姿态误差作为奖励信号，通过强化学习将2D扩散模型先验锚定在3D一致性流形上。实验表明该方法在单次编辑中实现稳定多视角一致性，编辑质量与效率均优于现有方法，验证了其在3D编辑中的有效性。
APRES: An Agentic Paper Revision and Evaluation System
Authors: Bingchen Zhao, Jenny Zhang, Chenxi Whitehouse, Minqi Jiang, Michael Shvartsman, Abhishek Charnalia, Despoina Magka, Tatiana Shavrina, Derek Dunfield, Oisin Mac Aodha, Yoram Bachrach
First: 2026-03-03T16:29:13+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T16:29:13+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Scientific discoveries must be communicated clearly to realize their full potential. Without effective communication, even the most groundbreaking findings risk being overlooked or misunderstood. The primary way scientists communicate their work and receive feedback from the community is through peer review. However, the current system often provides inconsistent feedback between reviewers, ultimately hindering the improvement of a manuscript and limiting its potential impact. In this paper, we introduce a novel method APRES powered by Large Language Models (LLMs) to update a scientific papers text based on an evaluation rubric. Our automated method discovers a rubric that is highly predictive of future citation counts, and integrate it with APRES in an automated system that revises papers to enhance their quality and impact. Crucially, this objective should be met without altering the core scientific content. We demonstrate the success of APRES, which improves future citation prediction by 19.6% in mean averaged error over the next best baseline, and show that our paper revision process yields papers that are preferred over the originals by human expert evaluators 79% of the time. Our findings provide strong empirical support for using LLMs as a tool to help authors stress-test their manuscripts before submission. Ultimately, our work seeks to augment, not replace, the essential role of human expert reviewers, for it should be humans who discern which discoveries truly matter, guiding science toward advancing knowledge and enriching lives.
中文标题/摘要
标题：APRES：一种基于代理的论文修订与评估系统
科学发现必须清晰传达才能充分发挥其潜力。若缺乏有效沟通，即使最突破性的成果也可能被忽视或误解。科学家主要通过同行评审来交流研究成果并获得社区反馈。然而，当前系统常导致评审意见不一致，最终阻碍论文改进并限制其潜在影响力。本文提出一种基于大语言模型（LLMs）的创新方法APRES，根据评估标准自动修订科学论文文本。我们的自动化方法发现一个高度预测未来引用量的评估标准，并将其整合到APRES系统中，以自动修订论文，提升其质量和影响力。关键在于，这一目标应在不改变核心科学内容的前提下实现。我们证明APRES成功将未来引用预测的平均误差降低19.6%（优于最佳基线），且经人类专家评估，修订后的论文79%的时间更受青睐。我们的研究结果为利用LLMs帮助作者在投稿前“压力测试”论文提供了有力实证支持。最终，我们的工作旨在增强而非取代人类专家评审的核心作用，因为唯有人类才能判断哪些发现真正重要，从而引导科学进步并丰富人类生活。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need to improve scientific communication and citation impact through more consistent peer review feedback, APRES leverages Large Language Models to automatically revise scientific papers based on a rubric predictive of future citations. The system first learns this rubric from historical citation data, then uses it to iteratively refine manuscript text while preserving core scientific content. Experimental results show APRES reduces citation prediction error by 19.6% compared to the best baseline and is preferred over original papers by human evaluators in 79% of cases, demonstrating its effectiveness in enhancing manuscript quality without compromising scientific integrity.
为提升科学传播效果与论文引用潜力，APRES 利用大语言模型根据预测未来引用量的评分标准自动修订科研论文，同时确保不改变核心科学内容。系统首先从历史引用数据中学习评分标准，再据此迭代优化论文文本。实验表明，APRES 相较于最佳基线方法将引用预测误差降低 19.6%，且在 79% 的情况下被人类评审专家认为优于原始论文，证明其在提升论文质量方面的有效性。
A Researcher's Guide to Empirical Risk Minimization
Authors: Lars van der Laan
First: 2026-02-25T02:26:23+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T16:28:45+00:00
Comments: Version 2; minor edits and clarifications, expanded references, extended Section 2 (high-probability bounds)
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
This guide provides a reference for high-probability regret bounds in empirical risk minimization (ERM). The presentation is modular: we begin with intuition and general proof strategies, then state broadly applicable guarantees under high-level conditions and provide tools for verifying them for specific losses and function classes. We emphasize that many ERM rate derivations can be organized around a three-step recipe -- a basic inequality, a uniform local concentration bound, and a fixed-point argument -- which yields regret bounds in terms of a critical radius, defined via localized Rademacher complexity, under a mild Bernstein-type variance-risk condition. To make these bounds concrete, we upper bound the critical radius using local maximal inequalities and metric-entropy integrals, thereby recovering familiar rates for VC-subgraph, Sobolev/Hölder, and bounded-variation classes. We also study ERM with nuisance components -- including weighted ERM and Neyman-orthogonal losses -- as they arise in causal inference, missing data, and domain adaptation. Following the orthogonal statistical learning framework, we highlight that these problems often admit regret-transfer bounds linking regret under an estimated loss to population regret under the target loss. These bounds typically decompose the regret into (i) statistical error under the estimated loss and (ii) approximation error due to nuisance estimation. Under sample splitting or cross-fitting, the first term can be controlled using standard fixed-loss ERM regret bounds, while the second depends only on nuisance-estimation accuracy. As a novel contribution, we also treat the in-sample regime, in which the nuisances and the ERM are fit on the same data, deriving regret bounds and showing that fast oracle rates remain attainable under suitable smoothness and Donsker-type conditions.
中文标题/摘要
标题：经验风险最小化的研究者指南
本指南为经验风险最小化（ERM）中的高概率后悔界提供参考。内容模块化：首先介绍直觉与一般证明策略，然后在高层次条件下陈述广泛适用的保证，并提供用于验证特定损失函数类的工具。我们强调，许多ERM速率推导可围绕三步配方组织——基本不等式、均匀局部集中界和不动点论证——从而在温和的伯恩斯坦型方差-风险条件下，以局部Rademacher复杂度定义的临界半径表示后悔界。为使这些界具体化，我们利用局部最大不等式和度量熵积分对临界半径进行上界估计，从而恢复VC子图、Sobolev/Hölder及有界变差类等熟悉的速率。 我们还研究包含干扰成分的ERM——包括加权ERM和Neyman正交损失——这些在因果推断、缺失数据和领域自适应中出现。遵循正交统计学习框架，我们指出这些问题通常允许后悔转移界，将估计损失下的后悔与目标损失下的总体后悔关联起来。这些界通常将后悔分解为（i）估计损失下的统计误差，（ii）因干扰估计导致的逼近误差。在样本分割或交叉验证下，第一项可通过标准固定损失ERM后悔界控制，而第二项仅依赖于干扰估计精度。作为新贡献，我们还处理了样本内情形——即干扰与ERM均在相同数据上拟合，推导后悔界并证明在适当光滑性和Donsker型条件下，仍可实现快速Oracle速率。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need for general yet practical regret bounds in empirical risk minimization, this work presents a modular framework centered on a three-step recipe: a basic inequality, a uniform local concentration bound, and a fixed-point argument, which together yield high-probability regret bounds expressed via a critical radius derived from localized Rademacher complexity under a mild Bernstein-type condition. The method recovers standard rates for VC-subgraph, Sobolev/Hölder, and bounded-variation classes by bounding the critical radius using local maximal inequalities and metric-entropy integrals. Additionally, the paper extends ERM to settings with nuisance components, such as weighted ERM and Neyman-orthogonal losses, showing that regret can be decomposed into statistical and approximation errors, with the former controlled via standard ERM bounds and the latter via nuisance estimation accuracy; it further demonstrates that fast oracle rates remain achievable in the in-sample regime under smoothness and Donsker-type conditions.
为获得经验风险最小化中普适且实用的高概率后悔界，本文提出一个模块化框架，基于三步法：基本不等式、均匀局部集中界与不动点论证，最终以局部Rademacher复杂度定义的临界半径表达后悔界，需满足温和的Bernstein型方差-风险条件。作者通过局部最大不等式与度量熵积分，推导出VC子图、Sobolev/Hölder及有界变差类等常见函数族的熟悉收敛率。此外，针对因果推断、缺失数据与领域自适应中的干扰成分问题，如加权ERM与Neyman正交损失，本文提出后悔转移界，将后悔分解为估计损失下的统计误差与干扰估计带来的逼近误差。在样本内情形下，作者证明在适当光滑性与Donsker型条件下，仍可实现快速Oracle收敛率。
